
-----title
德清 (出生地)
-----detail

-----title
杭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6ddc7eb9f26f4f278d5012d851b206f9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6ddc7eb9f26f4f278d5012d851b206f9");'><span id='6ddc7eb9f26f4f278d5012d851b206f9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1217&endYear=1217')">1217年</a>，23岁</div><div id='6ddc7eb9f26f4f278d5012d851b206f9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1217&endYear=1217')">1217年5月</a>　五月，举进士第一，授承事郎，签镇东军节度判官。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='0021cc8d8c06452f91c92c99d8364092_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0021cc8d8c06452f91c92c99d8364092");'><span id='0021cc8d8c06452f91c92c99d8364092_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1226&endYear=1228')">1226-1228年</a>，32-34岁</div><div id='0021cc8d8c06452f91c92c99d8364092' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1226&endYear=1226')">1226年11月</a>　十一月，服除，授秘书省正字。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1227&endYear=1227')">1227年</a>　为秘书省正字。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1228&endYear=1228')">1228年12月</a>　十二月，迁校书郎。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='845557d1c518498f89b14a1db226f634_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("845557d1c518498f89b14a1db226f634");'><span id='845557d1c518498f89b14a1db226f634_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1230&endYear=1232')">1230-1232年</a>，36-38岁</div><div id='845557d1c518498f89b14a1db226f634' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1230&endYear=1230')">1230年</a>　转朝散郎、尚书金部员外郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1231&endYear=1231')">1231年</a>　迁尚右郎官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1231&endYear=1231')">1231年</a>　上疏论都城火灾，乞修省以消变异。作品：《奏论都城火灾乞修省以消变异》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_1309828' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309828' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309828?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏论都城火灾乞修省以消变异<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍定四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1231年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309828")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309828_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309828'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309828'>臣一介疏贱，假守嘉兴，蒙恩召置郎省，于故事当对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309828_comment'></div>方斋心服形，思所以告陛下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309828_comment'></div>乃九月丙戌之夜，郁攸挻灾，自宗庙百司以至万姓之庐舍，自典章文告以至公私之货财，等罹煨烬，荡为瓦砾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309828_comment'></div>行人迷往来之路，飞鸟无栖宿之林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309828_comment'></div>死者焦灼，生者暴露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309828_comment'></div>臣不胜悲伤痛悼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309828_comment'></div>窃以为当言之事孰大于此，敬陈愚虑，仰渎渊聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309828_comment'></div>臣闻天人之际，应若影响，灾异之至，断不虚生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309828_comment'></div>且陛下自甲申履位，越一岁而山阳之变作，又一岁而盱眙之变作，又二岁而苏秀震凌之变作，又一岁而江西、福建之寇兴，台城飘没之变作，又一岁而穆桩之警与逆全之变作，又一岁而西蜀之兵、三衢之寇与今日回禄之变作，愈变愈异，日迫日危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309828_comment'></div>故太室燬则几于无宗祧矣，都省燬则几于无政事矣，御史台燬则几于无纪纲矣，秘书省燬则几于无文章矣，库务燬则几于无积贮矣，聚庐燬则几于无人民矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309828_comment'></div>此浸微浸削之兆，而非适值偶逢之故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309828_comment'></div>臣尝谓水火盗贼干戈之厄，容或可以数言，若乃否而不倾，屯而不丧，有变故而无乱亡，则全在于以德胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309828_comment'></div>惟我宁考在位三十年，固尝有火灾矣，未闻燔宗庙朝廷也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309828_comment'></div>尝有水灾矣，未闻冒城郭井邑也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309828_comment'></div>尝有盗贼之患矣，未闻纷扰近辅也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309828_comment'></div>尝有夷狄之虞矣，未闻陷失连城也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309828_comment'></div>尝有奸人窥伺矣，未闻一夫窃发于宫掖也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309828_comment'></div>尝有归陛反侧矣，未闻叛臣饮马于江浒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309828_comment'></div>盖先帝以节俭仁慈，严恭寅畏，格于天而天矜之，则天不怒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309828_comment'></div>暴于人而人亮之，则人不怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309828_comment'></div>是以有灾而旋弭，有变而自消，有艰屯而不至于危乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309828_comment'></div>今日之事，大非先帝时比矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309828_comment'></div>淮困于兵，蜀困于兵，江西、福建困于兵，严、衢之间，又重困于兵，凡大农、少府之储，无不尽困于兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309828_comment'></div>江、浙、湖、湘、京、汉频困于水，而京城之内又大困于火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309828_comment'></div>军国空虚，州县罄竭，加以贪官污吏虎噬狼吞，苞苴者二三，席捲者八九，耕夫无一勺之食，织妇无一缕之丝，生民熬熬，海内汹汹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309828_comment'></div>天下之势，譬如以漓胶腐纸粘缀破坏之器而置之几案，稍触之则应手堕地而碎耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309828_comment'></div>以前日昼夜之火，察辇毂军民之情，议论无端，證状甚异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309828_comment'></div>万一不幸有甚于火者，臣未知所以为陛下计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309828_comment'></div>及今改图，尚可挽回，傥仍掩护，将安所终！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309828_comment'></div>臣愿陛下斋戒修省，恐惧对越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309828_comment'></div>菲恶衣食，必使国人信之，毋徒曰减膳而已；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309828_comment'></div>疏摈声色，必使天下孚之，毋徒曰撤乐而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309828_comment'></div>阉宦之窃弄威福者勿亲，女宠之根萌祸患者勿昵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309828_comment'></div>以暗室屋漏为尊严之区，而必敬必戒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1309828_comment'></div>以恒舞酣歌为乱亡之宅，而不淫不泆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1309828_comment'></div>使皇天后土知陛下有畏之之心，使三军万姓知陛下有忧之之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1309828_comment'></div>然后明诏二三大臣，相与和衷竭虑，力改弦辙，昭示意向，以孔明之公道平政理，以杨绾之清德励风俗，收召贤哲，选用忠良，贪残者屏，回邪者斥，怀奸党贼者诛，贾怨误国者黜，毋并进君子小人以为包荒，毋兼容邪说正论以为皇极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1309828_comment'></div>自京师以达四方，凡监司帅守之为公论指目者，次第罢遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1309828_comment'></div>以培国家一线之脉，以救生民一旦之命，庶几天意可回，天灾可息，凡衰微败坏之證，可以徐徐经理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1309828_comment'></div>董仲舒有言：国家将有失道之败，天乃出灾害以谴告之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1309828_comment'></div>不知自省，又出怪异以警惧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1309828_comment'></div>尚不知变，而伤败乃至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1309828_comment'></div>今谴告出矣，怪异见矣，目前之事，亦浸浸于伤败矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1309828_comment'></div>弭灾为祥，易乱为治，转危极而为安存，是在陛下与二三大臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1309828_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「心乎爱矣，遐不谓矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1309828_comment'></div>臣不胜惓惓，惟陛下裁幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1309828_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1309828_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1231&endYear=1231')">1231年</a>　奏论重地当豫蓄人才以备患。作品：《奏论重地要区当豫蓄人才以备患事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_1309829' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309829' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309829?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏论重地要区当豫蓄人才以备患事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1231年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309829")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309829_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309829'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309829'>臣闻《说命》曰「有备无患」，《中庸》曰「事豫则立」，有国有家者格天大训也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309829_comment'></div>顷者逆全包藏𧛂心，窥伺东甸，庙算沈深，人莫测识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309829_comment'></div>储制臣于秣陵，而密为江海之防；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309829_comment'></div>置虎臣于京口滁阳，而阴为掎角之备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309829_comment'></div>一旦有警，亟合江淮之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309829_comment'></div>故其得以抚旧规，叶新画，亟颁帅宪之节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309829_comment'></div>故其得以朝闻命，夕会兵，布置转移，神机迅速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309829_comment'></div>并谋同志，臂指顺随，而逆全固已胆落矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309829_comment'></div>迄剪凶残，肃清淮浒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309829_comment'></div>原其机括，实在于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309829_comment'></div>此有备无患、事豫则立之明验也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309829_comment'></div>至若闽江三衢，赤子弄兵，关外四州，裔夷侵轶，计其收效之迟速，每恨储才之有无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309829_comment'></div>招捕更使则闽寇定，节阃易人则赣寇定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309829_comment'></div>起家食之彦，固足以纾蜀道之难也，然失之迟则抢攘而未定；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309829_comment'></div>起草氓之臣，固足以慰衢人之心也，然邻于窘则抚纳而仅定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309829_comment'></div>此可以验无备则患生，不豫则事废者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309829_comment'></div>厥今内寇粗消，而鸿雁未集，岳牧之臣，若之何而弗遴也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309829_comment'></div>淮服初平，而杕杜劝归，捍御之臣，若之何而反阙也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309829_comment'></div>臣窃以为疏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309829_comment'></div>臣愿陛下察天下之势，犹人之居室，不可有一隙漏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309829_comment'></div>察天下之人才，犹造室而择木，不可以一旦求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309829_comment'></div>如京师，如吴越，如江淮，如湘广，如京蜀，凡重地要区，与二三大臣是究是图，必惟其人，且蓄之贰，庶几临事无仓卒乏才之叹，亦无缓慢不及事之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309829_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309829_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1309829'>〔贴黄〕臣闻之道路，残金遣使，欲以淮阴、盱眙两城，求成于我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309829_comment'></div>使其果出于诚，继好息兵，岂非目前幸事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309829_comment'></div>但臣私忧过计，窃以本朝交金之初，正以幽燕故地，彼以和误我，我以和自误，非一日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309829_comment'></div>今其衰微丧败之馀，决无曩时气势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309829_comment'></div>然蜂虿有毒，困兽犹斗，积其累年绝币之怨，宁无求快于我之心？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309829_comment'></div>万一姑以和款我，閒费我日力，消沮我士心，宽弛我备御，而彼得以从容暇豫，酝酿奸谋，乘间窥伺，噬脐何及！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309829_comment'></div>又况逆全党类，尚存馀息，岂容以不可必之和议，而废吾所当严之实备乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309829_comment'></div>臣愚欲望圣断戒谕边臣，精选间谍，察其情伪，修饬守备，防其冲突，和之与否，亟求定论，毋为迁延两可，以误大计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309829_comment'></div>此亦有备无患、事豫则立之谊也，并乞留神省察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1309829_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1231&endYear=1231')">1231年</a>　贻书丞相史弥远论六事。作品：《上史相书·史弥远当国，火后上六事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷四。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1231&endYear=1231')">1231年</a>　与同僚上书论救火赏罚未当。作品：《再上史相书·论救火赏罚未当》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷四。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1232&endYear=1232')">1232年3月</a>　三月，友人游似赴任夔路转运判官，有词送之。作品：《鹧鸪天·和古乐府韵送游景仁将漕夔门》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_103322' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103322' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103322?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鹧鸪天 和古乐府韵送游景仁将漕夔门</a><span class='authorDate'>（1232年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103322")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103322_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103322'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103322'>去日春山淡翠眉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103322_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103322'>到家恰好整寒衣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103322_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103322'>人归玉垒天应惜，舟过吴江月半垂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103322_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103322'>千万绪，两三卮。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103322_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103322'>送君不忍与君违。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103322_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103322'>书来频寄西边讯，是我江南肠断时。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_103322_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1232&endYear=1232')">1232年</a>　奏论大顺之理贯通天人，当以此为致治之本。作品：《奏论大顺之理贯通天人当以此为致治之本》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_1309830' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309830' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309830?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏论大顺之理贯通天人当以此为致治之本</a><span class='authorDate'>（1232年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309830")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309830_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309830'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309830'>臣闻天下有大顺，贯通于天人，而纲维于君臣上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309830_comment'></div>自昔帝王，或肇造区宇，或削平祸乱，或垂世立统，或继志述事，大抵顺之则兴，逆之则仆，顺之则治，逆之则乱，顺之则成，逆之则败，断断乎不可易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309830_comment'></div>《书》曰「惠迪吉，从逆凶」，《易》曰「豫顺以动，顺以动豫，故天地如之」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309830_comment'></div>《礼》曰「明于顺，则能守危」，《传》曰「顺天者存，逆天者亡」，皆是物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309830_comment'></div>比者叛贼獗猖，疆埸纷扰，瞰江窥海，闻见惊疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309830_comment'></div>王怒奋张，庙算坚决，更革内地之牧守，责任边方之阃帅，矢之天而天默契，质之人而人允协，遂歼元恶，旋复坚城，顺之为效，捷于影响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309830_comment'></div>以此一事而推之于万事，无往而非顺，则无往而非吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309830_comment'></div>厥今外虞粗弭，人情颇舒，近辅小丰，谷直渐减，比故冬边遽之日与今夏潦降之时，顿宽厥忧，宁不可贺？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309830_comment'></div>然警告于天，则星文错异，百川涨腾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309830_comment'></div>变见于人，则江淮民流，畿甸寇作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309830_comment'></div>东楚虽归而两城犹未下，羌鞑虽退而西陲犹未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309830_comment'></div>忠智怀疑而不肯赴国家之急，憸壬伺间而反欲幸朝廷之菑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309830_comment'></div>察證观形，寻源溯本，无乃设施布置，犹有未顺于天者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309830_comment'></div>犹有未顺于人者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309830_comment'></div>犹有悖理而伤道，干和而召盭者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309830_comment'></div>盖人主端拱于宫阙，必孝于亲，必诚于身，必力戒耽乐，必喜闻忠直，必念闾阎之疾苦，必知稼穑之艰难，必疏便僻侧媚，必近正士端人，而后谓之顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309830_comment'></div>二三执政，弼谐于廊庙，必开诚心，必布公道，必与天下均其好恶，必与百姓同其视听，必进循良忠实之士，必斥险诐暴刻之徒，必崇气节，必尚廉隅，而后谓之顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309830_comment'></div>内而群有司百执事，必以公灭私，必以理制欲，必务节俭，必戒奔竞，必勤劳振职，必蹇谔尽言，必惩吏强官弱之风，必革弃法用例之习，而后谓之顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309830_comment'></div>外而监司郡守，必拳拳奉国，必孜孜爱民，必视公事如家事，必惜官物如己物，必绝囊橐，必止苞苴，必抑豪夺而矜鳏寡，必先教化而后刑罚，而后谓之顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309830_comment'></div>夫自天子而达之内外大小之臣，皆周旋于大顺之中，协气薰蒸，至于磅礴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309830_comment'></div>其应于天，则为景星，为甘露，为大祲，为屡丰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309830_comment'></div>其应于人，则为孝弟，为忠义，为尊君，为亲上，亦曰顺而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309830_comment'></div>一或反此，以吾之不顺，格彼之不顺，就目前之隐忧显患，长此将安终穷！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309830_comment'></div>臣愿陛下念祖宗之洪基大业，积累孔艰，察今日之天意人心，维持匪易，恐惧修省，身以顺率之，二三大臣而下，咸以顺辅之，谓不基平治、致中兴，延洪亿万年无疆之休，臣不信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309830_comment'></div>惟陛下裁幸。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1309830_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1232&endYear=1232')">1232年7月</a>　七月，迁太府少卿，总领淮西财赋。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='557178276bed441b8b9556c7bead53f0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("557178276bed441b8b9556c7bead53f0");'><span id='557178276bed441b8b9556c7bead53f0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1236')">1236年</a>，42岁</div><div id='557178276bed441b8b9556c7bead53f0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1236')">1236年</a>　权工部侍郎，知江州，辞不赴。请养宗子以系国本。作品：《奏乞选养宗子以系国本以镇人心》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1309840' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309840' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309840?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞选养宗子以系国本以镇人心</a><span class='authorDate'>（端平三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309840")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309840_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309840'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309840'>臣岁在癸巳之冬，待罪淮右饟事，恭奉求言之诏，尝僭条九事以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309840_comment'></div>其第二条，则乞陛下以社稷为心，遵用国朝典故，遴养小宗，以俟圣子之生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309840_comment'></div>盖导迎景贶，镇压群情，深计大虑，莫急于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309840_comment'></div>今阅三年矣，尚未闻有所施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309840_comment'></div>小人之家有千金之资，犹知反顾其后，陛下承祖宗三百年基业，独不念及此乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309840_comment'></div>臣一介疏逖，心切忠爱，是用不避鼎锅之诛，复祖前说以献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309840_comment'></div>惟陛下曲留圣衷，实社稷无疆之休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309840_comment'></div>并乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1309840_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='579620b9553844f8bb325d0daf09b4e3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("579620b9553844f8bb325d0daf09b4e3");'><span id='579620b9553844f8bb325d0daf09b4e3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1237')">1236-1237年</a>，42-43岁</div><div id='579620b9553844f8bb325d0daf09b4e3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1236')">1236年11月</a>　十一月，赴阙。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1237')">1237年</a>　改权兵部侍郎，兼检正。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1237')">1237年</a>　奏论士大夫私意之弊。作品：《奏论士大夫私意之弊》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1309841' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309841' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309841?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏论士大夫私意之弊</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉熙元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309841")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309841_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309841'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309841'>臣尝服膺先正沂公王曾之论曰，士大夫要当纯意国事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309841_comment'></div>纯之为言，一而不二之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309841_comment'></div>一则公，二则私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309841_comment'></div>甚矣私之为害也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309841_comment'></div>理有是非，私汩之则是者非，非者是；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309841_comment'></div>事有可否，私乘之则可者否而否者可；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309841_comment'></div>人有贤佞，私怵之则贤者佞而佞者贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309841_comment'></div>议论以私而不同心，则建明于此者彼之所疵瑕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309841_comment'></div>政事以私而不同力，则规置于甲者乙之所沮挠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309841_comment'></div>有观望而无忧爱，有虚诞而无忠实，有倾轧而无协和，物我对立于胸中，而国家若置于度外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309841_comment'></div>呜呼，此岂非今日士大夫之大弊哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309841_comment'></div>《书》曰：「无有作好，遵王之道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309841_comment'></div>无有作恶，遵王之路」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309841_comment'></div>作之为义，人而不天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309841_comment'></div>在昔疆埸无虞之时，臣固以逆忧其兆世道之消长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309841_comment'></div>及四郊多垒之后，则浸浸关国步之安危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309841_comment'></div>至于今日，封疆日蹙，烟焰日逼，万事不理，而尚以私爱憎、私恩怨为心，则消长安危，又不足言，将直系天下之存亡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309841_comment'></div>不幸变故之来，无及于救，当是时也，毋论名位之崇卑，毋分趋向之同异，槩堕涂炭，虽悔曷追！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309841_comment'></div>《传》曰「皮之不存，毛将安傅」，言之至此，可为于邑也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309841_comment'></div>昔苻坚欲谋伐晋，权翼以谓谢安、桓冲皆江左伟人，君臣辑睦，内外一心，未可图也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309841_comment'></div>晋将平吴，羊祜曰：吴濒江为国，东西数千里，所备者大，而将疑于朝，士困于野，兵临之际，必有应者，终不能齐力致死可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309841_comment'></div>夫内外一心，则晋不可攻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309841_comment'></div>不能齐力致死，则吴可灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309841_comment'></div>常人之虑，虑于有形；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309841_comment'></div>智者之虑，虑于无形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309841_comment'></div>夷狄之侵侮，天下之所共危，士大夫私愤之轇轕，臣之所独惧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309841_comment'></div>欲望陛下念祖业浸淫而将倾，伤士习陵夷而已坏，以静专察群动，以刚明消众慝，警于有位，各励至公，毋以违顺观人言，毋以毁誉行己意，毋以巧数相高，而以事功相勉，毋以阴计相间，而以识虑相先，有志之士则相与爱护，而毋操同室之戈，任事之人则相与扶持，而毋幸邻国之壑，协谋并智，戮力一忱，则危者尚可以安，而衰败之症尚可起也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309841_comment'></div>且前岁襄汉溃决，兴沔破亡，去岁两淮俶扰，三川陷没，今岁向春，纵使边遽稍缓，迟至秋冬，急症恐甚于前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309841_comment'></div>讲求救死扶伤之策，只有半年日力，惟君臣之间，勿以常言忽之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309841_comment'></div>臣不胜恳切，取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309841_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1309841'>〔贴黄〕臣又闻国以人重，亦以人轻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309841_comment'></div>国以人兴，亦以人废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309841_comment'></div>时当艰虞，固急于才智功名之士，而尤急于刚正骨鲠之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309841_comment'></div>昔晋大史屠馀见平公骄而无德义，知晋之将乱，以其图归于周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1309841_comment'></div>周桓公问天下之国孰先亡者，对曰：「晋先亡」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1309841_comment'></div>桓公问其说，对曰：「臣告之，邻国之不服，贤良之不兴」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1309841_comment'></div>公曰：「何害」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1309841_comment'></div>曰：「是谓不知所以存，所以亡，臣故曰晋先亡」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1309841_comment'></div>居三年而晋果亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1309841_comment'></div>桓公又问其次，曰：「中山」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1309841_comment'></div>又二年而中山亦亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1309841_comment'></div>桓公见其言之验，又问其次，而屠馀不肯对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1309841_comment'></div>固问之，则曰：「君次之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1309841_comment'></div>桓公惧，求国之贤者，得锜畴、田邑而礼之，又得史理、赵巽以为谏臣，以告屠馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1309841_comment'></div>曰：「君如此，可以保君之身」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1309841_comment'></div>汉淮南王谋乱，而其所惮者不在于公孙弘、卫青，以谓弘可说而青可刺者，而所惮者汲黯而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1309841_comment'></div>黯之居官，无以踰人，其功名才智，史未之见也，独以其能面折廷诤，有仗节死义之风，而乱臣贼子为之畏沮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1309841_comment'></div>然则刚正骨鲠之臣，其有益于人之国固如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1309841_comment'></div>曩者陛下躬揽政权，招徕众正，布在列位，不幸而臣德秀、臣咨夔、臣重珍相继沦没，其幸而存者，又皆流落江湖之上矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1309841_comment'></div>孟子曰：「王无亲臣矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1309841_comment'></div>昔者所进，今日不知其亡也，臣诚伤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1309841_comment'></div>欲望陛下明诏宰辅，择其最系人望而关民誉者，亟加收召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1309841_comment'></div>或还之于政涂，或归之于禁路，或反之于言责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1309841_comment'></div>贤者之领袖，既登进于朝廷，自能气类薰蒸，善人毕集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1309841_comment'></div>岂惟猛虎在山，藜藿不采，庶几国论归一，人心底定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1309841_comment'></div>士大夫之背公植私者，外有所矜式，内有所顾忌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1309841_comment'></div>其于天下国家，夫岂小补！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1309841_comment'></div>若曰端平以来，用贤而治不加进，遂以为贤者有虚名而无实用，例加厌薄之心，则失之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1309841_comment'></div>管仲曰：「有人而弗能知，害霸也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1309841_comment'></div>用而弗能信，害伯也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1309841_comment'></div>信而以小人参之，害伯也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1309841_comment'></div>不知陛下昔者之用贤，果能知之乎，知而果能信之乎，信而果能不以小人参之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1309841_comment'></div>今日之势，犹大病之人，众医束手，莫适为策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1309841_comment'></div>使其聚参苓芝术之剂以扶病者，万有一焉，元气之复还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1309841_comment'></div>若投以乌喙狼毒，则立毙矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1309841_comment'></div>此臣区区纳忠之悃款也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1309841_comment'></div>退念臣生晚学陋，实不足以望时贤之分寸，陛下徒以其粗尝服劳州县，擢置法从，内顾愧惕，莫知称塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1309841_comment'></div>故尤愿陛下登崇贤哲，以重本朝，则臣厕迹禁近，预有光荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1309841_comment'></div>并乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_68_1309841_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1237')">1237年</a>　奏论制国之事不惧则轻，徒惧则沮。作品：《奏论制国之事不惧则轻徒惧则沮》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1309842' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309842' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309842?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏论制国之事不惧则轻徒惧则沮</a><span class='authorDate'>（1237年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309842")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309842_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309842'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309842'>臣闻善制国者，先事不可不惧，已事不可徒惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309842_comment'></div>先事而不惧则失之轻，已事而徒惧则失之沮，皆非所以经纶世务而康济时屯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309842_comment'></div>陛下尊居九有，十四年矣，宝、绍而来，十载之岁月，虚掷于旧弼，岂惟天下之人惜之，虽陛下亦自惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309842_comment'></div>故端平改元，锐意兴起，平治之期，岂惟天下之人望之，虽陛下亦自望之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309842_comment'></div>而庙谟乖疏，政体丛脞，曰鼓铸，曰收币，曰变钞，曰恢疆，曰蒐卒，曰税亩，大率不审而遽行，既行而骤止，小则贻笑于国人，大则纳侮于夷狄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309842_comment'></div>于是更化而来，三载之岁月，又虚掷于旧傅，此先事不惧而失于轻之明验也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309842_comment'></div>今日天下，又非端平初年比矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309842_comment'></div>昔有危脉而今有危形，昔有亡理而今有亡證。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309842_comment'></div>回皇四顾，凛乎旦夕之不可保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309842_comment'></div>使贾谊复生，岂止痛哭流涕而已哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309842_comment'></div>然上有隐忧而无定虑，下有丛言而无实念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309842_comment'></div>每日而朝，群臣跪起而退则已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309842_comment'></div>间日而讲，儒臣诵说而退则已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309842_comment'></div>百司庶府，分曹列局，朝而出，暮而入，谨按文书，奉行常程则已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309842_comment'></div>幸而有论建之臣，条陈利害，粗中肯綮，可以见之施行者，又不过空费笔札，为缙绅间相与传诵之具则已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309842_comment'></div>泛泛悠悠，奄奄息息，若将一委之数而付之无可奈何者，毋乃徒惧而失于沮乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309842_comment'></div>少康以一旅兴夏，勾践以一栖伯越，燕以千里而畏人，楚以六千里而为雠人役，强弱无定势也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309842_comment'></div>厉王板荡之馀，周室衰矣，宣王继之则勃兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309842_comment'></div>宣帝厉精之馀，汉室昌矣，元、成继之则浸微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309842_comment'></div>难易无常时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309842_comment'></div>然则人能为时与势矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309842_comment'></div>陛下操大权，握神器，有土地人民，有甲兵士马，纪虽紊而纲尚存，裘虽弊而领固在，挈提振起，风采立异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309842_comment'></div>顾可听势之趋，任时之坏，而不为祖宗数百年社稷计乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309842_comment'></div>祖宗数百年社稷，在陛下之身，而扶持祖宗数百年社稷，在陛下之志而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309842_comment'></div>志立则有深思，思深则有真见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309842_comment'></div>必卑躬侧身，必勤邦俭家，必敷求真才而笃信之，必讲明实政而力行之，必不踵叔季之事以稔衰乱，必不口圣贤之言以务文饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309842_comment'></div>心诚意笃，精通气应，虽值艰难之会，自有挽回之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309842_comment'></div>如其惧而不戒，忧而不图，恶危而不计安，畏亡而不求存，寄时日于观娱，付危机于坐视，则前代倾危之辙，载在史册，有所不忍言矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309842_comment'></div>昔卫文公知畏狄难，至于服大布之衣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309842_comment'></div>汉高祖将图天下，至于妇女无所幸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309842_comment'></div>光武欲恢祖业，至于不御酒肉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309842_comment'></div>故曰「舜何人也，予何人也，有为者亦若是」，又曰「以齐王犹反掌也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309842_comment'></div>圣贤岂欺后世哉，然则在陛下而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309842_comment'></div>臣一介孤踪，去国五祀，陛下虽有兼采菲葑之度，而微臣邈无进效忠益之阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1309842_comment'></div>间尝随事献言，身远虑疏，祇取媢忌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1309842_comment'></div>退伏山林，自分已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1309842_comment'></div>陛下感于微末之长，并召时髦，下及庸陋，身未造阙，已玷除书，天地恩深，若为报称！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1309842_comment'></div>惟有竭尽底蕴，万一补助涓埃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1309842_comment'></div>然臣窃观时事丝纷毫委，高言之则恐以为迂阔而难行，浅言之则又病于猥细而无益，故愿陛下立志以先之，则夫疗疾之方，对證之剂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1309842_comment'></div>臣虽至愚，尚当殚虑研精，深维熟计，继此以进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1309842_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1309842_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1309842'>〔贴黄〕臣尝观先正魏公张浚《中兴备览》，其议固结人心，谓：「方天下无事之时，君臣上下之分，其势足以相维，虽人君不能修治其身，及绳正其左右，以失天下之心，其为祸也尚迟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1309842_comment'></div>乃若艰难多故，敌情不测，人心易怨，君人者倘有差失，祸乱不旋踵而作矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1309842_comment'></div>大势一去，不可复合，无以其微而忽之幸也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1309842_comment'></div>臣以为浚之言尤切于今日，伏惟陛下细加䌷绎，则必有惕然于圣衷者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1309842_comment'></div>并乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1309842_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1237')">1237年</a>　请分路取士，以收淮襄之人物，守淮襄之土地。作品：《奏乞分路取士以收淮襄之人物守淮襄之土地》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1309843' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309843' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309843?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞分路取士以收淮襄之人物守淮襄之土地</a><span class='authorDate'>（1237年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309843")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309843_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309843'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309843'>臣尝谓用淮襄之人物，守淮襄之土地，此不易之至计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309843_comment'></div>然国家之取士，与士之发身，所重者惟文科进士，而淮襄之士，率不利于科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309843_comment'></div>以每举春榜观之，淮西尚有三数人，而淮东则不逮矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309843_comment'></div>淮东间有一二人，而京湖则绝无矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309843_comment'></div>于是均、光、随、枣、郧、复、汉、沔之郊，士之预计偕者，往往不愿观光于上国，州郡为之劝驾而后就道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309843_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309843_comment'></div>不精于时文故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309843_comment'></div>士之精于时文者，闽为最，浙次之，江西东、湖南又次之，而每季之中第，亦以是为差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309843_comment'></div>淮襄之士，其入官者既少，则仕于淮襄者，居多闽、浙、江南之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309843_comment'></div>尝试以浅近之事论之，其便弓马，一不如土人也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309843_comment'></div>谙地里，二不如土人也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309843_comment'></div>耐风霜，三不如土人也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309843_comment'></div>熟虏之情伪及金鼓兵革之事，四不如土人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309843_comment'></div>以彼所习较此所不习，其难易之相去远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309843_comment'></div>然彼不得朝廷之官，无由仕于其土地，不中进士举，无由得朝廷之官，不能为时文，无由中进士举，则所谓用淮襄之人物守淮襄之土地者，其说终不可行矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309843_comment'></div>然则如之何则可？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309843_comment'></div>曰：分路取士而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309843_comment'></div>恭惟神宗皇帝慨念西北人才多废，尝议改贡举法，而先正司马光首建言，乞将诸路举人各立字号，考校大略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309843_comment'></div>谓古之取士，以郡国户口多少为率，或以德行，或以才能，随其所长，各有所取，近自族姻，远及夷狄，无小无大，不可遗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309843_comment'></div>今或数路之中，全无一人及第，则所遗多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309843_comment'></div>国家用人之法，非进士及第者不得美官，非善为经义诗赋者不得及第，非游学京师者不善为经义诗赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309843_comment'></div>然设官分职，以待贤能，大者道德器识，以弼谐教化，其次明察惠和，以绥拊州县，其次方略勇果，以捍御外侮，小者刑狱钱谷，以供给役使，岂可专取文艺之人，欲以备百官、清万事耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309843_comment'></div>然则四方之人，虽于文艺或有所短，而其馀所长者，有益于公家之用盖亦多矣，安可尽加弃斥，使终身不仕耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309843_comment'></div>其后遂将陕西五路举人，分项令考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309843_comment'></div>孝宗皇帝加惠三边，既诏四川类省专留两名，以取关外四州之士，又诏四川武举省试比试额通四十二人，以十分为率，利州路四分，取十六人，成都等路六分，取二十六人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309843_comment'></div>宁宗皇帝聿遵祖宗，遂诏武举省试，将京襄两淮人另行取放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309843_comment'></div>夫三圣当天下乂安时，其注意遐方之士犹若此，况今日乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309843_comment'></div>今日之势，非收京湖两淮之士以收京湖两淮之土豪，收京湖两淮之土豪以收京湖两淮之丁壮，臣恐秋风一高，鞑虏旋至，勇夫悍徒，无所系属，非越江而内鬨，则俯首以从鞑，深忧大患，将不在虏而在萧墙之内也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309843_comment'></div>臣愿陛下亟下明诏，自嘉熙三年省试为始，将京西、湖北、淮东、淮西举人，分路考校，并以十七人取一名，零分更与放一名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309843_comment'></div>庶几得淮襄之人物以守淮襄之土地，一利也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309843_comment'></div>因士以收其土豪，因土豪以收其丁壮，二利也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309843_comment'></div>稍抑时文之弊，以致有用之才，三利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309843_comment'></div>伏惟圣明以保封疆、复境土为念，特发睿断，宣谕中辅，速赐施行，多士幸甚，宗社幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309843_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1309843_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1309843'>〔贴黄〕臣尝以端平二年四路到省举人之数考之，淮东一百四十五人，湖北一百一十五人，京西五十九人，通计四百八十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1309843_comment'></div>若以大例十七人取一名，其过省者仅二十八人而已，初未尝多侵省试之额，而可以收四路之士心，亦何惮而不为也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1309843_comment'></div>并乞睿照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1309843_comment'></div>臣窃见京西七郡及湖北复州、荆门军、德安府、归、峡州，已行残破，今岁科举，各处士人未有就试之地，槐黄已迫，合议区处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1309843_comment'></div>臣愚欲乞行下京湖制置司，就江陵府踏逐寺观一所，立贡院，令项差官，合十二郡之士，混试一次，却以十二郡元来解额衮同取放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1309843_comment'></div>其十二郡曾请举人，不论已免解未免解，特许来检据，赴嘉熙二年省试一次，庶几少见朝廷悯恤之意，且足以招徕陷没郡县士人之心，其所关系，实为不小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1309843_comment'></div>并乞睿照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1309843_comment'></div>又臣观春秋之世，晋在中原，楚在夷狄，楚虽有材，晋实用之，故晋伯诸侯者百有馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1309843_comment'></div>其后典午之晋迁于建邺，久而习安，常以南士为高华，以北人为伧荒，由是中州豪杰悉归元氏，而江左所用，悉皆文脉纤巧之才，故晋不能保有中原，而六朝常有弱患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1309843_comment'></div>我高宗南渡，孝宗承之，立贤无方，意度恢阔，李世辅、王友直为将帅，王希吕、辛弃疾为率守监司，皆北来人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1309843_comment'></div>自故相外招李全之徒，而内实忌之，既使有所激而叛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1309843_comment'></div>而世之昧者习熟见闻，槩以厌薄疑忌为事，凡出于淮襄者已几待以胡粤，况自淮以北乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1309843_comment'></div>积疑成衅，积衅成叛，而范用吉、尚全、常进、郭胜辈，且皆为敌国于一水之外矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1309843_comment'></div>此由南北太分，既蓄之而反外之故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1309843_comment'></div>此意不改，豪杰不附，弃材以资敌，殆不止如春秋声子之所叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1309843_comment'></div>盖商鞅不用于魏，而秦孝取河西，王猛不归于晋，而苻坚取慕容，此则议者所不虑，而臣以为他日大可忧者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1309843_comment'></div>如从臣策，分路考士，不特多得淮襄之人以守淮襄之土，又可使因淮襄之俗以招北方之豪杰，是获才实，消奸雄，而朝廷不预知，习俗不骇异，事之善者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1309843_comment'></div>不然，岁年之后，立敌于北，各事其主，其患将有不可胜言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1309843_comment'></div>惟陛下与二三大臣熟图之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1309843_comment'></div>并乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1309843_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1237')">1237年</a>　暮春在临安，有词送吴昌裔。作品：《贺新郎·送吴季永侍郎》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_103213' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103213' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103213?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺新郎<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>送吴季永侍郎</a><span class='authorDate'>（1237年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103213")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103213_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103213'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103213'>说著成凄楚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103213'>正尘飞、岷峨滟滪，兔嗥狐舞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103213'>颇牧禁中留不住，弹压征西幕府。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103213'>便一舸、月汀烟渚。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103213'>四塞三关天样险，问何人、自辟鼪鼯路。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103213'>成败事，几今古。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103213'>荼蘼芍药春将暮。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103213'>最无情、飘零柳絮，搅人离绪。<div id='poem_sentence_7_103213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_103213'>屈指秋风吹雁信，应忆西湖夜雨。<div id='poem_sentence_8_103213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_103213'>谩岁月、消磨如许。<div id='poem_sentence_9_103213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_103213'>上下四方男子志，肯临歧、昵昵儿曹语。<div id='poem_sentence_10_103213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_103213'>呼大白，为君举。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_103213_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1237')">1237年</a>　暮春在临安，有词送吴泳。作品：《水调歌头·送叔永文昌》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_103111' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103111' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103111?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>送叔永文昌</a><span class='authorDate'>（1237年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103111")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103111_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103111'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103111'>才惜季方去，又更别元方。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103111_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103111'>惊心天上双凤，接翅下高冈。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103111_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103111'>万里瞿塘烟浪，一片昭亭云月，渺渺正相望。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103111_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103111'>夜雨连风壑，此意独凄凉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103111_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103111'>杜鹃声，犹不住，搅离肠。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103111_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103111'>黄鸡白酒，吾亦归兴动家乡。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103111_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103111'>人事纷纷难料，世事悠悠难说，何处问穹苍。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103111_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103111'>肯落儿曹泪，一笑付沧浪。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_103111_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1237')">1237年4月</a>　四月，以权兵部侍郎兼同修国史、实录院同修撰。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1237')">1237年</a>　初夏，有词寄吴昌裔。作品：《满江红·和吴季永侍郎见寄》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_996108' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_996108' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/996108?labeling=true' target='_blank'>满江红 和吴季永侍郎见寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1237年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_996108")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_996108_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_996108'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_996108'>乍雨还晴，正轻暖轻寒帘幕。<div id='poem_sentence_0_996108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_996108'>时怅望、故人烟水，鹭翻鸥落。<div id='poem_sentence_1_996108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_996108'>老去可堪离恨结，新来转觉吟情薄。<div id='poem_sentence_2_996108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_996108'>况等闲、客里送年华，成挥霍。<div id='poem_sentence_3_996108_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_996108'>天一顾，西南角。<div id='poem_sentence_4_996108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_996108'>人万里，风埃阔。<div id='poem_sentence_5_996108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_996108'>笑长卿归蜀，锦衣徒著。<div id='poem_sentence_6_996108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_996108'>不是等闲螳臂怒，也休刚道鸡声恶。<div id='poem_sentence_7_996108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_996108'>但千年、往事误平凉，今番莫。<div id='poem_sentence_8_996108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_996108'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_996108_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='d1ed2b8479c4427fad5103fd1c88d0e4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d1ed2b8479c4427fad5103fd1c88d0e4");'><span id='d1ed2b8479c4427fad5103fd1c88d0e4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1240&endYear=1241')">1240-1241年</a>，46-47岁</div><div id='d1ed2b8479c4427fad5103fd1c88d0e4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1240&endYear=1240')">1240年</a>　进工部尚书，改吏部尚书兼知临安府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1240&endYear=1240')">1240年2月</a>　二月上疏，乞遵旧法收士子监漕试。作品：《奏乞遵旧法收士子监漕试》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1309856' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309856' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309856?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞遵旧法收士子监漕试</a><span class='authorDate'>（1240年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309856")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309856_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309856'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309856'>臣顷在仲春，恭睹明诏，嘉庆历、元祐之词章，乐乾道、淳熙之儒术，思得贤能之士，上追盛时，有曰「攸介攸止，烝我髦士，有司之事也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309856_comment'></div>大哉王言，所望于兴贤兴能者厚矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309856_comment'></div>窃意廷臣必能上体圣心，开宽裕之路，毕臻众俊，乃旬日以来，所闻特异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309856_comment'></div>卿大夫士，咸谓新令具严，虽亲子孙亲弟侄，合牒国子监试者，于保官二员外，更用局长保明，以此各怀疑忌，重费料理，将遂遣其骨肉之亲，归就里选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309856_comment'></div>至如四方士子，或为监司守倅之客及亲者，则谓旧法牒试既不可复，今又罢寓试而行附试，取人至狭，皆欲弃科举而不应诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309856_comment'></div>臣窃惑焉，何前日诏旨之广，而今日法令之密，岂阳欲求之而阴实沮之也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309856_comment'></div>臣窃惟国家之事，惟当以祖宗成法为重，法茍未为极弊，不必自取多事可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309856_comment'></div>况取士之要，不过在于得人，得人之方，不专在于用法令也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309856_comment'></div>舍先朝之宽博，用新令之蹇狭，所以待士者，其意已薄，则庆历、元祐、乾道、淳熙之盛美，尚可得而望哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309856_comment'></div>臣窃观绍兴十三年指挥，文武职事官，本宗同居五服内，并异居大功以上亲，釐务官、文臣京官、武臣朝官，本宗同居小功以上亲，并许牒赴国子监取应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309856_comment'></div>乾道、淳熙以来，并遵此令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309856_comment'></div>嘉定十二年，虽曾亲立武臣只牒武举之制，至陛下即位，悉仍绍兴、乾道、淳熙之旧，法简意宽，鸢鱼飞跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309856_comment'></div>奈何今日乃束缚而蹙狭之也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309856_comment'></div>臣又观乾道重修贡举令，诸在京职事官，文臣监察御史以上，武臣职事杂压在监察御史以上者，并牒门客一人，赴本路运司收试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309856_comment'></div>至于监司之客与亲，听牒邻路，守倅之客与亲，听牒本路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309856_comment'></div>皆由妨嫌，所当避互，初非优异，故为名色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309856_comment'></div>自端平增贡额，而监司守倅门客之试罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309856_comment'></div>夫意其非客非亲之冒牒，而并废其实亲实客之当牒，亦岂良法？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309856_comment'></div>爰至今日，既不尽复，又不尽罢，亦徒为多事而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309856_comment'></div>臣典司浩穰，岂皇他恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309856_comment'></div>然念班忝法从，职与经筵，于朝廷之事皆所当言，用敢列绍兴以来之明令，述宝庆初元之盛心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309856_comment'></div>仰望陛下亟颁睿旨，悉还旧法，内而监牒凡属同居异居、小功大功以上亲者，只用牒官保官状收试外，而漕牒凡属门客姑姨之亲者，亦如用牒官保官状收试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309856_comment'></div>厚以待卿大夫，而不必逆其诈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309856_comment'></div>宽以待天下士，而不必多其防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309856_comment'></div>庶几圣度开广，同符祖宗，与近者宾兴之诏旨始不相违，用此取士，所得必多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309856_comment'></div>其有不顾清议，或为伪冒，事觉之后，并以条制坐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309856_comment'></div>在上得体，在下无辞，是亦祖宗用法之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309856_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1309856'>〔贴黄〕臣窃见嘉熙元年，大臣奏请创行寓试，凡卿监郎官监司倅之门客，及姑姨之亲、同宗之子弟，与游士之不便于归乡就试者，滚同试于转运司，以四十人为额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309856_comment'></div>虽其中或有实系门客姑姨之亲者，不能无嫌，犹不失宽大之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309856_comment'></div>秪缘得废待补，以致次年分路补试，耳目不及，所取淆杂，遂为论者所疵，竟罢今举寓试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309856_comment'></div>以臣鄙见，陛下如采用臣言，尽复绍兴、乾道、淳熙之令，且照嘉熙元年新令，放行寓试，却仍旧法，复取待补，亦自甚便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309856_comment'></div>但于内有府学诸生，月书分数，类申国子监者，三年在学，实为辛勤，合与比附大学教养之数，另项考校，少增其额，以示优异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309856_comment'></div>庶于不均齐之中，乃有至均齐之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309856_comment'></div>并乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1309856_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1240&endYear=1240')">1240年</a>　奏论艰屯蹇困之时，非反身修德，无以求穷通之理。作品：《内引第一札奏论艰屯蹇困之时非反身修德则无以求亨通之理》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1309857' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309857' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309857?labeling=true' target='_blank'>内引第一劄奏论艰屯蹇困之时非反身修德则无以求亨通之理</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉熙四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309857")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309857_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309857'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309857'>臣一介庸虚，仰蒙圣恩，俯锡召纶，旋加亲擢，获奉穆清之对，敢尽责难之恭，惟睿慈垂听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309857_comment'></div>臣闻《易》曰「云雷屯，君子以经纶」，是艰屯之时，乃君子所以经纶其大业也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309857_comment'></div>又曰「山上有水蹇，君子以反身修德」，是蹇难之世，非反身修德，无以自济也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309857_comment'></div>又曰「困亨」，是困厄之中，有亨通之理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309857_comment'></div>厥今事势，陛下既自熟于圣心矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309857_comment'></div>披猖之虏，如蠹旁蚀，而四肢已断；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309857_comment'></div>流徙之民，如疽方结，而腹心可虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309857_comment'></div>耗者众而粟力竭，出者多而楮力竭，行伍咨嗟，市廛诽议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309857_comment'></div>怨气上干，极为今年之彗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309857_comment'></div>怨声下彻，极为去年之潮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309857_comment'></div>此其为坎盈之屯、艮险之蹇与泽无水之困，盖已在天成象，在地成形矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309857_comment'></div>然而此正陛下经纶之日，反身修德，在困求亨之时也，特未知所以应此者何如耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309857_comment'></div>夫水漂而火焚之，盗迫而邻侵之，当此之际，未有不重足而栗、捣心而悲者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309857_comment'></div>俄而贲育过焉，则嘻笑赴之，而懦者皆起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309857_comment'></div>夫血气之勇，犹足以胜危惧而当祸患，况勇于义理而以帝王之位行之乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309857_comment'></div>故夫有土不可以为贫，有民不可以为弱，有庆赏刑威则不患不能奔走群动，有利势操柄则不患不能旋斡万为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309857_comment'></div>少康兴于一旅，句践伯于一栖，燕以千里而畏人，楚以六千里而为雠人役，何相远若是哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309857_comment'></div>大抵自古未尝无大坏极弊之时，亦未尝无扶衰救病之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309857_comment'></div>其或乍仆而忽起，寖微而终否者，全在时君世主之勇不勇而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309857_comment'></div>天下之至不勇者，莫若秦皇、汉武，惟成汤为智勇，文武为大勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309857_comment'></div>盖刚者君德之体，健者君德之用，自刚而克，由健而发，是之谓天德之勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309857_comment'></div>乾以静专，坤以直大，皆是物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309857_comment'></div>陛下宽简如尧，克勤如禹，柔恭如文王，可谓有帝王之资，惟在充而用之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309857_comment'></div>用之莫先于去心过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309857_comment'></div>何为心过？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309857_comment'></div>一曰欲，二曰慢，三曰欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309857_comment'></div>且天下之事极矣，惟天回则事可回，而此三者之过，乃所以斁天理、亵天威而怠忽天命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309857_comment'></div>是故有欲心者，与天为二矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309857_comment'></div>有慢心者，不知有天矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309857_comment'></div>有欺心者，则又以天资口耳，而不以天事身心矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309857_comment'></div>陛下于此用吾勇焉，如刀断丝，如堤截水，微去之，渐去之，顿去之，以至于尽去之，则三者之心，雨晞雾散，而清明见矣，何忧乎潮汐，何畏乎彗孛，何患乎回鞑！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309857_comment'></div>困之能亨，蹇之自反，屯之经纶，孰有妙于此乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309857_comment'></div>臣请复述前闻，以赞陛下之勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309857_comment'></div>我太宗皇帝之端拱二年六月，彗出东井之积木，日见东北，夕见西北，历右摄提，阅三十日，至亢乃灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1309857_comment'></div>其后大观四年五月，彗出自王良造父，历阁道，入紫宫，干帝座，二十馀日而灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1309857_comment'></div>我仁宗皇帝之至和三年七月，连雨不止，水入国门，渰浸太社，破缺城垣，城外冢墓，皆遭漂荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1309857_comment'></div>其后宣和元年六月积水暴至，迨近都城，漂没人民庐舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1309857_comment'></div>夫去年之潮，今年之彗，其与先朝何异？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1309857_comment'></div>然端拱、至和，不过一时之灾，而大观、宣和之后，其事有不忍道者，陛下将何鉴哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1309857_comment'></div>臣不胜忧爱之情，惟陛下裁之，幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1309857_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1309857_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1240&endYear=1240')">1240年</a>　奏乞遴选近族，以系人望而俟太子之生。作品：《内引第二札奏乞遴选近族以系属人心而俟太子之生》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1309858' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309858' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309858?labeling=true' target='_blank'>内引第二劄奏乞遴选近族以系属人心而俟太子之生</a><span class='authorDate'>（1240年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309858")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309858_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309858'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309858'>臣仰惟皇帝陛下发祥艺祖，继体宁皇，以历数考之，中天再造，蛰蛰绳绳，实当陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309858_comment'></div>弧韣屡应，匕鬯尚虚，陛下虽有诒谋垂裕之永图，思欲为社稷万世之至计，而犹豫虚徐，未有赞其决者，非所以申固天命，系属人心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309858_comment'></div>按祖宗故实，甲观未期则遴选近族，前星既协则归奉宗藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309858_comment'></div>真宗皇帝六年，适有周王之戚，即取宗室子养于宫中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309858_comment'></div>及仁宗既就外傅，则宗室子亦归邸矣，濮安懿王是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309858_comment'></div>明道元年，仁宗皇帝圣寿二十有二，而安懿生子，又数年亦取养于宫中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309858_comment'></div>其后后宫多就馆者，而王子乃还濮邸，用前例也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309858_comment'></div>绍兴五年，高宗皇帝谓宰相曰「朕年已二十九，尚未有子」，且谓自有国朝故事，当导迎景贶，镇压群疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309858_comment'></div>事体得宜，意虑及远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309858_comment'></div>此实累圣大公至正之度，非若汉唐叔末讳护牵制之为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309858_comment'></div>夫以仁皇春秋甫二十三，高皇春秋甫二十九，真皇即位之六年，亦少陛下两岁，而长虑却顾皆若此，陛下宁不以祖宗之心为心乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309858_comment'></div>前古辙迹，载在简编，多以仓卒之间，稔成衰乱之證，可为永监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309858_comment'></div>故臣深愿曲留圣虑，特采旧章，博求小宗，必有岐嶷，少迟绿车之出，以俟朱邸之还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309858_comment'></div>百世本支，万年基绪，实系于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309858_comment'></div>臣驽下，虽不能为皇祐之司马光，亦粗为绍兴之娄寅亮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309858_comment'></div>惟陛下裁赦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309858_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1309858_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1240&endYear=1240')">1240年5月</a>　夏五月初，奏论尹京三事非其所能。作品：《内引第三札奏论尹京三事非其所能》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1309859' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309859' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309859?labeling=true' target='_blank'>内引第三劄奏论尹京三事非其所能</a><span class='authorDate'>（1240年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309859")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309859_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309859'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309859'>臣至愚极陋，仰荷陛下非常特达之知，猥加拔擢，叠组两部，兼领神皋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309859_comment'></div>盖尝蚤夜而思，窃以为才有短长，时有艰易，物有盈虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309859_comment'></div>如臣之才，使之抚摩百姓，则粗可勉竭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309859_comment'></div>使之发奸摘伏，则非其所能矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309859_comment'></div>使之驱驰外服，则粗可勉竭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309859_comment'></div>使之弹压众大之区，则非其所能矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309859_comment'></div>使之持法守，奉理道，则粗可勉竭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309859_comment'></div>使之酬应人情，周旋世态，则非其所能矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309859_comment'></div>此所谓才有短长者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309859_comment'></div>历参时变，载考京邑，禧、泰之际艰于乾、淳，宝、绍之时艰于禧、泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309859_comment'></div>端、熙以来，其难又非昔日之比矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309859_comment'></div>陛下异时择牧，率皆八面疏通之士，犹惧弗济，况臣迂愚钝拙，与物多忤者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309859_comment'></div>此所谓时有艰易者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309859_comment'></div>米乃民之命脉，而苦于直之涌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309859_comment'></div>楮乃民之血脉，而苦于直之低。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309859_comment'></div>四民之道俱穷，百物之产不继，谈河不可以止渴，画饼何能以充饥！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309859_comment'></div>此所谓物有盈虚者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309859_comment'></div>重惟本朝上以文明启治功，下以儒雅成习俗，凡投身簿书狱讼之间，甲兵钱谷之内，纵使学者，亦贻俗吏之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309859_comment'></div>先帝朝，徐谊、徐邦宪号一时名流，皆尝尹正京畿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309859_comment'></div>先臣某实与之为友，每以书责之，谓非秀才所当做官职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309859_comment'></div>臣以圣意坚决，圣恩深厚，未免冒清议，违先训，勉服威命，惶惧就职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309859_comment'></div>虽欲刻苦奋励，图报万分，然际时之难，适事之极，恐决无以仰副陛下选择而使之之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309859_comment'></div>昔赵母指括之必败，以全其宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309859_comment'></div>臣有老母，预乞圣慈曲轸危悃，他日姑从薄罚，不为亲忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309859_comment'></div>臣无任陨越恳祈之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309859_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1309859_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1240&endYear=1240')">1240年5月</a>　五月戊子，兼侍读经筵。作品：《经筵奏论救楮之策所关系者莫重于公私之籴》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1309860' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309860' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309860?labeling=true' target='_blank'>经筵奏论救楮之策所关系者莫重于公私之籴</a><span class='authorDate'>（1240年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309860")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309860_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309860'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309860'>臣一介迂疏，猥叨亲擢，典神皋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309860_comment'></div>顷者锡对便朝，恭承王音，以钱楮为第一义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309860_comment'></div>臣祗服训词，不过宣布陛下德音志虑于众，而臣民亿兆，皆昭知陛下忧勤恳恻之心，靡然听从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309860_comment'></div>钱既流通，楮亦增重，目前市邑，粗免萧条急迫气象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309860_comment'></div>然臣反覆过计，以为此特制之于其末而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309860_comment'></div>譬之流水，曲为堤防，使不倾泄，故可以成一溉之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309860_comment'></div>若不浚其本源，俾之汪洋浩渺，不幸一隙不牢，堤防稍决，其涸可立而待，臣实未知其所终也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309860_comment'></div>本源者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309860_comment'></div>救楮而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309860_comment'></div>朝廷亟思所以救楮，则百物之价便可以损三分之二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309860_comment'></div>而其最所关系者，莫重于公私之籴事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309860_comment'></div>以朝廷和籴言之，则可以宽国计；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309860_comment'></div>以阎闾日籴言之，则可以宽民生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309860_comment'></div>夫古今未有石米之直为缗丝三四十千而国不穷，民不困，天下不危乱者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309860_comment'></div>臣以为天下大变大故，犹有自定之理，若财殚粟竭，不起而图之，则决无天雨财鬼输粟之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309860_comment'></div>《书》曰「弗为胡成」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309860_comment'></div>厥今事势，本未尽至于不可为，而君臣上下似欲以不为侥倖镇静之名、安平之福，臣不知其果何说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309860_comment'></div>况朝廷帑藏之储，已浸浸乎里巷富翁之不若，更三四月，边尘一惊，周章四顾，不审执事者将何以为陛下计乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309860_comment'></div>臣忧心如捣，惟陛下与二三大臣速图之，宗社幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309860_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1309860_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1240&endYear=1240')">1240年</a>　六月后，奏论庚子辛丑气数人事。作品：《奏论国朝庚子辛丑气数人事》<div id='poem_1309861' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309861' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309861?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏论国朝庚子辛丑气数人事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1240年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309861")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309861_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309861'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309861'>臣闻天运有吉凶之相推，世道有升降之相易，当其会虽圣君不能违，值其阨虽治世不能免，亦在于小心兢业而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309861_comment'></div>臣窃观比岁有火有潦，有风有潮，然而未有彗也，未有蝗也，未有旱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309861_comment'></div>乃今踵见于一年之间，浸淫于数月之久，众目恐怖而窃议，四鄙枵竭而坐完，田野焦枯而莫耕，河港断绝而弗济，不惟南亩之入杳无望期，抑使太仓之输邈有滞积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309861_comment'></div>是自比岁以来，极咎徵之备，丛沴气之多，未有今岁若也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309861_comment'></div>臣俯察物宜，仰稽造化，窃以为有气数焉，非人之所能逃也，有人事焉，非天之所能预也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309861_comment'></div>臣于是求之国史，盖国朝自膺大历服，至于咸平之二年三年，始得庚子、辛丑，自是而为嘉祐之五年六年，自是而为宣和之二年三年，自是而为淳熙之七年八年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309861_comment'></div>考其年，求其故，不有天灾，必有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1309861", 1309861, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>天变</span>，不有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1309861", 1309861, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>天变</span>，必有盗贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309861_comment'></div>盖二者皆火之仇，土之舍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309861_comment'></div>仇者得志，旺者告病，是亦阳九百六之会与！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309861_comment'></div>是故天狗堕于西南，彗心缠于星宿，日食地震，淫雨大水，禁卫为盗，民多流亡，嘉祐之庚子、辛丑然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309861_comment'></div>太阴荧惑，屡失其度，旱暵雨潦，相继为灾，湖南则曰旱势未已，广德则曰旱灾异常，严□□以十馀日，越之潦至八万亩，淳熙之庚子、辛丑然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309861_comment'></div>而其甚者，咸平则王均僭蜀，宣和则方腊盗浙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309861_comment'></div>计庚子、辛丑之间，二方之民，死于盗死于兵者，各以数十万计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309861_comment'></div>夫以真庙之恭俭，仁宗之宽仁，孝宗之忧勤，虽不幸而当此气数之交，要亦幸而当此圣明之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309861_comment'></div>是以因灾而慄慄，随事而孜孜，群臣尽言，大臣尽心，州县尽力，此其所以终保有咸平、嘉祐、淳熙之盛时，而不至为宣和之庚子、辛丑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309861_comment'></div>宣和惟其不然也，故祸作而政愈疵，变形而人愈缪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309861_comment'></div>凡自古所谓与乱同事者不极不止，而气数尽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309861_comment'></div>向非高宗以一旅兴于大江之南，则九庙之祀，未知所属也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309861_comment'></div>今陛下又不幸而逢庚子、辛丑之气数，姑舍咸平、嘉祐而概以淳熙，陛下有淳熙之忧而治不如，大臣有淳熙之枋任而协同不如，州县亦淳熙之天下而事力不如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309861_comment'></div>至于财殚粟匮，钱弊楮穷，强敌凭陵，骄卒桀傲，梁益俶扰，襄樊沦亡，人心动摇，国势兀隍，此又淳熙之所尽无而今日之所备有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309861_comment'></div>若上下勤恤，君臣克艰，汲汲皇皇，常若乱亡之迫其后，万一国尚可为，民尚可保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309861_comment'></div>不然，天与人莫之通，人与政莫之省，帝怒叵测，世数难回，臣恐均、腊之奸，将有伏于草莽饥寒窟者，同时而出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309861_comment'></div>其或邕广有一隙之虚，施黔有一罅之漏，江沱有一缝之缺，饥氓为流民之导，流民为贼寇之导，不知浮脆之□豢养之京师，将何以御之乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309861_comment'></div>臣闻未病而服药者上也，当病而服药者次也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309861_comment'></div>今不得而服未病之药矣，臣请勉其次者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309861_comment'></div>臣初闻医国之方于经传，最速于见效者，其药有三：一曰修身，二曰用贤，三曰畏天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309861_comment'></div>服此药者，必各有戒：修身之戒在欲，用贤之戒在谗，畏天之戒在欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309861_comment'></div>持此戒者，亦各有法：欲节欲莫如刚，欲远谗莫如明，欲去欺莫如敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309861_comment'></div>陛下非不服此药也，亦尝守此戒以待其效欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309861_comment'></div>陛下非不持此戒也，亦尝由此法以防其决欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309861_comment'></div>祸福同行，安危共辙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309861_comment'></div>宣和、淳熙，相去一间，女真、蒙靼，非有异人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309861_comment'></div>禹戒舜曰无若丹朱，旦戒成曰无若商受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309861_comment'></div>舜与成不为忤，禹与旦不为讦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1309861_comment'></div>盖君子之立本，皆出于天地之大义，期于以一念之真切相成，以万世之誉闻相保，上非冀其容悦，下非希其宠利，一于道而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1309861_comment'></div>臣诚不忍陛下以大有为之资，而浸浸于不可为之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1309861_comment'></div>天人之證日异，国家之事难言，是用罔避忌讳，俯伏陈露，庶几少启陛下瞿然惕然之思，而先自三者至心行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1309861_comment'></div>然后申敕二三大臣，惜分寸之光阴，以图回实政，采军民之公论，以布置人才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1309861_comment'></div>最急者莫如食，其次钱币。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1309861_comment'></div>若流民盗贼夷狄，皆当视以为必至之忧，无可疑之患，如在火焚水溺之中，求为脱一生于万死之计，庶几犹可及止也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1309861_comment'></div>咸平、嘉祐、淳熙之庚子、辛丑，不可望矣，宣和之庚子、辛丑，可复蹈乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1309861_comment'></div>臣不胜惓惓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1309861_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1309861_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1240&endYear=1240')">1240年8月21日</a>　八月二十一日轮进读，因奏尹京事并乞速归田里，遂免兼临安府。作品：《奏尹京事并乞速归田里》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1309862' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309862' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309862?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏尹京事并乞速归田里</a><span class='authorDate'>（1240年8月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309862")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309862_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309862'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309862'>臣窃见京都前日之虑有三，其最见钱之涩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309862_comment'></div>臣虽防之使不泄，诱之使不藏，然实仰托陛下威灵，善良听命，奸豪屏迹，钱陌顿还于旧观，市井不至于萧条，此臣之可藉以逃责者一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309862_comment'></div>其次潮汛之冲，臣虽增岸阔高，补堤圮坏，添筑子埂，旁护新塘，然实仰托陛下威灵，海门之淤既快，江浒之沙浸生，舟行西兴，潮复故道，此臣之可藉以逃责者二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309862_comment'></div>其次风烛之虞，臣虽立为规模，粗可防弭，然实仰托陛下威灵，荧惑顺轨，祝融避舍，当此连月之亢旱，曾无数家之燎延，此臣之可藉以逃责者三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309862_comment'></div>乃若深怀保抱之情，不敢少负刍牧之责，弛关市讥征以通商贾之路，蠲残零苗税以惠田里之氓，沿门借本以苏经纪之细民，创库损息以便典质之下户，散之药饵以疗其疾病，给之棺槥以周其死亡，强者免攘夺于街衢，弱者少枕藉于沟壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309862_comment'></div>至于安富，所以恤贫，时宽敷粜之期，祈请补籴之数，零替者减放，困削者蠲除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309862_comment'></div>荷朝廷之响从，觉阛阓之驩动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309862_comment'></div>凡可极力所至，莫匪以心求之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309862_comment'></div>惟有百物之时直未平，良由四方之会陌浸落，此非朝廷速行措置，无缘郡县可以转移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309862_comment'></div>使内外之楮价相登，则郡邑之物价自定，此则庙堂之事，匪独微臣之责矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309862_comment'></div>惟是臣于夏五初对便殿之时，固已知神皋非臣可以立足之地，盖至今日，渐验臣言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309862_comment'></div>伏望圣慈哀怜，俾令速归田里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309862_comment'></div>啜菽饮水，永戴赐于尧天；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309862_comment'></div>全身保家，免贻忧于括母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309862_comment'></div>仰祈睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1309862_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1240&endYear=1240')">1240年</a>　授宝谟阁学士知绍兴府浙东安抚使，未赴。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1240&endYear=1240')">1240年12月</a>　十二月，改福建安抚使，知遂宁府，辞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1241&endYear=1241')">1241年</a>　请守本官致仕。作品：《奏乞守本官致仕》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1309863' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309863' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309863?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞守本官致仕</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳祐元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309863")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309863_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309863'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309863'>臣近尝再具公牍，辞免新除恩命，仍乞挂神武之冠，以补过愆，以消灾咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309863_comment'></div>方屏息以俟俞允之旨，忽传西掖见上缴章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309863_comment'></div>臣窃伏惟念，政使朝廷轸念簪履之旧，欲全护于施行之间，此尤臣之所大惧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309863_comment'></div>臣至愚极陋，载念先臣某在乾淳间，亲接诸儒之脉，所师者文公朱熹，所友者彭龟年、楼钥、黄度、杨方、杨简、袁燮、柴中行，皆一时大老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309863_comment'></div>尝提耳而命臣曰：「士之为士，当明君子小人之朋，若得罪于君子，则终身不可立于天地间矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309863_comment'></div>臣泣而识之不敢忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309863_comment'></div>今夫近日之攻臣者，皆君子之巨擘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309863_comment'></div>夫既得罪于君子之巨擘，则必其积尤稔忒，有不可进于君子者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309863_comment'></div>岂惟终身无以自立于天壤之间，他日何以见先臣于地下乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309863_comment'></div>再三思之，惟有纳禄公朝，归伏先臣之坟墓，庶几藉蚤退之一节，少洗平生之玷，以不终得罪于君子，而他日尚有颜面可见先臣于地下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309863_comment'></div>兼臣身病日增，无复生全之望，亲年愈迈，当为终老之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309863_comment'></div>虽贪慕于明时，实怵迫于私计，是用不避三渎之诛，哀吁君父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309863_comment'></div>共望圣慈察其恋主之心虽切，而守身之义尤急，报国之志虽坚，而辱亲之忧尤大，特攽睿旨，容臣守本官职致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309863_comment'></div>臣仰瞻阙庭，无任恳切请祷之至，仰乞睿照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309863_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1309863'>〔贴黄〕臣窃惟近年以来，国家可谓多事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309863_comment'></div>然而元气尚充，外邪不得而干犯者，特在于朝廷能重台谏给舍之职，而为台谏给舍者，能各自尽其职而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309863_comment'></div>盖台谏给舍之职举则纪纲立，纪纲立则元气充，元气充则外邪不能入，此端平更化而后，陛下躬揽大权之明效大验也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309863_comment'></div>臣一介孤拙，昨台谏劾之，而朝廷曲为之全护，是以臣而屈朝廷之纪纲一矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309863_comment'></div>今中舍缴之，而朝廷又曲为之全护，则是以臣而屈朝廷之纪纲再矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309863_comment'></div>以区区蝼蚁之身，而至于重屈朝廷之纪纲，窃恐通国之人，凡知台谏给舍之权当尊，凡知朝廷之纪纲当立，皆以臣为口实矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309863_comment'></div>以区区蝼蚁之身，而通国之人以为口实，则是朝廷所以全护之者，恐适所以益其疾而重其咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309863_comment'></div>臣实陨穫忧惧，不知其死所也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309863_comment'></div>兼臣犹忆去岁八月二十有一日，臣轮当进读之馀，入劄子丐罢，陛下宣谕，以为徐荣叟、彭方适有疏论卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309863_comment'></div>臣遂奏云：「臣罪过山积，招致人言，上累陛下知人之明，乞即行斥逐」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309863_comment'></div>陛下复宣谕云：「卿岂可便去，已谕荣叟、方，令卿免兼临安府，二臣已无他说，卿可安心」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309863_comment'></div>臣又奏云：「此虽出于陛下保全之恩，然臣于进退之谊，只当便去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309863_comment'></div>臣只今出关，谨下殿辞谢」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309863_comment'></div>臣继即出钱塘门，以待威命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309863_comment'></div>本拟是日迤逦前迈，却缘临安职事，又非他官之比，未免小驻，书押财赋文字，牒往以次官交管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309863_comment'></div>次日忽蒙陛下特遣天使，宣押臣赴部供职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309863_comment'></div>臣以君上之命不敢固拒，于是暂入国门，盘旋匠监，以示眷恋阙庭之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309863_comment'></div>旋上奏疏，乞行台谏之言，以正朝廷之体统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309863_comment'></div>而臣继出北郭矣，复蒙陛下升以舜阁之隆名，宠以稽山之会府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309863_comment'></div>臣是时即欲挂冠，以谢清议，又恐涉孟轲悻悻之戒，故迟迟半载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1309863_comment'></div>适叨三山易地之命，方敢述引咎悔过之情，伸纳禄谢事之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1309863_comment'></div>盖自始至今，未尝敢以私情干求陛下之官职，破坏朝廷之纪纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1309863_comment'></div>此不惟立身行己之当然，而臣备员法从，其于国体，谊当相与保惜扶持也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1309863_comment'></div>今陛下之曲加圣造，一再全护者，不过以臣昨者备员尹正，实以勉奉圣意，非出臣之本心，则陛下实有「此除出朕亲擢，卿不须过虑」之训，故陛下有不忍施行者耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1309863_comment'></div>然自古圣帝明王之运动天下，驾驭人才，惟其至公而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1309863_comment'></div>物论以为可用而用之，物论以为可用而用之，此其所以为至公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1309863_comment'></div>陛下虽加之委曲全护，然臣恐重拂国人之论，而使臣益深据蒺履冰之惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1309863_comment'></div>臣是以焚香东望，复此奏陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1309863_comment'></div>欲望圣慈以断恩义，特赐夬决，容臣挂神武之冠，以自循省，庶几少救东隅之失，尚及为圣世之全人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1309863_comment'></div>是乃陛下所以保全之大者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1309863_comment'></div>孔子曰畏天命，畏大人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1309863_comment'></div>盖大人者，指大人君子而言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1309863_comment'></div>大人君子之好恶，实与天命相关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1309863_comment'></div>臣所以畏大人者，即所以畏天命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1309863_comment'></div>畏天命者，即所以畏陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1309863_comment'></div>臣请词竭尽，惟陛下监察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1309863_comment'></div>并乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1309863_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='77f329b4d16d449b9242cda3e94aca4f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("77f329b4d16d449b9242cda3e94aca4f");'><span id='77f329b4d16d449b9242cda3e94aca4f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1247')">1246-1247年</a>，52-53岁</div><div id='77f329b4d16d449b9242cda3e94aca4f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年11月</a>　转中大夫，试兵部尚书，兼侍读；转翰林学士，知制诰，兼侍读。作品：《奏论天地之复与人之复》<div id='poem_1309867' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309867' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309867?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏论天地之复与人之复</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳祐六年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309867")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309867_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309867'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309867'>臣忧患馀生，久蛰山林，荣望已绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309867_comment'></div>乃者陛下孟冬之吉，晨谒原庙，夕洒宸奎，在列诸贤，以次登进，而臣亦获与黄纸除书之目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309867_comment'></div>上恩深厚，勉造阙廷，适以仲冬，对扬便殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309867_comment'></div>维是月也，于辰为子，于卦为《复》，盖圣人所以著三才参合之妙而开万化新美之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309867_comment'></div>臣方学《易》，用敢推详其旨，以为入告之义，陛下试垂听焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309867_comment'></div>臣闻天之所赋者性也，性之所具者善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309867_comment'></div>夫茍率性而行，正亦何暇于复？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309867_comment'></div>惟其有形体而气禀梏之，有气禀而嗜欲乘之，有嗜欲而境物诱之，不能命五官而命于五官，不能宰七情而宰于七情，于是始有恶焉，与善而对立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309867_comment'></div>恶寖滋而寖长，则善寖蚀而寖微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309867_comment'></div>然恶虽滋而本无，善虽蚀而本有，一息之觉，天理毕呈，寸隙之光，人伪俱丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309867_comment'></div>譬之重阴固冱，而一阳萌檗，黄钟动葭灰飞而气应，井泉温荔挺出而物应，生生递续，化化不穷，故曰「复其见天地之心乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309867_comment'></div>天地之心，人之心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309867_comment'></div>天地之心，以动而复者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309867_comment'></div>若动而遽止，非复也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309867_comment'></div>周文之繇曰：「复亨，出入无疾，朋来无咎」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309867_comment'></div>此言天地之复，必至于二阳三阳之朋来而为《泰》，四阳五阳六阳之朋来而为《乾》，然后为复之全功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309867_comment'></div>人之心以知而复者也，若知而屡迁，非复也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309867_comment'></div>孔子之赞曰：「颜氏之子，其殆庶几乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309867_comment'></div>有不善未尝不知，知之未尝复行」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309867_comment'></div>此言人之复，必如颜氏子之过而必改，改而不贰，然后为复之全德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309867_comment'></div>以复之全德，而配复之全功，其斯为圣学之功用欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309867_comment'></div>自昔时君世主，固有昏冥颠悖，迷而不复，终其身乱亡相寻者，不足言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309867_comment'></div>亦有乍明乍晦，复而不悔，复而不终，以一人之身而自为始乱者，不必言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309867_comment'></div>其善于复者，臣于商、周得二君焉，成汤、宣王是已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309867_comment'></div>成汤自制心检身之复，以达于显忠从谏，官德赏功，而极其效为东征西夷怨，南征北狄怨，则以大事小之耻复矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309867_comment'></div>宣王自侧身脩行之复，以推于受箴纳诲，任贤使能，而极其效为《六月》之北伐，《采芑》之南征，则以夷狄侵中国之耻复矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309867_comment'></div>惟其复于义理而不渝，所以复于事业而不爽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309867_comment'></div>《诗》《书》所载，粲然光明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309867_comment'></div>恭惟陛下缉熙就将，日与羲文周孔神游于千载之上，特不知陛下亦尝体认于复之义否乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309867_comment'></div>夫初之不远复，观省之功也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309867_comment'></div>五之敦复，持循之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309867_comment'></div>观省之功，知及之者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309867_comment'></div>持循之力，仁守之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309867_comment'></div>且夫甲午改纪，陛下之一复也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1309867_comment'></div>然制于身心而达于天下国家，其本末犹是也，是陛下之复未固也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1309867_comment'></div>甲辰改纪，陛下之再复也，至是陛下春秋盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1309867_comment'></div>孔子四十而不惑，孟轲四十不动心，曾参五十而心化，蘧伯玉五十而知四十九年之非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1309867_comment'></div>盖四十五十之间，圣贤心为成德之候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1309867_comment'></div>然则陛下今日之复，其可以不固乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1309867_comment'></div>凝然其正，湛然其明，为陛下心之复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1309867_comment'></div>得毋有欲以便僻侧媚蛊吾之复者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1309867_comment'></div>国必有副，爱惟其亲，为陛下家之复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1309867_comment'></div>得毋有欲以迁延犹豫滞吾之复者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1309867_comment'></div>于是而之于国之于天下，君子复于进矣，凡以阴谗密愬而贰其复者，当察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1309867_comment'></div>小人复于退矣，凡以通神使鬼而摇其复者，当察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1309867_comment'></div>纪纲复于振饬矣，凡以偏私系累而蠹其复者，当察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1309867_comment'></div>政事复于宽大矣，凡以烦苛细碎而残其复者，当察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1309867_comment'></div>以至民之未复于富庶，如之何抚摩培植，以要其复欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1309867_comment'></div>兵之未复于盛彊，如之何整齐教训，以求其复欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1309867_comment'></div>财用之未复于殷阜，如之何裁制均节，以臻其复欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1309867_comment'></div>境土之未复于规恢，如之何经营布置，以底其复欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1309867_comment'></div>由一念之复而求證于庶事之复，因庶事之复而求端于一念之复，内与外互观，行与知并进，如是而陛下不为尧舜之君，天下不被尧舜之泽，臣未之前闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1309867_comment'></div>不然，复于暂而未必能复于久，复于名而未必尽复于实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1309867_comment'></div>君以已复为足，而不以行健先其臣，臣亦以已复为足，而不以健顺承其君，刚来而有往之机，道升而有降之渐，危心易放，正气难持，既无以保复而汇进于六阳，安知不反复而骤决于一阴乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1309867_comment'></div>不可留者光阴，不可料者世变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1309867_comment'></div>然而天下之事，岂堪频复哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1309867_comment'></div>臣不胜惓惓孤忠，取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_56_1309867_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年</a>　奏论君子小人之进退。作品：《奏论君子小人进退》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1309864' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309864' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309864?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏论君子小人进退</a><span class='authorDate'>（1246年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309864")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309864_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309864'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309864'>臣前既推明复之义，以条列复之事矣，窃以为事之最切于今日者，君子小人之进退是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309864_comment'></div>盖君子之当进与小人之当退，自昔人主，鲜有不知之，亦鲜有真知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309864_comment'></div>知不真则行不力，故君子常屈，小人常伸，故治日常少，乱日常多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309864_comment'></div>臣请得以究极其说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309864_comment'></div>且有虞之盛际，皋、夔、稷、契之所为，非共工、驩兜也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309864_comment'></div>有周之盛际，周、召、毛、毕之所为，非飞廉、恶来也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309864_comment'></div>终始一桓公，管仲辅之则治，易牙辅之则乱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309864_comment'></div>终始一明皇也，姚崇、宋璟功垂万世，而算计见效。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1309864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1309864'><span
