class='label'>按：</span>此行原缺十一字，下又缺七行，每行十八字。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1309864_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1247')">1247年</a>　春，知贡举。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1247')">1247年4月</a>　四月，自翰林学士除端明殿学士同签书枢密院事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1247')">1247年5月</a>　五月，兼权参知政事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1247')">1247年7月</a>　七月，罢参知政事，依旧端明殿学士知福州，福建安抚使。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='05daff99531a4d269c58820e1d349dd2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("05daff99531a4d269c58820e1d349dd2");'><span id='05daff99531a4d269c58820e1d349dd2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1250&endYear=1252')">1250-1252年</a>，56-58岁</div><div id='05daff99531a4d269c58820e1d349dd2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1250&endYear=1250')">1250年1月</a>　元宵节后，入政府供职。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1250&endYear=1250')">1250年</a>　奏论处时之难，治功不可以易视，并论大学治国平天下之道。作品：《内引第一札论今日处时之难治功不可以易视及论大学治国平天下之道》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1309865' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309865' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309865?labeling=true' target='_blank'>内引第一劄论今日处时之难治功不可以易视及论大学治国平天下之道</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳祐九年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309865")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309865_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309865'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309865'>）<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>不惟德礼教化日就颓阙，凡天下之事物，莫不壅底捍格，无一就吾之条理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309865_comment'></div>臣意陛下必有不快于心者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309865_comment'></div>推原其故，夫亦玩于时，而积至于时之难邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309865_comment'></div>惟其难也，则尤不可以易视之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309865_comment'></div>惟其不敢易也，而后难者可图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309865_comment'></div>国朝自开基至于庆历，积德百年矣，仁宗皇帝察天下之势渐趋于弱，欲一起而新美之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309865_comment'></div>时则有臣仲淹，慨然欲举明主于三代之隆，然论建虽广，异议乘之，终于不获展尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309865_comment'></div>神宗皇帝逮事仁祖，习闻祖道，而又负智勇不世出之资，粤从践祚，亦欲挈天下之弱势一起而新美之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309865_comment'></div>时则有臣安石，亦慨然欲举明主于三代之隆，然学术一差，几误天下，至今以为口实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309865_comment'></div>仲淹坏于人，而安石自坏之，此尚论国朝之治体者所痛惜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309865_comment'></div>夫以二祖之圣明，且当天下无虞之际，犹不足以遂其大可为之志，况陛下处时之难乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309865_comment'></div>故臣以为不可易视之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309865_comment'></div>一国犹一身也，国家之不能无弊，犹人之不能无疾病然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309865_comment'></div>今日之病，不但仓公、扁鹊望而惊，庸医亦望而惊矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309865_comment'></div>乌啄狼毒，病未必可伐，而先以戕生，臣知其决不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309865_comment'></div>借参苓芝术可以养生之说，以盖其茍安姑息之实，而听疾病之自为进退，臣知其亦不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309865_comment'></div>惟有酌温凉之剂，适宣补之宜，图其大而略其小，急其事而缓其功，精神与荣卫并充，腹心与肢体不悖，则疾其庶几渐瘳乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309865_comment'></div>此臣所以谓不可易视之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309865_comment'></div>臣愿陛下笃任元老，以为医师，博采众益，以为医工，使臣辈得以效溲勃之助，以不辱陛下知人之明，臣之幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309865_comment'></div>臣无任感恩激烈，惟陛下裁赦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309865_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309865_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1309865'>〔贴黄〕臣窃见陛下锐精经术，盖尝表章朱熹之四书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309865_comment'></div>四书，《大学》其首也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309865_comment'></div>近时真德秀复著《衍义》一编，久登乙览，《大学》之道明若观火矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309865_comment'></div>臣窃以为治国平天下，乃《大学》之极功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309865_comment'></div>一章之中，反复数百言，大抵不过贤才货财二事而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309865_comment'></div>盖贤才见用则天下平，贤才不见用则天下不平；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309865_comment'></div>货财不偏聚则天下平，货财偏聚则天下不平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309865_comment'></div>古今治乱安危之源不出此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309865_comment'></div>等而上之，为脩身齐家，为正心诚意，为格物致知，本末先后，具有差级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309865_comment'></div>盖由正心诚意而至治国平天下，属圣之事，终条理者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309865_comment'></div>由格物而致知，属智之事，始条理者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309865_comment'></div>何谓格？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309865_comment'></div>推而极之之义，如《书》所谓格于上下是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1309865_comment'></div>何谓致？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1309865_comment'></div>引而来之之义，如《语》所谓学以致其道是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1309865_comment'></div>物物皆当格，而天地人物为物之大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1309865_comment'></div>天地人物之理无时而终穷，而天地人物之迹有时而变化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1309865_comment'></div>穷其理以玩其迹，是为格物之大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1309865_comment'></div>格来格去，忽有觉焉，是为大知，而非小知，是为自致之知，而非强致之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1309865_comment'></div>致则至矣，至则举天下之外境万种万类，皆不能动之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1309865_comment'></div>举天下之万种万类不能动之，则意自诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1309865_comment'></div>意诚而心正，心正而身脩，身脩而家齐，家齐而国治天下平，皆安行而顺导之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1309865_comment'></div>臣顷年获侍清光，共闻圣训，谓向来尝日用两时静坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1309865_comment'></div>夫静坐者，格物致治之阶梯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1309865_comment'></div>故臣愿陛下益守此静，以造于纯粹之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1309865_comment'></div>纯粹生高明，高明生广大，道且在我矣，而况事为之末哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1309865_comment'></div>尚何忧时之难为，治之难济哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1309865_comment'></div>臣不任愿陛下为尧舜之君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1309865_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1309865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1309865'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_1309865_0'>⑴ （原缺七行又第八行首缺六字</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1309865_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1250&endYear=1250')">1250年</a>　言国家变故略与晋同，西北之夷狄固当防，而东南之乱尤不可忽。作品：《第二札论国家变故略与晋同西北之夷狄固当防而东南之盗贼尤不可忽》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1309866' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309866' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309866?labeling=true' target='_blank'>第二劄论国家变故略与晋同西北之夷狄固当防而东南之盗贼尤不可忽</a><span class='authorDate'>（1250年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309866")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309866_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309866'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309866'>臣闻古语有云，「大福不再，大忧不再」，此天道也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309866_comment'></div>又云「福生于畏，忧生于忽」，此人道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309866_comment'></div>晋司马氏宅都于洛，刘、石煽难，怀、悯劫迁，元帝遂中兴于江左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309866_comment'></div>其后苻坚乘方张之势，拥百万之众，直欲平吞晋室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309866_comment'></div>小捷淮淝，遂毙苻氏，此大忧不再之明證也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309866_comment'></div>百馀年晋之所防率在西北，而其亡也，乃由大盗孙恩、卢循之徒出没于海，而刘裕得以乘之，此忧生于所忽之明證也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309866_comment'></div>我国家仁义德泽，纪纲法度，比隆三代，固非晋氏之比，然中罹阳九之厄，思陵南渡，略与晋同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309866_comment'></div>逆亮叩江之事势，亦岌岌矣，不战而自陨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309866_comment'></div>鞑为不道，践我荆蜀，扰我两淮，瞰我江面，十五年于兹，而吾之根本终不为之动摇，今且闻其衰微有兆矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309866_comment'></div>故臣以为晋人之不再者，在今日未可喜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309866_comment'></div>而晋人之所忽者，在今日当深虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309866_comment'></div>虽然，盗贼本民也，又率于民而相挺于盗，固可诛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309866_comment'></div>然自浙之东西以达于广，海面五六千里，宁能尽空其巢穴而诛之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309866_comment'></div>则亦有消弭之道而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309866_comment'></div>消弭之道，置其衣食之源而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309866_comment'></div>况钱塘枕海而国，形势迫近，又非晋在秣陵之比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309866_comment'></div>故臣敢以告陛下而重有司之责焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309866_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1309866_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1250&endYear=1250')">1250年11月</a>　十一月，请解机政，不允。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1251&endYear=1251')">1251年3月</a>　三月，自太中大夫同知枢密院事除参知政事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1251&endYear=1251')">1251年4月</a>　四月，与理宗论边防形势。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1251&endYear=1251')">1251年</a>　为魏了翁文集作后序。作品：《魏鹤山文集后序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1309901' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309901' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309901?labeling=true' target='_blank'>魏鹤山文集后序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1251年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309901")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309901_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309901'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309901'>端平二年冬，潜以右文殿修撰知太平州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309901_comment'></div>时文靖魏公繇枢筦督视江淮京湖军马，其始辟幕府领袖之士，每极天下选，然率以时好向背违不就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309901_comment'></div>潜于公非交游知旧，亦骤辱拔引为上客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309901_comment'></div>或谓潜曰：盍审诸！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309901_comment'></div>潜曰：公善类之宗也，可无从乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309901_comment'></div>乃疋马追公于湓浦之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309901_comment'></div>虽玉帐赞筹，专务戎事，而暇日尊俎笑谈，获见公高文大册及闻公崇论宏议，日充然有所得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309901_comment'></div>尝曰学必本六经之谓正学，道必本尧舜禹汤文武周公孔孟之谓正道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309901_comment'></div>彼邪说诐行是乃荆榛，辟而通之则理到文醇矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309901_comment'></div>至于天文地理，礼乐律历，官制兵法，典章文物，莫不极纚纚，如辨白黑而数一二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309901_comment'></div>潜益信公根柢学问，枝叶文章，落陈启新，翼华抵实，天出神入，不可羁控，此岂偶然之故哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309901_comment'></div>后二年公殁，潜哭之流涕，曰天丧斯文矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309901_comment'></div>又十有五年，公之子近思、克愚相与蒐遗罔轶，有正集、外集、奏议一百卷，将锓梓行于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309901_comment'></div>既属叔氏序其首，又俾潜曰：子为申言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309901_comment'></div>潜窃谓渡江以来，文脉与国脉同其寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309901_comment'></div>盖高宗于司马文正公《资治通鉴》，谓有益治道，可为谏书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309901_comment'></div>自孝宗为《苏文忠公文集》御制一赞，谓忠言谠论，不顾一身利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309901_comment'></div>洋洋圣谟，风动四方，于是人文大兴，上足以接庆历、元祐之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309901_comment'></div>至乾、淳间，大儒辈出，朱文公倡于建，张宣公倡于潭，吕成公倡于婺，皆著书立言，自为一家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309901_comment'></div>凡仁义之要，道德之奥，性理之精微，所以明天理而正人心，立人极而扶世教，使天下晓然知人之所以异于禽兽，吾道之所以异于佛老，圣经贤传之务息邪说，有君臣有父子而不蚀其纲常之正者，功用弘矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309901_comment'></div>永嘉诸老如陈心斋、叶水心之徒，则又创为制度器数之学，名曰实用，以博洽相夸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309901_comment'></div>虽未足以颉颃二三大儒，然亦有足稽者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309901_comment'></div>寥寥然四五十载，我公嗣之，识照古今而不自以为高，忠贯日月而不自以为异，德望在生民，名望在四夷，文章之望在天下，后世盖所谓兼精粗、一本末、集乾淳之大成者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309901_comment'></div>惜其位不称德，命不待时，不及相明天子以兴礼乐，致太平，而斯文之泽所见仅止于此，悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309901_comment'></div>公讳了翁，字华父，邛之鹤山人，天下士师尊之曰「鹤山先生」云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1309901_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1251&endYear=1251')">1251年10月</a>　十月，五疏乞罢机政，不允。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1251&endYear=1251')">1251年11月</a>　十一月，奏留程公许。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1251&endYear=1251')">1251年11月</a>　十一月甲寅，自参知政事授宣奉大夫右丞相兼枢密使，依前金陵郡开国公加封邑。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1252&endYear=1252')">1252年</a>　春，秤提会子，专任其责。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1252&endYear=1252')">1252年8月</a>　八月，乞解机政，疏四上不报。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1252&endYear=1252')">1252年10月</a>　十月，提举国史实录院及日历所。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1252&endYear=1252')">1252年11月</a>　十一月庚寅，罢右丞相。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1252&endYear=1252')">1252年12月</a>　十二月乙卯，以观文殿大学士提举江州太平兴国宫。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='c23e137bb1354ae4bdd455e752466bfd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c23e137bb1354ae4bdd455e752466bfd");'><span id='c23e137bb1354ae4bdd455e752466bfd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1260')">1259-1260年</a>，65-66岁</div><div id='c23e137bb1354ae4bdd455e752466bfd' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年9月19日</a>　九月十九日，召为醴泉观使兼侍读。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年10月1日</a>　十月一日入对，论敌恃力而中国恃理。作品：《冬十月一日内引奏札论夷狄恃力中国恃理四事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1309883' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309883' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309883?labeling=true' target='_blank'>冬十月一日内引奏劄论夷狄恃力中国恃理四事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年10月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309883")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309883_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309883'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309883'>臣顷待罪鄞阃，迫于衰疾，屡上乞骸之请，仰荷从欲，获返山林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309883_comment'></div>突未及黔，忽叨命召，俾奉内祠而侍经幄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309883_comment'></div>一攽天笔，再遣使辂，四勤宣谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309883_comment'></div>捧读圣训，有曰「待卿之来，以刻为岁」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309883_comment'></div>臣感激流涕，不能自持，何敢以出处之常节，废君臣之大义？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309883_comment'></div>戴星疾驰，趋赴阙下，兹叨内见，瞻望清光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309883_comment'></div>积八年葵向之忱，辄吐涓埃，上裨海岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309883_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下临政愿治，三纪于兹，适际时艰，以四十馀年兵不解甲之天下，而当数千年以来所无之夷狄，忱戛乎其难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309883_comment'></div>然中国夷狄，自古常对立于天下，夷狄之所恃者力，中国之所恃者理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309883_comment'></div>在彼者有彼之可恃，而或窃我之所恃，在我者无彼之可恃，而又失我之所恃，则胜负之形已判矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309883_comment'></div>故中国之所谓理者，在畏天命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309883_comment'></div>《书》曰「天难谌，命靡常，常厥德，保厥位」，又曰「惟吉凶不僭在人，惟天降灾祥在德」，又曰「皇天无亲，惟德是辅」，茍对越之际多违，谴告之至不察，畏于口而意不实，敬以文而事则非，有好畤太乙之祷祈，无桑林云汉之克责，是我失其所恃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309883_comment'></div>故中国之所谓理者，在结民心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309883_comment'></div>《书》曰「民为邦本，本固邦宁，予临兆民，凛凛乎若朽索之驭六马」，又曰「民罔常怀，怀于有仁」，又曰「民情大可见，小人难保」，茍内之司存，外之郡县，借体国之名而穷聚敛，假奉公之说而极诛求，用有司之刑狱桎梏为一己之苞苴囊橐，是我失其所恃矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309883_comment'></div>故中国之所谓理者，在进贤才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309883_comment'></div>《书》曰「天命有德，五服五章哉」，又曰「佑贤辅德，显忠遂良」，克知三有宅心，灼见三有俊心，以敬事上帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309883_comment'></div>苟服谗蒐慝，诬善丑正，无保惜爱护之意，有摧折困沮之风，仁贤空虚，气象萧索，是我失其所恃矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309883_comment'></div>故中国之所谓理者，在通下情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309883_comment'></div>《书》曰「稽于众，舍己从人」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309883_comment'></div>又曰「每岁孟春，遒人以木铎徇于路，官师相规，工执艺事以谏」，又曰「责人斯无难，惟受责俾如流，是惟艰哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309883_comment'></div>茍上下蔽蒙，耳目涂塞，持禄固位之习锢，犯颜逆耳之节微，全身保家之计精，悯时忧国之念薄，是我失其所恃矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309883_comment'></div>我既失其所恃，宁不虞彼窃而用之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309883_comment'></div>譬之身焉，天命所以寿考我也，民心所以元气我也，贤才所以精神我也，下情所以宣导我也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309883_comment'></div>顾自有而自弃之，可乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309883_comment'></div>虽然，若此者皆群臣之罪，非陛下之本心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309883_comment'></div>陛下本心如青天白日，云阴暂翳，未尝不随即开明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309883_comment'></div>臣区区之愚，欲望皇帝陛下自咎自艾于天地祖宗之前，亟下痛切之诏，务在明白洞达，不必回护掩覆，昭布旧失，力图今是，以回吾之所可恃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309883_comment'></div>所谓悔过不嫌于深，责己不嫌于重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309883_comment'></div>如使念虑之真实，自然幽明之感通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309883_comment'></div>人情既舒，天意必悦，天意既悦，狄难必宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309883_comment'></div>其他备御之方，自可次第而举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309883_comment'></div>惟陛下留神，宗社幸甚，生灵幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1309883_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年</a>　蒙古兵分路深入而时相匿报，因涕泣入奏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年10月2日</a>　十月二日，特进左丞相兼枢密使，监修国史，进封相国公。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年10月6日</a>　十月六日，改庆国公。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年11月</a>　十一月，乞令在朝之臣各陈所见以决处置之宜。作品：《冬十一月日以鞑寇深入具奏乞令在朝文武官各陈所见以决处置之宜》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1309884' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309884' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309884?labeling=true' target='_blank'>冬十一月日以鞑寇深入具奏乞令在朝文武官各陈所见以决处置之宜</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309884")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309884_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309884'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309884'>臣辄沥危衷，仰干圣听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309884_comment'></div>臣迟暮之迹，比从鄞阃，属疏乞骸，甫获归田，忽叨命召，俾厕经幄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309884_comment'></div>一攽天笔，四承宣谕，两遣使华，圣训真切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309884_comment'></div>臣跪诵一言则血泪一滴，非不知鄂寇已迫于江沱，广寇已踰于宾柳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309884_comment'></div>重惟君臣之大义，不敢徇出处之常节，疾驱赴阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309884_comment'></div>止谓备数劝读之末，时效一得之愚，上裨圣算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309884_comment'></div>不料仅入国门，即被扬庭之命，擢置左辖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309884_comment'></div>主忧臣辱，不敢牢辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309884_comment'></div>虽黾勉夙夜，应酬科琐，然不过粗安京师畿甸之人心，岂能遽却侵犯内地之强敌！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309884_comment'></div>孟子所谓三年之艾尚不能炙七年之病，况沉痼之疾，弄成坏證，而欲以顷刻之艾炙之，使卢、扁复生，且将望之而走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309884_comment'></div>今鄂渚有重臣以宣威，有骁将以御侮，援师云集，胜势日张，似可少宽西顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309884_comment'></div>若湖湘一路，直透腹心，无高山大泽以为之限，无精兵良将以为之防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309884_comment'></div>如广南制司前月二十有四日报称，贼叩静江城门，交射而却，旋退屯四十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309884_comment'></div>自是越二十馀日，无一字到朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309884_comment'></div>至十月二十日，则湖南帅宪两司之报猝至，谓贼已于初十日突至清湘矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309884_comment'></div>今又八九日，帅宪两司并无续报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309884_comment'></div>万一又有如广南之一节无报，而清湘之警报猝至，不知上下将何以为策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309884_comment'></div>或进或退，或行或守，皆非一旦之所能办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309884_comment'></div>窃恐误君父，误社稷，误生灵，贻笑万世，是时惟有一死，何益于国！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309884_comment'></div>汉人有云：「先事而言，常患不信，事至而应，又患无及」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309884_comment'></div>今不可谓之先事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309884_comment'></div>臣非不能为宽譬之言，曰此非鞑也、蛮也，又曰此蛮与溃兵合也，非真鞑也，又曰虽鞑也，然又不能多也，又曰鞑所志者金帛子女，既有所掳掠，不久能自遁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309884_comment'></div>此言幸而中，则可窃镇静之名，善料敌之誉，不幸而不中，祸变忽临，纵食为此言者之肉，果何补哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309884_comment'></div>臣愚欲望圣慈以臣此章宣示二三执政、给舍、台谏、殿帅，使各述其所见，并指陈鞑贼有无必至之患，目前当作如何布置，亲具手疏以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309884_comment'></div>却乞降付臣参酌，庶臣可资众益，以为处置之决，毋徒曰国家之事一相任之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309884_comment'></div>臣不任恳切，伏望睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1309884_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年12月14日</a>　十二月壬子改封许国公。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年12月</a>　十二月论国家安危理乱之源与君子小人之界限。作品：《奏论国家安危理乱之源与君子小人之界限》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1309886' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309886' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309886?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏论国家安危理乱之源与君子小人之界限</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309886")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309886_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309886'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309886'>臣辄沥危衷，上干圣听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309886_comment'></div>臣一介衰迟，顷自鄞阃引疾乞骸，仰荷从欲之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309886_comment'></div>还山甫浃日，而闻广寇踰宾柳而东，鄂寇越黄汉而南，陛下亟以经幄召臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309886_comment'></div>臣重惟君臣之大义，不敢以时艰为避就，扶病赴阙，亦不过谓密侍毡厦，时贡小忠而已，不谓陛下遽以前人之败局而付之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309886_comment'></div>臣既入国门，无路可逃，黾勉祗承，应酬科琐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309886_comment'></div>犹赖陛下惕然悔悟，引咎责躬，大洗冤沉，毕达幽枉，臣遂得以凭藉尸位数旬之久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309886_comment'></div>然其间关于国家安危理乱之源，与君子小人之界限，臣向未及痛哭流涕，为陛下言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309886_comment'></div>前日忽睹章鉴涂归高斯得之章，臣为之骇愕，不能自持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309886_comment'></div>照得臣于斯得素非腹心之交，金石之友，岁在丁未，臣在田野，但闻斯得为浙东刑狱使者，疏劾郑清之、史宅之辈亲党数人，邸报流传，四海之人皆为击节，臣于是始敬其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309886_comment'></div>逮岁在辛亥，臣猥蒙陛下擢置次辅，一时收召当世知名之士，而斯得预焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309886_comment'></div>奈其好为危言激论，上拂陛下之听，下忤首相之意，而阴窥密伺者因得以遂其一网之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309886_comment'></div>自壬子以至己未，八年之间，公道晦蚀，私意横流，仁贤空虚，名节丧败，忠嘉绝响，谀佞成风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309886_comment'></div>天怒而陛下不知，人怨而陛下不察，稔成夷狄之祸，实为宗社之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309886_comment'></div>幸陛下奋由圣断，甫为善类伸一线之脉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309886_comment'></div>而奸人又从而摧遏之，臣实痛焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309886_comment'></div>如斯得闽漕之事，臣固未详其虚实，特二吏之毙，正是有位者杀之以灭口，而反以为證乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309886_comment'></div>近日赃吏动至数千百万，甚者召寇启戎，使国步颠危，生灵鱼肉，陛下玉食为之不御，枕席为之不宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309886_comment'></div>鉴胡为尽付瘖哑，而独加怒于陛下已拔拭录用之斯得乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309886_comment'></div>窃见鉴尘容俗状，谄笑胁肩，徒以尝与大全同官，倾心附丽，躐跻要途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309886_comment'></div>斯得纵非全名之士，不犹愈于腹无点墨、面有甲颜、淟涊依违、尝粪舐痔之鉴乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309886_comment'></div>昔元祐间，孔文仲为谏议大夫，劾朱光庭除太常少卿不当，宰臣吕公著率同列辨甚力，乃寝其奏，光庭竟就职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309886_comment'></div>董敦逸、黄庆基为御史，劾苏轼兄弟，宰臣吕大防力争，乃罢敦逸、庆基言职，与州军差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309886_comment'></div>夫元祐最为国朝盛时，台谏论列不当，宰相犹得争是非，辨曲直，况给舍乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309886_comment'></div>臣自视望实轻浅，决不能效先朝元臣大老回天之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309886_comment'></div>然阴阳消长之机，世道反覆之候，于此觇焉，臣不得不为陛下告也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309886_comment'></div>臣曩叨柄任，萧泰来首弹李伯玉，是时臣不能明目张胆以感悟陛下，仅尝于榻前救解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309886_comment'></div>群小噂沓，国事日非，浸淫至于今日，臣亦岂容不分任其咎哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309886_comment'></div>鉴近日数诣臣，乞为弟铸除郎，又乞为除职因任，又为其姻家郎伋求归班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309886_comment'></div>臣实鄙贱其人，不复与之酬答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309886_comment'></div>孟子所谓与恶人处，如以朝衣朝冠坐于涂炭，臣之于鉴，何以异此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309886_comment'></div>臣若不早折其萌，又将贻天下善类之祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309886_comment'></div>累卵之危，国家宁堪重坏哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309886_comment'></div>欲望陛下稍垂日月之明，毋使小人之阴乍翕而骤张，暂息而遽燃，以成夷狄之阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309886_comment'></div>臣虽陷鼎镬之诛，亦所不辞，谨具手疏以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1309886_comment'></div>臣干犯宸严，无任激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1309886_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1309886_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1309886'>〔贴黄〕臣顷尸鄞阃，抗疏乞身，固尝告陛下，以臣骨相素奇屯而命运适冲并，若留之一方，必将兴灾招衅，非军民之福，陛下于是纵臣之归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1309886_comment'></div>今鄂寇未清，湘寇叵测，囚停则智长，事久则变生，社稷生灵之忧，凛凛乎未知攸济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1309886_comment'></div>臣既无耆庞福艾之相，又非扶颠持危之才，终恐误陛下大计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1309886_comment'></div>欲望陛下亟发睿断，放臣退伏田里，别选奇才厚福之人，正位台席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1309886_comment'></div>臣数旬之间，髭发尽白，百骸九窍，无非是病，惟陛下怜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1309886_comment'></div>并乞睿照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1309886_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_1309886'>〔又贴黄〕臣又有未尽之悃，敢空臆为陛下陈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1309886_comment'></div>臣最痛切者，群臣上下合党以欺陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1309886_comment'></div>惟陛下不知，而稔成国家之祸，则陛下独当之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1309886_comment'></div>且如高斯得之事，此其蒙蔽陛下之大者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1309886_comment'></div>斯得为湖南提刑，尝发部民陈衡老之奸恶，清之当国，遂将衡老黥籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1309886_comment'></div>而高铸者，为衡老行财营救，斯得遂发其事，高铸遂被黥配。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1309886_comment'></div>时高铸名高锜，后方改名铸，冒受官资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1309886_comment'></div>大全得志，高铸用事，恨憾斯得，欲置之大谴大呵之域，于是大全用章鉴之弟章铸为福建漕，以搜剔斯得之过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1309886_comment'></div>适斯得平日持论大苛，每于与𥲅逢人攻诋，又积与𥲅之怒，而沈炎实为与𥲅心腹爪牙，大全、高铸发踪指示，而炎甘为之搏噬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1309886_comment'></div>今奸党盘据，血脉贯通，故鉴又为此举，而炎亦姑泛论大全以愚陛下，使陛下真以为非大全之党也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1309886_comment'></div>欺皇天后土，欺一祖十二宗，欺陛下，以趣天下之危乱者，皆此等一宗小人为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1309886_comment'></div>陛下如不信臣言，乞索高铸元配案视阅之，庶几信而有證。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1309886_comment'></div>今以高铸一黥吏之故，而戕贼善类，略不顾惜，上天为何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1309886_comment'></div>臣言之至此，血泪迸流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1309886_comment'></div>伏乞睿照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1309886_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1309886'>〔又贴黄〕臣老矣，粗谙世故，岂不知事有缓急，时有难易？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1309886_comment'></div>惟愿包荒隐忍，以渐启沃，使君子小人各得其所，以养国家安靖和平之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1309886_comment'></div>不谓何物老丑，乃敢挑衅召闹，以格陛下明诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1309886_comment'></div>所谓世无终弃之才、永锢之士，其怀谄扶奸，罔上附下，情理尤为巨蠹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1309886_comment'></div>并乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_61_1309886_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1260&endYear=1260')">1260年3月1日</a>　三月一日，痛陈当前危急形势，推原乱本祸根，乞为更大之悔悟。作品：《春三月一日奏论鞑贼深入乞充前日之悔悟以祈天永命消弭狄难事（景定元年）》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1309885' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309885' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309885?labeling=true' target='_blank'>春三月一日奏论鞑贼深入乞充前日之悔悟以祈天永命消弭狄难事</a><span class='authorDate'>（景定元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309885")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309885_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309885'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309885'>臣一介迟暮，顷陛下以狄难孔殷，召臣于山林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309885_comment'></div>臣重惟主忧臣辱，不敢以时艰为避就，力疾赴阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309885_comment'></div>始不过谓密侍经帷，时贡小忠而已，不图圣恩复加柄任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309885_comment'></div>臣既入国门，无穴可逃，黾勉就列，倏五越月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309885_comment'></div>赖旬宣重臣提大兵以解鄂渚之围，分精兵以剿湖南之寇，四方上下，日冀肃清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309885_comment'></div>然贼智愈深，贼势渐阔，虫蠹木而荏苒，蚕食叶而浸淫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309885_comment'></div>大抵其狡焉之谋，最善于以退为进，以久为速，以聚为散，以客为主，以徘徊延款之形，藏飘忽震荡之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309885_comment'></div>又善于造讹设诈，使被掳而来归与背虏而投拜者妄相传播，以中吾之所喜，宽吾之所忧，而迄遂其所大欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309885_comment'></div>今已入吾堂奥，溃吾腹胁，正恐其未肯遽舍而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309885_comment'></div>纵去，吾内固已困矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309885_comment'></div>推原乱本祸根，良由十数年来，奸臣憸士创为虚议论、实事功之说，以迷国误朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309885_comment'></div>凡忠君爱上、规正阙失之言，尽诿之为虚议论；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309885_comment'></div>凡残民尅下、陷害忠良之举，反推之为实事功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309885_comment'></div>举一世之人，犹食稻衣锦而趋之者，则与乱同事之事也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309885_comment'></div>举一世之人，若赴汤蹈火而避之者，则与治同道之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309885_comment'></div>创哗讦之名，摽不靖之目，以空国中之善人，而其祸至一二年而愈酷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309885_comment'></div>于是驱民以附贼，驱士以从贼，驱天下之人以不仇贼，而反幸贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309885_comment'></div>夫人主欲有所为，而大臣不敢纠其非，大臣欲有所为，而百执事与士庶人不敢纠其非，附和逢迎，媕阿谄媚，虽至背理伤道，亦付之一默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309885_comment'></div>朝廷之上可为靖矣，可谓不哗不讦矣，讵料积而为夷狄之大不靖乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309885_comment'></div>官职富贵，则稔祸之臣撄拿以去，而大患难则以遗陛下，可胜痛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309885_comment'></div>臣虽勉竭于科琐，仅而左右之支撑，反覆深思，惟有祈天永命之一说，全在陛下而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309885_comment'></div>所谓祈天永命，全在陛下悔悟之透彻而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309885_comment'></div>天下只是一个理，理只是一个天，天只是一个心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309885_comment'></div>傥非陛下存于中者念念与天通，发于外者事事与天合，则皇天决未悔祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309885_comment'></div>皇天未悔祸，而欲敌之悔祸，犹却行而求前也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309885_comment'></div>自昔尧舜禹汤文武之君，稷契伊傅周召之臣，都俞吁咈，口口只是说天，夫岂推注于荒忽诞慢之域者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309885_comment'></div>忱以人主为天之子，父子之间，情愫易达，善恶易见，感应易孚，故曰「上帝临汝，毋二尔心」，故曰「文王陟降，在帝左右」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309885_comment'></div>此非可以言貌欺，非可以缁黄祷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309885_comment'></div>如使意不忱而心不实，徒有收拾君子之迹，而厌薄君子之根未除，徒有屏弃小人之迹，而回护小人之根未除，徒有远声色之迹，而蛊惑之根未除，徒有贱货利之迹，而丰殖之根未除，徒有开言路之迹，而浸润之根未除，徒有扶持公道之迹，而恩爱之根未除，徒有培植邦本之迹，而戕贼之根未除，徒有爱惜民力之迹，而营缮之根未除，诸根未除，则是陛下之念虑未纯乎天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309885_comment'></div>陛下之念虑未纯乎天，而求天之纯佑陛下，岂可得哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309885_comment'></div>故臣专望陛下充前日之悔悟，而更为今日之大悔悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309885_comment'></div>夫至灵至明者莫过于此心，陛下以神武睿哲之资，加以历事变之久，阅义理之熟，一自反观于至虚至明之心，则知宗庙社稷、人民亿兆、后妃宗戚，其休戚存亡，皆在陛下之一身，而陛下尤欲自寿其身，以久享至高极贵尊荣之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309885_comment'></div>念之至此，则必有惕然不能自已者，特恐陛下不念尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309885_comment'></div>臣年将七十，无丝发眷恋人世，捐躯致命，自所不辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1309885_comment'></div>但所深病者，坏局在他人之手，而臣万一代受其败，书之史册，必曰今相某，而不曰前相某，又必赞之曰某既无扶颠持危之才，且不能尽忠竭忱，正救其主，泯泯棼棼，黯无晶光，以至于弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1309885_comment'></div>臣负此沉冤，九陨且不瞑目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1309885_comment'></div>故数十日之间，髭发尽白，疾病转深，形骸仅存，神识已散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1309885_comment'></div>是用略伸愚悃，仰渎圣聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1309885_comment'></div>傥陛下幸听臣言，而皇天不为之佑助，夷狄不为之消弭，则是唐虞三代圣人之言不足凭，孔子六经之书不足信，天下决无是理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1309885_comment'></div>惟是臣才术短浅，无以济时康国，上负陛下注倚，且不能自尽其难，而猥效古人责难之义，罪大不可赦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1309885_comment'></div>并乞特发睿断，亟赐窜逐，虽投之斧钺，是乃臣得其正命之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1309885_comment'></div>但使天下后世谅臣心迹，则臣死犹生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1309885_comment'></div>执笔摅词，无任陨越感涕之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1309885_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_1309885'>〔贴黄〕臣窃惟鞑贼截江中流，为彼捷径，停留至于半载，创残被于三路，何翅孔明所谓危急存亡之秋！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1309885_comment'></div>而通国之人，方偃然嬉笑如平日，臣虞其为数所囿，而莫之省觉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1309885_comment'></div>若非陛下有回天之大德业，则虽臣等百数，何补于事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1309885_comment'></div>近忧后虑，百结寸肠，于是臣之前疏，五就橐而五就燬矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1309885_comment'></div>而终不容于不一言者，恐负陛下，负社稷，负生灵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1309885_comment'></div>恐万世之下，不知臣授任之时，上流之贼已踰黄汉而南，广右之贼已蹈宾柳而东，谓臣坏陛下之天下也，臣之情亦可哀已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1309885_comment'></div>惟陛下财幸。</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1309885_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1260&endYear=1260')">1260年3月14日</a>　三月十四日，奏论士大夫当纯意国事。作品：《十四日具奏论士大夫当纯意国事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1309887' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309887' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309887?labeling=true' target='_blank'>十四日具奏论士大夫当纯意国事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1260年3月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309887")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309887_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309887'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309887'>臣闻韩琦初除谏官，往谢王曾，曾语之云：「士大夫当纯意国事，向来如高若讷辈惟知徇利，如范希文亦未免好名」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309887_comment'></div>琦服行其言，故其平生大节独光明俊伟，为朝硕辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309887_comment'></div>臣谓纯意国事四字，岂惟台谏当然，凡在臣子，皆当如参前倚衡之，不容须臾离也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309887_comment'></div>近者徐庚金等抗疏言事，谓之非谠论不可也，惟臣独察其情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309887_comment'></div>庚金盖谢方叔之死党也，其初未尝交方叔，臣丁未典举，庚金实为选士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309887_comment'></div>已而臣叨尘右席，庚金犹未有一日考任，臣拔之为京府教官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309887_comment'></div>旋背臣而右附于方叔矣，于是连得峻迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309887_comment'></div>及其去国，乃始贻书于臣，殆如牛腰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309887_comment'></div>臣再叨柄任，甚厚望于臣，臣以包荒明望之义，复引而进之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309887_comment'></div>忽一日，其馆主人吴氏以不仁不义激乡民之变，将有严陵何氏之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309887_comment'></div>臣方喻帅臣叶隆礼亟行销弭，而庚金告臣，必欲以大盗诬治乡民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309887_comment'></div>时边遽正急，内地恶少多有啸聚夺攘之證，臣密行布置弹压，仅得无虞，庶几其不为外寇之资，未免斥却庚金，而庚金怨臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309887_comment'></div>方应发者，臣不知其为就何人属吏，以外改文字白臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309887_comment'></div>臣但见其尝为校勘，而不知其尝为宗谕，颇难之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309887_comment'></div>饶虎臣力加引进，臣乃处以博士，而应发终怨臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309887_comment'></div>程元岳，固丁大全所识拔为校勘者也，臣以国子录迁之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309887_comment'></div>元岳怒，以为左降，教今武学谕黄梦炎致曲于臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309887_comment'></div>亟叙之为博士，而元岳亦怨臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309887_comment'></div>昔者有蔡抗，系臣己酉省闱所放进士，为其改秩，其登朝多臣之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309887_comment'></div>岁在壬子，臣引之为国子司业，犹未尝历郎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309887_comment'></div>人方议其进擢之骤，属臣荐徐霖为说书，而抗恨不己及，于是归投方叔，求有以自效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309887_comment'></div>未几则假借小故，以身引去，且率诸生偕去以动摇臣，而臣果去矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309887_comment'></div>方叔乃召抗，一时迁为法从，以至参大政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309887_comment'></div>庚金等谓弄躅在前，可振袂而趋之，或能动摇臣，或虽不能动摇臣，而使天下传之，曰学官相率而去朝廷，亦可以为臣相业之玷，他日不妨可为蔡抗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309887_comment'></div>迹庚金所寄声馆中之士，有曰「若辈只会权郎，只会兼讲，略不能助我辈立赤帜」，则其贪爱官职、怨怼朝廷之真心可见矣，是岂纯意国事者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309887_comment'></div>虽然，不可以情之非而没其事之是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309887_comment'></div>宋臣为天下怨府，虽三尺童子皆欲剸刃其腹，虽秃千兔之毛，刊万山之竹，不足以形容其过恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309887_comment'></div>陛下聪明远迈尧舜，固不能不喜其供奉之勤，而未尝不知其奸凶之迹，诛远弃斥之意固已久矣，岂待诸臣之言而始焉夬之决哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309887_comment'></div>特圣心仁厚，不能为四夷之屏而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309887_comment'></div>然以臣愚见，内外皆祠也，孝宗尝置甘升于沾宁庙，尝置王仲谦于池，若今宋臣以外祠，或越，或嘉兴，或安吉，俾往居住，亦可以保全其富贵而全其终身，岂非君臣始末之大恩哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309887_comment'></div>何必留之辇毂之下，以滋舆人之议也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309887_comment'></div>沈炎自为小官，本无大过，特用非其据，不自植立，附阿时宰，举天下之善人莫不碎于其手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309887_comment'></div>且彼自言非大全之党，而奏疏中称颂大全，有曰「鼎辅方新，钧平持正，精神之所感召，意气之所鼓动，臣民仰首以观化，夷狄闻风而损威」，又曰「睿谟深远，明见万里，料敌制胜，动中事机」，又曰「朝廷清明，户廷无壅，朝奏夕报，捷如影响」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309887_comment'></div>夫招业之变，大变也，「精神之所感召，意气之所鼓动」者如是乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1309887_comment'></div>「明见万里，动中事机，户庭无壅，朝奏夕报」者如是乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1309887_comment'></div>其为党亦昭昭矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1309887_comment'></div>而曰非党者，欺陛下也，欺天也，欺心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1309887_comment'></div>一人之言，可以塞天下之口乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1309887_comment'></div>陛下固谓庶官攻台谏，有坏纲纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1309887_comment'></div>然臣窃观仁庙朝，苏舜钦为大理评事，监在京宅务，上疏有云：「张观为御史中丞，高若讷为司谏，二人者皆登高第，颇以文词进，而温和软懦，无刚鲠敢言之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1309887_comment'></div>斯皆执政引拔建置，欲其缄默，不敢举扬其私」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1309887_comment'></div>夫宅务小小监当耳，尚敢攻中丞、司谏，则祖宗故事尚可考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1309887_comment'></div>端平初，陈埙以编修官轮对，首攻殿中侍御史何琮、监察御史何处久，陛下旋以琮为权户部侍郎，处久为秘书监，而埙出知处州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1309887_comment'></div>陛下之英断，岂反不逮二十七年之前乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1309887_comment'></div>顷臣授任之初，蒙被训饬，谓台谏给舍，宰臣不当干预。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1309887_comment'></div>是时即欲具疏敷陈，见陛下忧边正苦，不敢以此伤陛下之意，今可因事而言矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1309887_comment'></div>夫给舍台谏，乃国家治乱安危之所由出，而宰相不许干预，不知陛下谋之谁耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1309887_comment'></div>陛下深居九重，与天下之士大夫未尝相接，何以察其贤否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1309887_comment'></div>非谋之近习则谋之恩幸之臣，又不然，则谋之台谏之长为陛下鹰犬者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1309887_comment'></div>陛下且谓近习恩幸之臣，能识天下之贤才乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1309887_comment'></div>言路之甘为陛下鹰犬者，肯荐天下之贤才乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1309887_comment'></div>其不肖之士为给舍台谏者，近习恩幸之臣与甘为鹰犬之臣，肯为陛下排之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1309887_comment'></div>昔高宗中兴，当绍兴之七年，狄难已消，天下已略定矣，高宗以经筵召赵鼎，旋俾再相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1309887_comment'></div>鼎告高宗曰：「进退人才，乃臣职分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1309887_comment'></div>今之清议所与如刘大中、胡寅、吕本中、常同、□季什之徒，陛下能用之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1309887_comment'></div>妒贤党恶如赵霈、胡世将、周秘、陈公辅，陛下能去之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1309887_comment'></div>陛下于此或难，则臣何敢措手也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1309887_comment'></div>于是有旨，给事中、兼侍讲、直学士院胡世将，夺夕琐为试兵部侍郎，御史中丞周秘，罢为徽猷阁直学士知秀州，如霈、公辅等，皆相继补外，而刘大中等以次收召无遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1309887_comment'></div>则是宰相可以去中丞、去给事中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1309887_comment'></div>而陛下以为不当干预，毋乃非高皇帝之家法乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1309887_comment'></div>陛下自谓台谏皆出亲擢，可以控制宰相，不知特可以控制君子之宰相尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1309887_comment'></div>其小人之宰相，则内交近习，外交恩幸之臣，转以私人祝其荐引，以为台谏，不分内外上下，缔为死党，只欺得陛下一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1309887_comment'></div>故陛下之亲擢台谏，实不能控制小人之宰相也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1309887_comment'></div>以臣愚见，曷若以一权侍郎解炎台职，而徐庚金、方应发、程元岳、杨潮南、丁应奎，并与祠禄，则不失轻重抑扬之义，而可以服天下之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1309887_comment'></div>陛下何惮而不为此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1309887_comment'></div>臣去冬固尝疏炎之缪，而不敢尽言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1309887_comment'></div>今所以先述庚金等之私意，而后叙天下之公议者，盖欲释陛下嗾使之疑，以开陛下神明之听也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1309887_comment'></div>臣不任拳拳，取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1309887_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_1309887'>〔贴黄〕臣犹有未毕之悃，敢敷陈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1309887_comment'></div>臣去冬尝准御笔，欲以沈炎为户部侍郎，兼知临安府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1309887_comment'></div>臣岂不将顺陛下之意，乘机而出之，则物论之定久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1309887_comment'></div>然臣扪心定虑，谓乘机则有机心矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1309887_comment'></div>一有机心，则何以上对苍穹，阴消夷狄？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1309887_comment'></div>故止告陛下，曰炎非尹京才也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1309887_comment'></div>于是炎尸位台端，又踰半载矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1309887_comment'></div>盖臣平生自勉，念念不敢欺天，步步不敢违天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1309887_comment'></div>若乘机而出之，则虽陛下无疑，而臣则有愧于心，不若尽言而出之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1309887_comment'></div>虽陛下不能无忤，而臣则无愧于心矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1309887_comment'></div>使为陛下臣子者人人与天为徒，而一毫人为不杂于其中，则夷狄之祸何至披猖至此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1309887_comment'></div>奈何为小人者固不知所谓天，而号为君子者，亦往往参之以人，故徒能欺人欺世，而不能欺天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1309887_comment'></div>故臣愿陛下纯以天为心，则天下事大定矣，猾虏何足畏哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1309887_comment'></div>并乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_81_1309887_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1260&endYear=1260')">1260年3月14日</a>　三月十四日，具奏令丁大全致仕等四事。作品：《同日具奏四事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1309888' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309888' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309888?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同日具奏四事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1260年3月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309888")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309888_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309888'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309888'>一、乞御笔，丁大全首降授中奉大夫，生前致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309888_comment'></div>一、乞御笔，董宋臣改提举绍兴府千秋鸿禧观，就绍兴府居住。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309888_comment'></div>臣又照得建康府门司官况极佳，若陛下以此畀之，亦不失仕宦之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309888_comment'></div>并取圣裁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309888_comment'></div>一、乞御笔，沈炎除权户部侍郎，徐庚金、方应发、程元岳、杨潮南、丁应奎并与祠禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309888_comment'></div>一、乞内批，高铸令羁管州军，决脊杖二十，配本州牢城，仍籍没家财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309888_comment'></div>同日奉御笔云：「览卿所奏，具悉来意，已依所拟施行，庶以示朕意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309888_comment'></div>卿之此劄，既不付出，却不须报行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309888_comment'></div>徐庚金等，卿已以一单劄以发其奸，沈炎等不必见之奏劄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309888_comment'></div>沈炎姑少缓除出，庶免为草茅辈所攻，以辱台纲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309888_comment'></div>卿宜深悉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309888_comment'></div>同日又奉御笔云：「览卿所奏极当，拟进三条，即已施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309888_comment'></div>李介叔充司业、二人免兼尤妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309888_comment'></div>是所引去之人，卿不可不发其奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309888_comment'></div>前日之判，有识之士莫不叹服也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309888_comment'></div>十五日又奏云：「臣恭准内批付下徐庚金等与祠事，以臣愚见，当来若不以炎权户部，从而出之，则庚金等与祠为称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309888_comment'></div>今陛下既少迟炎之出，则庚金不若与在外合入差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309888_comment'></div>然大略不过添倅干官而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309888_comment'></div>伏乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1309888_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1260&endYear=1260')">1260年4月1日</a>　四月一日，为沈炎所弹劾。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1260&endYear=1260')">1260年4月12日</a>　四月十二日，罢左相，以观文殿大学士提举临安洞霄宫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1260&endYear=1260')">1260年7月25日</a>　七月二十五日，夺观文殿大学士，罢祠，削二秩，谪居建昌军。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='fea6f535e304457b8737f30efe442ed0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fea6f535e304457b8737f30efe442ed0");'><span id='fea6f535e304457b8737f30efe442ed0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1262&endYear=1276')">1262-1276年</a>，68-卒后14年</div><div id='fea6f535e304457b8737f30efe442ed0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1262&endYear=1262')">1262年6月8日</a>　六月初八，诏许归葬。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年3月11日</a>　三月十一日，追复元官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>　赠谥，特赠少师。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
绍兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='110069386a7e458bb728ca470468fc2b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("110069386a7e458bb728ca470468fc2b");'><span id='110069386a7e458bb728ca470468fc2b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1218&endYear=1218')">1218年</a>，24岁</div><div id='110069386a7e458bb728ca470468fc2b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1218&endYear=1218')">1218年</a>　为镇东军节度判官。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='bd3a84fa649e4f959eabdbc941a44551_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bd3a84fa649e4f959eabdbc941a44551");'><span id='bd3a84fa649e4f959eabdbc941a44551_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1249&endYear=1249')">1249年</a>，55岁</div><div id='bd3a84fa649e4f959eabdbc941a44551' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1249&endYear=1249')">1249年11月18日</a>　冬到绍兴，十一月十八日吴文英出迓舟中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1249&endYear=1249')">1249年12月</a>　作存悔斋十二箴以励后学。作品：《宋存悔斋十二箴》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《两浙金石志》卷一二。）</span><div id='poem_1309913' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309913' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309913?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋存悔斋十二箴</a><span class='authorDate'>（1249年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309913")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1309913_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309913'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309913'>性一以静，心虚而明。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1309913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1309913'>以明合静，曰纯粹精。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1309913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1309913'>昂昂天民，昭昭帝命。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1309913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1309913'>万善百行，始于持敬。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1309913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1309913'>云行雨施，鱼跃鸢飞。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1309913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1309913'>愚、回早觉，达、赐晚知。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1309913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1309913'>濂溪光霁，延平洒落。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1309913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1309913'>其间工夫，先去刚恶。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1309913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1309913'>大小往来，屈伸感应。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1309913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1309913'>其机不停，莫若中正。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1309913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1309913'>吉生于悔，吝必有凶。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1309913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1309913'>所以圣贤，贵乎反躬。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1309913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1309913'>辱踵荣后，毁居誉前。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1309913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1309913'>吉无不利，在乎谦谦。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1309913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1309913'>蹇则修德，困则致命。<div id='poem_sentence_14_1309913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1309913'>无怨无尤，敬恭以听。<div id='poem_sentence_15_1309913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1309913'>为善成名，求名丧善。<div id='poem_sentence_16_1309913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1309913'>有为无为，义利之判。<div id='poem_sentence_17_1309913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1309913'>言倍招忧，事倍招患。<div id='poem_sentence_18_1309913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1309913'>以约失之，吾见亦罕。<div id='poem_sentence_19_1309913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1309913'>当遁戒尾，当集贵翔。<div id='poem_sentence_20_1309913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1309913'>圣人之道，进退存亡。<div id='poem_sentence_21_1309913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1309913'>两字包尽，偶阴对阳。<div id='poem_sentence_22_1309913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1309913'>君子所履，南方之强。<div id='poem_sentence_23_1309913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1309913'></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1309913_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1249&endYear=1249')">1249年12月</a>　十二月乙巳，召同知枢密院事兼参知政事。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
扬州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c648e296801f4585b28565d3912dc552_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c648e296801f4585b28565d3912dc552");'><span id='c648e296801f4585b28565d3912dc552_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1219&endYear=1219')">1219年</a>，25岁</div><div id='c648e296801f4585b28565d3912dc552' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1219&endYear=1219')">1219年</a>　初识姜夔于维扬。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='d5186f25c55244b69bbdf57cfed2414c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d5186f25c55244b69bbdf57cfed2414c");'><span id='d5186f25c55244b69bbdf57cfed2414c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年</a>，45岁</div><div id='d5186f25c55244b69bbdf57cfed2414c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年</a>　春日，渡江与赵葵踏青于瓜洲，有词记事。作品：《酹江月·瓜洲会赵南仲端明》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_103313' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103313' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103313?labeling=true' target='_blank'>酹江月/念奴娇<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>瓜洲会赵南仲端明</a><span class='authorDate'>（1239年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103313")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103313_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103313'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103313'>红尘飞骑，报元戎小队，踏青南陌。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103313'>雪浪堆边呼小渡，吴楚半江分坼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103313'>岁月惊心，风埃迷目，相对头俱白。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103313'>杨花撩乱，可怜如此春色。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103313_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103313'>谁道燕燕莺莺，多情犹自，认得年时客。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103313'>重唱江南肠断句，为我满倾云液。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103313'>画鼓舟移，金鞍人远，一饷烟波隔。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103313'>斜阳冉冉，依然无限凄恻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_103313_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
宣城
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='278312f220b544e895e0db64e10b5dc4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("278312f220b544e895e0db64e10b5dc4");'><span id='278312f220b544e895e0db64e10b5dc4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1224&endYear=1225')">1224-1225年</a>，30-31岁</div><div id='278312f220b544e895e0db64e10b5dc4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1224&endYear=1224')">1224年11月23日</a>　父柔胜卒，十一月二十三日，与兄长渊将其葬于宣城县石港之原。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1225&endYear=1225')">1225年</a>　丁父忧。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='d22bdbc3d9874250ae5fe2d9be3f3f49_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d22bdbc3d9874250ae5fe2d9be3f3f49");'><span id='d22bdbc3d9874250ae5fe2d9be3f3f49_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年</a>，44岁</div><div id='d22bdbc3d9874250ae5fe2d9be3f3f49' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年</a>　初夏在宣城，有词寿吴泳兄弟。作品：《八声甘州·寿吴叔永文昌季永侍郎》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_103102' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103102' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103102?labeling=true' target='_blank'>八声甘州<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>寿吴叔永文昌、季永侍郎</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103102")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103102_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103102'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103102'>记高冈、两凤揽朝晖，翩翻万里来。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103102'>向槐厅深处，松厅紧里，却立徘徊。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103102'>一舸风帆烟浪，拟竖锦江桅。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103102'>聊为玄晖老，共拂尘埃。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103102_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103102'>我亦归来岩壑，正不妨散诞，笑口频开。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103102'>算人间成败，何用苦惊猜。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103102'>便江南、求田问舍，把岁寒、三友一园栽。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103102'>今宵酒，只消鲸吸，不要论杯。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_103102_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='8cefd9588df74aaea159cc0da2bd245d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8cefd9588df74aaea159cc0da2bd245d");'><span id='8cefd9588df74aaea159cc0da2bd245d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1245&endYear=1245')">1245年</a>，51岁</div><div id='8cefd9588df74aaea159cc0da2bd245d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1245&endYear=1245')">1245年</a>　丁母忧。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='cd52bf34beb842728ec99dc6a2956172_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cd52bf34beb842728ec99dc6a2956172");'><span id='cd52bf34beb842728ec99dc6a2956172_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1253&endYear=1256')">1253-1256年</a>，59-62岁</div><div id='cd52bf34beb842728ec99dc6a2956172' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1253&endYear=1253')">1253年</a>　居宣城响山，种竹筑堂，咏眺自适。时与刘震孙宴游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1254&endYear=1254')">1254年</a>　提举临安洞霄宫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1255&endYear=1255')">1255年7月</a>　秋七月，录进旧闻理宗有关建储谈话，乞付史馆。作品：《秋七月因皇子进封忠王遵故事具奏录进旧来所得圣语乞付史馆》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1309868' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309868' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309868?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋七月因皇子进封忠王遵故事具奏录进旧来所得圣语乞付史馆<span class='inlineComment2'>（宝祐三年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1248年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309868")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309868_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309868'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309868'>臣伏见朝廷故事，每行下前宰执之家，宣索自来所得圣语，录付史馆，所以备纪载，扬休烈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309868_comment'></div>臣昨者恭睹皇帝陛下焕发神断，肇建皇储，增封王社，而皇子忠王德业日茂，令闻日章，薄海内外，莫不仰赞吾君之有子，实为社稷大庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309868_comment'></div>臣夙叨简拔，久侍清光，前后所闻玉音，关于国本之大计者颇详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309868_comment'></div>窃以为圣谟睿算，素定渊衷，蚤计预图，奠安宗社，巍巍圣功，诚非前代帝王之所能髣髴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309868_comment'></div>臣所合纪述本末，缮录家藏，以俟他时朝廷宣索。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309868_comment'></div>属臣频岁抱疴，近而转剧，深恐一旦溘先朝露，无以彰圣时之光明，谨具画一奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309868_comment'></div>欲望圣慈宣付史馆，登之琬琰，以昭示万世，与宋无极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309868_comment'></div>臣无任踊跃忭蹈之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309868_comment'></div>一、岁在丙午冬十月，臣蒙恩以兵部尚书召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309868_comment'></div>时皇子初除观察使，赐名某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309868_comment'></div>臣以十一月到阙，二十有一日蒙赐对于缉熙殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309868_comment'></div>臣第一劄子专以《复》卦为说，其间有云：「国必有副，立爱惟亲，此为陛下家之复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309868_comment'></div>得无有以迁延犹豫滞吾之复者乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309868_comment'></div>玉音云：「朕已喻卿意，此事朕意已有定属」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309868_comment'></div>臣恭聆圣训，谨寘诸心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309868_comment'></div>一、岁在丁未，臣待罪枢府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309868_comment'></div>七月初九日，同丞相郑清之、参政王伯大奏事，玉音云：「昨日有江西布衣王其姓者上书，其言诡异，颇于国本有关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309868_comment'></div>莫须稍示惩戒，以昭意向」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309868_comment'></div>臣与王伯大皆合辞赞和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309868_comment'></div>至十一月，郑清之谒告，臣与王伯大造朝，方坐漏舍，王伯大谓臣前日殿上所闻，可见主上圣谟高远，未尝顷刻忘天下大计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309868_comment'></div>吾辈何如将顺上意，因及国本正而后人心一之说，臣云甚善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309868_comment'></div>有顷奏事间，方稍稍敷陈，玉音即曰：「此事朕志已定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309868_comment'></div>但有两说，一则王夫人执谦，常有满盈之惧，犹未确许；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309868_comment'></div>二则某年方八岁，饮食起居，皆王夫人亲自看视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309868_comment'></div>若正名，须便入宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309868_comment'></div>万一起居饮食之间有失照管处，其间有多少事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309868_comment'></div>所以少迟岁月」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309868_comment'></div>臣与王伯大仰窥圣意之坚决，圣虑之深远，惟切赞诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309868_comment'></div>玉音又云：「朕以此事挂怀，兼年来国事多艰，焦劳忧虑，饮食亦自减少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309868_comment'></div>向来每日遇子午时，常宴坐移晷，收拾身心，近亦未免作辍」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309868_comment'></div>臣与王伯大奏：陛下处崇高富贵之中，而能凝神习定如此，万寿无疆，于此可卜，臣不胜叹仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309868_comment'></div>一、岁在庚戌，臣待罪政府，恭承陛下宣谕，郑清之等欲为皇子改赐嘉名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309868_comment'></div>一日玉音云：「朕欲于大字下寻一字」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309868_comment'></div>臣奏此乃老子《道德经》四大之义，蒙陛下首肯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1309868_comment'></div>臣有以仰见陛下期属皇子之意，非臣下管窥之所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1309868_comment'></div>一、岁在辛亥，臣待罪政府，闰十月二十有四日，同郑清之等奏事，恭奉玉音曰：「国本一事，朕志之定久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1309868_comment'></div>外论不察，犹多进定国本之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1309868_comment'></div>殊不知正名少迟者，盖以其年尚稚，未能便入禁中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1309868_comment'></div>况资善已建，更复何疑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1309868_comment'></div>恐缙绅间未尽知此意，卿等可以此说谕之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1309868_comment'></div>臣与同列恭领圣训而退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1309868_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1309868'>〔贴黄〕照对臣自丙午之冬，归文昌旧班，以至两登政地，迄于辛亥之冬，其闻玉音关于国本之重者，已备录在前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1309868_comment'></div>继而叨尘次辅，垂及期年，虽已窥圣意，必不出宝祐改元之后，资善志学之年，孚号正名，然为大臣之体，则惟有谨默将顺而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1309868_comment'></div>不谓萧泰来忽生异论，近又见有轮对者，复祖其说而阴煽之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1309868_comment'></div>臣窃以为陛下神谟睿烈，为社稷亿万年无疆之计，断在圣衷，岁月已久，皆非臣下一毫之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1309868_comment'></div>薄海内外之人，不论缙绅韦布，不论三军百姓，不论君子小人，向则延颈而企望，今则举手而欢欣，盖同此一心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1309868_comment'></div>而憸人邪士，乃凿空造隙，自为纷纷，以疑惑天下之听，甚无谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1309868_comment'></div>臣尝忝预宰司，休戚利害，与国同之，尤不可以不明言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1309868_comment'></div>伏乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1309868_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1255&endYear=1255')">1255年</a>　蔡抗寓书劝勉再出，其答以无意再仕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年4月23日</a>　四月，授沿海制置大使，判庆元府。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
嘉兴（嘉兴府）

<div class='label1' id='a4e39955f54f449e8d92483dad1bc62c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a4e39955f54f449e8d92483dad1bc62c");'><span id='a4e39955f54f449e8d92483dad1bc62c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1229&endYear=1229')">1229年</a>，35岁</div><div id='a4e39955f54f449e8d92483dad1bc62c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1229&endYear=1229')">1229年5月</a>　五月，添差通判嘉兴府，权发遣府事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1229&endYear=1229')">1229年</a>　与姜夔再会于嘉兴。<br /></div>
