class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1235&endYear=1235')">1235年</a>　奏造斛斗输诸郡租，宽恤人户，培植根本凡十五事。作品：《奏以造熟铁斛斗发下诸郡纳苗使用宽恤人户事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1309834' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309834' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309834?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏以造熟铁斛斗发下诸郡纳苗使用宽恤人户事</a><span class='authorDate'>（端平二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309834")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309834_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309834'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309834'>臣窃惟朝廷自更大化，诏旨之所戒敕，臣工之所建明，惟曰保护邦基，爱惜民力，于是宽恤之目以覈二税之中，以减损秋苗斛面为急，繇二浙以及于闽，又及于江之东，百姓蒙惠甚休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309834_comment'></div>独江右去天辽邈，且有司奉行弗虔，泽不下流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309834_comment'></div>臣猥仍承乏，输将一道，深惟此事乃端平亲政之第一义，凡在臣子，职当将顺布宣，是用不量驽钝，检准本司元被受指挥，再加诹度，仍刷到各郡秋苗租额及每岁受纳则例，量其丰匮，酌其多寡，或因或革，立为永制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309834_comment'></div>且从本司用文思院斛较制，创置熟铁斗斛，雕镌记号，发下各郡，自端平二年为始，专充交收秋苗使用，并令人户自行槩量，不许额外别创名色，多取颗粒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309834_comment'></div>如违，许人户越诉，自守贰以至受纳官，并行举劾问窜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309834_comment'></div>庶几远方赤子均被惠泽，少称圣天子爱养元元之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309834_comment'></div>须至开具奏闻者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309834_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1309834'>一、隆兴府管催秋苗一十九万一千七百一十石八斗四升九合五勺，每一石以一石六斗为准，正耗、义仓等米并在其内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309834_comment'></div>仍给五斗铁斛十只，一斗铁斛十只。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309834_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1309834'>一、吉州苗盐米一十六万石，约收米二十四万一千六百石，每一石以一石五斗为准；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309834_comment'></div>屯田米四万石，约收米四万九千六百石，每一石以一石二斗为准，正耗、义仓等米并在其内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309834_comment'></div>仍给五斗铁斛十六只，二斗铁斛十六只。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309834_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1309834'>一、吉州吉水、永丰、太和、万安、龙泉县共受领九万九千二百二十二石一斗六升，同前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309834_comment'></div>仍各给五斗铁斛四只，二斗铁斛四只。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309834_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1309834'>一、赣州岁催秋苗八万六千五十七石五斗四升，每一石以一石三斗为准，正耗、义仓等米并在其内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309834_comment'></div>仍给五斗铁斛八只，三斗铁斛六只。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309834_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1309834'>一、袁州岁额催秋苗一十一万九千四百五石五斗三升五合七勺六抄，每一石以一石五斗为准，正耗、义仓等米并在其内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309834_comment'></div>仍给五斗铁斛十只。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309834_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1309834'>一、瑞州岁额催秋苗九万七千三百五十七石一斗七升四合一勺四抄，每一石以一石六斗为准，正耗、义仓等米并在其内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309834_comment'></div>仍给五斗铁斛八只，一斗铁斛六只。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309834_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1309834'>一、江州岁额催米四万三千六十九石七斗八升，每一石以一石六斗为准，正耗、义仓等米并在其内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309834_comment'></div>仍给五斗铁斛六只，一斗铁斛六只。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309834_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1309834'>一、江州德安县米一万一千七百五十二石一斗七升五合，每一石以一石二斗五升为准，正耗、义仓等米并在其内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309834_comment'></div>仍给五斗铁斛四只，二斗五升铁斛四只。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309834_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1309834'>一、抚州额管实催临川等五县苗屯米一十三万七千二百七十九石四斗九升，每一石以一石四斗五升为准，正耗、义仓等米并在其内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309834_comment'></div>仍给五斗铁斛十只，四斗五升铁斛六只。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309834_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1309834'>一、临江军岁额实催四万九千一百六十七石六斗九升，每一石以一石四斗为准，正耗、义仓等米并在其内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309834_comment'></div>仍给五斗铁斛六只，四斗铁斛六只。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309834_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1309834'>一、临江军新淦县额实催苗五万六千八十四石一斗四升，每一石以一石四斗为准，仍给五斗铁斛六只，四斗铁斛四只。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309834_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1309834'>一、建昌军额管实催四万九千五百二十五石三斗八升，每一石以一石七斗为准，正耗、义仓等米并在其内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309834_comment'></div>仍给五斗铁斛七只，二斗铁斛六只。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309834_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1309834'>一、兴国军实催米二万八百三十五石八斗四升，每一石以一石五斗为准，正耗、义仓等米并在其内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309834_comment'></div>仍给五斗铁斛六只，二斗五升铁斛四只。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309834_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_1309834'>一、兴国军大冶县合催米四千一百一十三石三斗九升，每一石以一石四斗为准，正耗、义仓等米并在其内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1309834_comment'></div>仍给五斗铁斛四只，四斗铁斛四只。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1309834_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_1309834'>一、南安军岁催苗米八千七百五十八石二斗三升，每一石以一石七斗为准，正耗、义仓等米并在其内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1309834_comment'></div>仍给五斗铁斛四只，二斗铁斛四只。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1309834_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_1309834'>右开具在前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1309834_comment'></div>臣再照得昨来诸路监司遵奉御笔指挥，除减所部州县秋苗斛面，如浙西州郡有一岁顿减数万石者，江东州郡有一岁顿减二三万石者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1309834_comment'></div>所在守臣，能仰体九重宽大之泽，通融斡旋，补助支遣，初不见其不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1309834_comment'></div>今臣榷定之数，系据诸郡从实申到数目，量加裁损，于诸郡初无大段亏折，委可行之经久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1309834_comment'></div>如蒙圣慈更赐明诏，诸郡确意奉行，其于培植根本之计，诚非小补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1309834_comment'></div>伏候敕旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1309834_comment'></div>并申尚书省、御史台、谏院，伏乞照会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1309834_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_1309834'>〔贴黄〕臣再照得本路诸郡所裁减秋苗斛面，为数不多，尽可通融裨补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1309834_comment'></div>惟南安军旧系两石纳一石，今与除蠲三斗，比之诸郡，其数稍多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1309834_comment'></div>却恐本军地接溪峒，财计素殚，设有非逆支遣，未易支吾，合议贴助，庶可悠久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1309834_comment'></div>本司今契勘得本军南康县及抚州乐安县，每岁合解本司代发湖广总领所米价钱八千八百石，内南康县五千石，乐安县三千八百石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1309834_comment'></div>本司从例收籴本色米六千四百二十五石，并将合得兴国军首复米一千石，共凑七千四百二十五石，起解赴总领所交卸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1309834_comment'></div>今来本司欲于南康县五千石价钱内，拨二千三百七十五石，裨助本军支遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1309834_comment'></div>所有自馀二千六百二十五石价钱及乐安县三千八百石价钱，并兴国军首复正米一千石，正撞每岁合解总所七千四百二十五石之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1309834_comment'></div>欲乞睿断行下所属，径自解赴总所，本司更不拘催收籴代发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1309834_comment'></div>仍劄下湖广总领所照会，实为永远莫大之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1309834_comment'></div>伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1309834_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1235&endYear=1235')">1235年</a>　奏废隆兴府进贤县土坊镇。作品：《奏乞废隆兴府进贤县土坊镇以免抑纳酒税害民滋扰》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷二。宛敏灏《吴潜年谱》“滋扰”作“之扰”）</span><div id='poem_1309835' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309835' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309835?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞废隆兴府进贤县土坊镇以免抑纳酒税害民滋扰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1235年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309835")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309835_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309835'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309835'>窃见本府进贤县管下有聚落一区，地名土坊，居民不满数十，商旅稀少，强名曰镇，而有酒税务一所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309835_comment'></div>所谓税者，考其岁额入于本府者止三千馀缗，入于通判厅者止一千三百馀缗，然实解不及三分之二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309835_comment'></div>通一岁而论，官司之所得者，不过二千馀缗而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309835_comment'></div>所谓酒者，初无酝造，亦无发卖，系于镇户量其家第之高下，抑令纳钱，一户或四五十文，或三十文，或七八文，以是为月解，岁亦不过千数百缗而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309835_comment'></div>合二者而计之，可谓毫末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309835_comment'></div>而本镇却有酒税官一员，专拦数辈，恶少爪牙数十人，皆蚕食于数十户之市民，甚则罗织村氓，攘夺商旅，又甚则拦截客舟于二三十里之外，以是为办官课，而实则为官吏专拦等辈囊橐之地，民旅之被扰，非一日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309835_comment'></div>臣窃以为事有不便于民，虽官有大利，尚当决去，况此无甚利于官，而有害于民，然此为有司者，何忍以二三千缗之岁入，而使一方赤子永无聚庐托处之安乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309835_comment'></div>臣除已将本镇酒税一面住收外，欲望圣慈轸念民瘼，亟赐允俞，将本镇酒税务特行废罢，下吏部永不作缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309835_comment'></div>其见任人，令赴部别行注授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309835_comment'></div>庶几遐陬僻壤之民，鼓舞圣恩，如在殿角。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309835_comment'></div>臣无任恳望之至，谨具奏闻，伏候睿旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309835_comment'></div>并申尚书省，欲望钧慈更赐敷奏，亟降指挥施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309835_comment'></div>伏候钧旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309835_comment'></div>并申御史台、谏院照会。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1309835'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1309835_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1235&endYear=1235')">1235年</a>　奏将隆兴府绍定六年以前官物住催乞行下本路一体蠲阁。作品：《奏江右诸郡兵荒已将隆兴府绍定六年以前官物住催乞行下本路一体蠲阁》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1309836' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309836' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309836?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏江右诸郡兵荒已将隆兴府绍定六年以前官物住催乞行下本路一体蠲阁</a><span class='authorDate'>（1235年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309836")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309836_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309836'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309836'>照对臣猥以菲才，蒙恩将指，尝惧无以抚摩凋瘵，保护根本，少称明时临遣之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309836_comment'></div>窃见江右诸郡，仍年寇攘水毁之馀，市井萧条，田里憔悴，不堪举目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309836_comment'></div>去岁虽得中熟，譬犹尪羸伤败之人，仅能饮食，正要扶持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309836_comment'></div>而臣访闻所部州军之吏，大率聚敛之政多，宽恤之政少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309836_comment'></div>其见催四年柴料，如端平元年夏税秋苗、二年夏税，民閒自不应拖欠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309836_comment'></div>若乃绍定五年六年逋负，例皆细民下户些小奇零，及逃亡倚阁不可催理之数，所在征取，尚多峻急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309836_comment'></div>公家之所得，其实无几，奸吏之并缘，其害不赀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309836_comment'></div>臣偶兼权隆兴府职事，遂将本府财计考核源流，剔括弊蠹，见得仅可支吾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309836_comment'></div>已将绍定六年以前应于民间未纳官物并与住催，仍以隆兴府为准，行下本路州军，一体蠲阁施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309836_comment'></div>庶几宽之一分，民受一分之赐，仰副圣主子惠困穷之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309836_comment'></div>须至奏闻者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309836_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1309836'>〔贴黄〕照得臣所兼管隆兴府虽称都会，财计所入，极为殚窘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309836_comment'></div>而用度至为不赀，勉强支撑，尚可少施及物之政，诸郡可以类推。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309836_comment'></div>臣所以先自隆兴蠲阁，正欲以身率所部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309836_comment'></div>并乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1309836_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1235&endYear=1235')">1235年</a>　论计亩官会一贯有九害。作品：《奏论计亩官会一贯有九害》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1309837' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309837' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309837?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏论计亩官会一贯有九害</a><span class='authorDate'>（1235年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309837")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309837_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309837'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309837'>据隆兴府都厅申，准九月十一日省劄，行下两浙、江东西、福建、湖南等路，应有官之家并寺观，每田一亩出官会一贯，以助收减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309837_comment'></div>窃详上件指挥，关系不小，臣叨缀班行，职奉使指，万民利害，所当讲明，一郡施行，又当任责，须至奏闻者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309837_comment'></div>臣闻利不十者不变法令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309837_comment'></div>略计一件指挥，其害有九，其利有一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309837_comment'></div>且利不十则不为，况一利而九害乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309837_comment'></div>官会之多，三十年矣，端平以来，适当其极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309837_comment'></div>始者求快一时，尽收两界，已事遄往，无以议为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309837_comment'></div>今欲使官户寺观计亩纳会，以目前论之，会价必踊，且可收会，此一利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309837_comment'></div>然朝廷不过欲秤提官会耳，立国在民，民心一失，民力又穷，虽尽收会子，纯用铜钱，能保祸乱之不作乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309837_comment'></div>请言其害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309837_comment'></div>且有官之家，除富人外，其它初筮贫儒，觕守先业，偶以入仕，便令出会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309837_comment'></div>出会必用钱，用钱必鬻产。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309837_comment'></div>唐德宗间架收税，犹给军须，今朝廷计亩出钱，但收故纸，是计出唐下，而人怨则同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309837_comment'></div>其害一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309837_comment'></div>簪缨之后，既少见禄，又拙经营，仅有薄田，以给衣食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309837_comment'></div>百亩以上，或未开析，及此身者多，是凡称官户，皆不免也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309837_comment'></div>虽云百亩以下，本户无人入仕者免，此非计属不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309837_comment'></div>将有实满百亩而得免，亦有不及百亩而勒出者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309837_comment'></div>既出官会，又赂乡胥，何以当此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309837_comment'></div>其害二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309837_comment'></div>比年以来，朝廷以和籴抛降，以秤提官会，以庆典郊恩，计今江浙、福建之民，盖校尉连车，而迪功平斗矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309837_comment'></div>未沾铢金之俸，遽同入仕之科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309837_comment'></div>且既令出会以买此官，又因得官而再出会，臣恐自今以后，人人不特以官会为戒，尤以有官为戒矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309837_comment'></div>未必收秤提之功，已先失鬻爵之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309837_comment'></div>又况贫乏士人，偶得一解，遭际庆典，本为亲荣，岂料反为家祸！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309837_comment'></div>其害三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309837_comment'></div>两浙形势之家，虽计亩多而出会易，然陛下仁慈，估籍之典，犹不欲行于贪吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309837_comment'></div>况其父祖非勋旧则宗戚，亦何忍使比闾小吏数其籍而索其赀，为大不美，若泥中之斗兽乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309837_comment'></div>且有官之家既不得免，簪缨之后又不得免，而权贵之家尤不得免，然则天下皆不得免也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309837_comment'></div>以为不忍有扰于民而施于有官，岂官户非民耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309837_comment'></div>抑但以商贾佃户为民耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309837_comment'></div>且彼无所从出，不过均诸佃户耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309837_comment'></div>今又为之法，许其越诉，是教佃户以诉主家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309837_comment'></div>其害四也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1309837_comment'></div>寺观所在不同，湖南不如江西，江西不如两浙，两浙不如闽中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1309837_comment'></div>然比年贿赂盈门，主首类皆席卷，以偿所费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1309837_comment'></div>闽中僧寺，犹狼狈不如旧，它可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1309837_comment'></div>若道观则所设无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1309837_comment'></div>且田莫多于寺观，然欲于田之外责以一钱，实无从出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1309837_comment'></div>为国取民，一至于此，亦太无具甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1309837_comment'></div>有万亩者当出万缗，非起债则逃窜，此事未行而其兆已见，不待知者而后知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1309837_comment'></div>行香祝寿，汉官旧仪，一顿萧条，恐非美事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1309837_comment'></div>且为僧者必少，祠牒愈不可鬻矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1309837_comment'></div>其害五也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1309837_comment'></div>一路之田，岂无三数百万亩，是一路白出三数百万缗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1309837_comment'></div>一州之田，岂无四五十万亩，是一州白出四五十万缗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1309837_comment'></div>向者朝廷已竭帑藏，出数千百万以收此楮，而此事已无成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1309837_comment'></div>今州郡又竭闾阎，出数千百万以收此楮，而此事必有甚焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1309837_comment'></div>安有古今天下，内捐数千百万，外捐数千百万，不为用兵，不为振民，不为土木，乃为区区故纸而费之若此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1309837_comment'></div>可谓拙矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1309837_comment'></div>其害六也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1309837_comment'></div>今立法而约之曰，折阅吾楮，官吏按劾，百姓徒配。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1309837_comment'></div>然且不信而日轻，顾乃明示之以截凿不用，是教之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1309837_comment'></div>臣恐法行之后，民间愈不用会，而会子皆无用矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1309837_comment'></div>其害七也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1309837_comment'></div>且陛下亲政以来，尝兴十万之师矣，尝阅殿步二司之兵矣，而中外骚动，祸变随之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1309837_comment'></div>幸而圣德彰闻，天命巩固，人心自定，事变自消。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1309837_comment'></div>今又不戒，轻听议者之言，遽为率尔不审思之举，谤讟由此而兴，盗贼由此而起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1309837_comment'></div>昔之谤讟，官吏受之，今之谤讟，朝廷受之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1309837_comment'></div>昔之盗贼，有罪无辞，今之盗贼，有辞无罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1309837_comment'></div>且姑舍是，其目前必可知者，有四患焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1309837_comment'></div>有田亩不整之患，有土产不齐之患，有势必用刑法之患，有每事行赂之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1309837_comment'></div>何谓有田亩不整之患？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1309837_comment'></div>盖官户寺观，若一一要见实数，必用追索干照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1309837_comment'></div>而江浙之间，以诡户走苗税，又多白契，不登簿书，仓猝整会，必落吏手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1309837_comment'></div>如此则下户独受其害，而上户可免，中户亦以计会免矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1309837_comment'></div>独寺观可以簿书考，将恐寺观亦巧计飞走，寄附形势，而因之以失常住矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1309837_comment'></div>何谓有土产不齐之患？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1309837_comment'></div>闽中田贵而税轻，然人户田少，五七十亩已充里正，而钱尤难得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1309837_comment'></div>江东西又不然，除平野上腴之外，水田多潦，山田多旱，亩直不过一二千，盖有数年不得收者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1309837_comment'></div>若例出一券，为之奈何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1309837_comment'></div>以田售之于人则人不欲，以田归之于官则官不受，典质则空竭，称贷则艰难，亦有逃移流移而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1309837_comment'></div>二浙之田，独湖、苏、秀为最美，而常、杭则次之，衢、越为常稔，而严、婺、台则不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1309837_comment'></div>且和籴和买，取之悉矣，独未出会耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1309837_comment'></div>何谓有用刑行赂之患？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1309837_comment'></div>二税五赋，豪良且不乐输，况乎白科抑而责以体国乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1309837_comment'></div>施行之初，既曰礼谕，必不严督，其送纳必迟迟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1309837_comment'></div>上司未免行下，则追监继之，不集则鞭朴继之，若又不集，必重其罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1309837_comment'></div>于是人户有性命之忧，而县道又添一项催科之苦矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1309837_comment'></div>凡官司举事，茍一涉民，无非吏福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1309837_comment'></div>且户出若干会，必经司，必经揽户，必经县吏，必经州郡，必经上司，所经之处，非金钱不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1309837_comment'></div>使强明之吏临之，尚或庶几，不然则走弄文移，出入赋籍，增减田亩，千蹊万辙，尽归吏奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1309837_comment'></div>此固平日朘吾民膏血者所喜闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1309837_comment'></div>四患晓然，非有难见，然则天下多事矣，又况如前所谓谤讟盗贼之患乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1309837_comment'></div>其害八也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1309837_comment'></div>《春秋》讥初税亩者，履亩而税也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1309837_comment'></div>今朝廷以为吾截凿所入，以示不为己私，与彼之履亩不同，然它日国有大费，无所从给，则又将责有官之家，曰：曷不体国！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1309837_comment'></div>一纸举行，易收减为轻费，岂不可乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1309837_comment'></div>作法于凉，其弊犹贪，作法于贪，弊将若何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1309837_comment'></div>其害九也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1309837_comment'></div>臣以至愚极陋，少蒙先帝亲擢于多士之中，又蒙皇帝陛下简记于外寮之末，今者数月之顷，至三锡命，虽见控免，决不敢留，而一日必葺，罔间去留，可为忠言，敢有避忌？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1309837_comment'></div>臣自闻朝旨，夜思昼度，以为恐不可行，害多利少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1309837_comment'></div>而江西一道，官户者多贫，为富室者多讼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1309837_comment'></div>且比年盗贼焚毁，军兵经过，人无盖藏，甫得一稔，若重以无艺，必大狼狈，萧墙之内，将有不测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1309837_comment'></div>臣虽碎首死国，何补于事！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1309837_comment'></div>用敢冒大诃谴，先事言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1309837_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下鉴圣经之所讥，审国论之所极，亟收计亩之令，别求通币之策，庶保安静之福，不启怨谤之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1309837_comment'></div>所有上件省劄，臣除已权宜行下诸郡别听回降外，欲乞睿断早与收回，天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1309837_comment'></div>伏候指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1309837_comment'></div>谨奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1309837_comment'></div>并申尚书省照会施行，御史台、谏院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1309837_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_101_1309837'>〔贴黄〕臣照得秤提官会，当随方而为之术，择人而行其智，本无甚难，今犹可救，正不在出此下策，并乞睿照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1309837_comment'></div>又臣窃恐朝廷之上，重于反汗，未以愚言为然，区区更有愚悃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1309837_comment'></div>江右十年兵盗，如建昌、抚州、章贡、庐陵管下，皆尝破残，瑞州所部，亦曾有窃发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1309837_comment'></div>所谓上户者奔窜流离，藏盖空竭，方幸小稔，疮痍未瘳，可为哀痛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1309837_comment'></div>或蒙圣慈以江右创残非他道比，权与寝免目前，庶几一路之人知圣主轸念遐陬，如在殿角，感激爱戴，盗贼自消。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1309837_comment'></div>并乞睿照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1309837_comment'></div>又臣又有深忧过计，窃见朝廷更新大化，登用俊良，群阴屏迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1309837_comment'></div>或恐失职之人故设此画，以愚建议之臣，使朝廷结怨天下，万一有意外之虞，则此得以遂其所志，不可不察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1309837_comment'></div>并乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_109_1309837_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1235&endYear=1235')">1235年</a>　再论计亩纳钱。作品：《再论计亩纳钱》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1309838' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309838' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309838?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再论计亩纳钱</a><span class='authorDate'>（1235年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309838")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309838_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309838'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309838'>照对臣昨奉朝旨行下，官户寺观，计亩出会，以助秤提，仍委臣访察本路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309838_comment'></div>臣即尝条利害，冒昧奏闻，未准回降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309838_comment'></div>再准省劄，仰日下措置奉行，毋得再行违阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309838_comment'></div>臣素抱朴忠，粗知国体，极知楮券之弊，深轸君相之忧，茍可扶救于万分，所愿推行于尺寸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309838_comment'></div>第以国脉民命，关系匪轻，沥血陈词，诚当万死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309838_comment'></div>今未暇论万世之是非，四方之利害，只以臣本道言之，事体实有未便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309838_comment'></div>盖自嘉定至绍定三十年间，常有盗贼，近方宁息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309838_comment'></div>丁亥至癸未十年间，常苦水旱，近方稔熟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309838_comment'></div>残破之处，未还旧观，荡析之人，未复旧业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309838_comment'></div>井邑多瓦砾，田野多草莱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309838_comment'></div>昔号富实之家，今皆空虚之室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309838_comment'></div>比之他路，委实不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309838_comment'></div>兼南安、建昌、吉、赣，道接山峒，类以招安而受爵，与夫防拓而得官，平时官司，尚难调御，一旦科配，易激纷纭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309838_comment'></div>至其寺观，尤其荒凉，既欲征钱，必动常住，既动常住，必无以赡养其徒，必溢而之四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309838_comment'></div>驱毁情灭性之人，而置之饥寒离散之异域，人所不料，岂无可虞！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309838_comment'></div>如近时湖南谢了圆之事，可以鉴矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309838_comment'></div>臣反复思惟，与其召变于他时而贻九重之忧，宁若方命于此日而贻一身之谴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309838_comment'></div>是用不避窜斥，荐至数陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309838_comment'></div>欲望圣慈特发睿断，以江右寇盗甫平，饥馑甫息，免同诸路一例敷歛，臣与十一州赤子，不任延颈望幸之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309838_comment'></div>须至奏闻者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309838_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1309838'>〔小贴子〕臣窃惟朝廷命令举措，上关宗社安危，下关生灵休戚，故必审而后发，发而无悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309838_comment'></div>如往者北伐之议，起于癸巳之冬，成于甲午之春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309838_comment'></div>臣时待罪淮西总饷，尝奏疏一通，力陈兵之不可轻用，又尝上宰执白劄子，力陈兵之不可轻用，而陛下不之察，朝廷不之省，迄致败缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309838_comment'></div>盖无隙而动，终负师曲之名，为敌人口实，一可恨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309838_comment'></div>精兵良将，粮储器械，未免失亡，二可恨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309838_comment'></div>挠败之形，懦怯之證，呈露于中原四战之冲，使夷狄生心，英雄窃笑，三可恨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309838_comment'></div>今日计亩敷券之事，不审而发，发而必有后悔，胡以异此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309838_comment'></div>剜心肉以救眼创，拨根本以扶枝叶，纵使目前会价渐穷，物价渐减，而朝廷之印造不已，奸民之伪造不已，铜钱则海道之漏泄不已，器用之鉟销不已，朝满夕除，势所必至，不过年岁，弊将如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309838_comment'></div>而心肉之已剜者则不可复补，根本之已拨者则不可复培矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309838_comment'></div>此非陛下自著精神，大为断制，恐无以回物情于已散，挽人心于将离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309838_comment'></div>不然，以国家之急政要务，天下之危机骇证，方纷然错杂于前，而陛下高拱如平时，一听其自起自仆，臣恐变故日臻，祸乱日至，后虽噬脐，嗟何及矣，岂特楮之一事而已哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309838_comment'></div>臣年二十三，蒙先皇帝亲擢之恩，旋屏废者十年，迄无一线之路，上报先帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309838_comment'></div>岁在丙戌，蒙陛下收召于闲冷之中，数载之间，内而省寺，外而麾节，忝窃过矣，称塞渺然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309838_comment'></div>中夜以思，陨涕如雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1309838_comment'></div>故茍有区区之见关于国家理乱安危之大端者，诚不敢以疏远自诡，缄默而不告陛下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1309838_comment'></div>一寸丹心，不任忧爱恳切之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1309838_comment'></div>并乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1309838_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1235&endYear=1235')">1235年</a>　进右文殿修撰、集英殿修撰、枢密都承旨、督府参谋官兼知太平州，五辞不允。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
当涂
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a488e67f70494dbd99a2e681a22bfd83_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a488e67f70494dbd99a2e681a22bfd83");'><span id='a488e67f70494dbd99a2e681a22bfd83_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1236')">1236年</a>，42岁</div><div id='a488e67f70494dbd99a2e681a22bfd83' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1236')">1236年1月11日</a>　正月十一日，谒魏了翁于采石镇，转陈孟珙所报军情。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='6c4c8bdbc7f448098a5589bdb5fbab13_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6c4c8bdbc7f448098a5589bdb5fbab13");'><span id='6c4c8bdbc7f448098a5589bdb5fbab13_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1236')">1236年</a>，42岁</div><div id='6c4c8bdbc7f448098a5589bdb5fbab13' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1236')">1236年</a>　未赴江州，仍回太平州。<br /></div>

-----title
九江（江州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8c85aca7b65e4bdfb7a05a94db70fe2c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8c85aca7b65e4bdfb7a05a94db70fe2c");'><span id='8c85aca7b65e4bdfb7a05a94db70fe2c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1236')">1236年</a>，42岁</div><div id='8c85aca7b65e4bdfb7a05a94db70fe2c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1236')">1236年2月</a>　二月间赴九江，留督府参谋军事。上疏言和战成败大计，宜急救襄阳。作品：《奏论和战成败大计襄宜急救备不可阙》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1309839' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309839' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309839?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏论和战成败大计襄宜急救备不可阙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1236年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309839")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309839_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309839'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309839'>臣恭惟皇帝陛下奋发英断，遴选枢臣，出助六师，察臣世受大恩，觕有爱国忧边之志，再颁隆旨，俾参谋画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309839_comment'></div>唯今事势，悉在目前，区处曲折，当禀行府，成败大计，盍告朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309839_comment'></div>曾参日省其身，以为人谋不忠为急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309839_comment'></div>况臣为陛下谋东南之事，知而不言，是谓不忠，言而不达，是谓不智，谨昧死言之，伏惟皇帝陛下试垂听焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309839_comment'></div>臣尝伏读国朝通鉴，每于宣和、靖康之事，痛愤流涕，以为虏非能也，亦非天也，我有三大缪焉尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309839_comment'></div>其初也轻于交敌，其继也轻于挑敌，其末也轻于奉敌，是谓三大缪，而皆自轻于为谋始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309839_comment'></div>夫吉凶关于举动，存亡决于转移，茍不谨重而轻于一发，由轻得败，由败得畏，由畏得亡，此王黼、耿南仲之徒所以误宣和、误靖康，又将误来者而未已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309839_comment'></div>臣不识忌讳，窃迹比年边事颇近似而无甚异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309839_comment'></div>蔡州之攻，是登州之约也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309839_comment'></div>汴京之议，是平州之约也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309839_comment'></div>两校之行，是王云之渐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309839_comment'></div>然而其祸未流，其来犹缓，则以襄与扬犹有兵，犹有任责之人，而彼犹有所顾忌也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309839_comment'></div>天下之愿和者，其人有三种：小人愿和，庸人愿和，敌人愿和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309839_comment'></div>敌人之愿和者，亦莫甚于近世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309839_comment'></div>本朝尝和金，金人尝和鞑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309839_comment'></div>夫惟既和，然后我无任责之人，无死敌之志，而大祸至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309839_comment'></div>是故金鞑常先于和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309839_comment'></div>我利其所欲者，在和可以息兵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309839_comment'></div>于是小人幸以为功，庸人幸以为安，而又忌夫任责之士也，则穷之以所不能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309839_comment'></div>故靖康以战穷李纲，纲以败去，而后和议定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309839_comment'></div>纲去而种师道邀击之策遂不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309839_comment'></div>北方无纲无师道，而后大河无备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309839_comment'></div>越明年而二酋分道并进，前无一人一骑之梗，仓卒之间，遂罹大祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309839_comment'></div>其本在于以战而穷任责之士，自撤其藩篱，后延之入也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309839_comment'></div>夫襄阳亦今之太原也，赵范之为人，虽未必尽如纲之贤，然不可谓无纲之忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309839_comment'></div>朝廷岂可不亟加拯援，而使虏得以并兵也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309839_comment'></div>襄事危则和有兆，和成则国事去矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309839_comment'></div>抑臣窃有疑焉，夫督府之来，为何事也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309839_comment'></div>将以解襄急也，抑徒以塞人言也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309839_comment'></div>将以解襄急也，则当如高宗皇帝手诏付张浚，使浚得以示刘光世，光世大骇，即日勒兵走伪齐七十万众，刘豫遂亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309839_comment'></div>故左相赵鼎常曰，督府事须从朝廷维持，浚每有事，鼎必取而施行之，此则沈与求辈所不及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309839_comment'></div>夫种在内，蠡在外，鼎在内，浚在外，譬犹埙篪相应而成声音，譬犹首尾相应而成权衡，譬犹太阿尽与之柄而后剸割，譬犹毛锥尽伸其肘而责以运转也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309839_comment'></div>不如是，督府虽遣，事必无成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309839_comment'></div>事无成而急不解，必中虏欲而和议决，臣尚忍言之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1309839_comment'></div>且督府又有甚难者，沿江有大制阃焉，京湖有大制阃焉，鄂也，庐也，扬也，各有制阃焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1309839_comment'></div>兵皆其兵，将皆其将，财皆其财，督府既不可得而调发，又不可得而寄治矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1309839_comment'></div>夫此皆要处也，皆盛藩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1309839_comment'></div>要处盛藩既不得即，于是不得已而之金陵，则金陵近，不得已而之江陵，则江陵远，乃不得已而之浔阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1309839_comment'></div>夫浔阳昔重而今轻，昔中而今左，岂可以六朝例论哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1309839_comment'></div>斗绝一隅，婴城自守，岂可以上援汉、下备淮哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1309839_comment'></div>夫遣之而无谋，居之而非都会，二者亦既异于张浚、叶义问之来矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1309839_comment'></div>如臣愚见，会兵黄州，勒兵而进，开府于鄂，进师江陵，示以形势，压以声威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1309839_comment'></div>春水方生，疾疫将起，彼虽禽兽，亦熟于兵，敢不解乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1309839_comment'></div>抑臣所虑既解之后，有以误靖康者误国论矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1309839_comment'></div>欲望圣慈下采愚虑，亲洒宸翰，一如绍兴督府勒兵，诸将用命，以解襄阳倒垂之急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1309839_comment'></div>既解之后，大为部分，改弦易辙，练兵积粟，一一可恃，杜绝和议，常为战备，示之以不可犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1309839_comment'></div>彼越大漠，踰两河，空虚无人，进有坚塞，退无因粮，必不敢出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1309839_comment'></div>持以数年，其内自乱，中原分裂，徐制其后，安知旧物之不复还哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1309839_comment'></div>臣岁在癸巳、甲午，总饷淮右，知朝廷有开边之议，尝因应诏上封事，力陈兵之不可轻用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1309839_comment'></div>又尝上宰执白劄子，力陈兵之不可轻用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1309839_comment'></div>而天高听邈，莫遂挽回，曾不旋踵，臣言粗验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1309839_comment'></div>今又不度疏贱，辄陈大计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1309839_comment'></div>盖前之战，今之和，其误一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1309839_comment'></div>官以谋为职，不敢不尽愚，惟陛下幸赦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1309839_comment'></div>谨具录奏闻，伏候指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1309839_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
湖口（江州）
-----detail

-----title
苏州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='936db04545364f048cedbd8c23d117a9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("936db04545364f048cedbd8c23d117a9");'><span id='936db04545364f048cedbd8c23d117a9_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1237')">1237年</a>　知平江府，秋冬时，有词作。作品：《满江红·姑苏灵岩寺涵空阁》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷二。）</span>《汉宫春·吴中齐云楼》<span id='poem_content_103298'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103298'>客子愁来，闲信马、到涵空阁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103298'>谁为我、敛云收雾，青天为幕。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103298'>八万顷湖如镜静，波神护断东南角。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103298'>望孤帆、杳杳度微茫，山邀却。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103298_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103298'>三塞外，纷狐貉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103298'>三径里，悲猿鹤。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103298'>算鸱夷老子，占他头著。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_103298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_103298'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_103298_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_103138' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103138' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103138?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汉宫春 吴中齐云楼</a><span class='authorDate'>（1237年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103138")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103138_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103138'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103138'>楼观齐云，正霜明天净，一雁高飞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103138_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103138'>江南倦客徙倚，目断双溪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103138_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103138'>凭栏自语，算从来、总是儿痴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103138_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103138'>青镜里，数丝点鬓，问渠何事忘归。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103138_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103138'>幸有三椽茅屋，更小园随分，秋实春菲。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103138_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103138'>几多清风皓月，美景良时。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103138_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103138'>陶贤乐圣，尽由他、岐路危机。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103138_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103138'>须信道，功名富贵，大都磨蚁醯鸡。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_103138_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年1月</a>　正月，看梅沧浪亭，和吴文英《贺新郎》词。作品：《贺新郎·吴中韩氏沧浪亭和吴梦窗韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_103204' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103204' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103204?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺新郎<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>吴中韩氏沧浪亭和吴梦窗韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103204")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103204_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103204'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103204'>扑尽征衫气。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103204_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103204'>小夷犹、尊罍杖屦，踏开花事。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103204_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103204'>邂逅山翁行乐处，何似乌衣旧里。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103204_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103204'>叹荒草、舞台歌地。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103204_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103204'>百岁光阴如梦断，算古今、兴废都如此。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103204_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103204'>何用洒，儿曹泪。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103204_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103204'>江南自有渔樵队。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103204_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103204'>想家山、猿愁鹤怨，问人归未。<div id='poem_sentence_7_103204_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_103204'>寄语寒梅休放尽，留取三花两蕊。<div id='poem_sentence_8_103204_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_103204'>待老子、领些春意。<div id='poem_sentence_9_103204_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_103204'>皎皎风流心自许，尽何妨、瘦影横斜水。<div id='poem_sentence_10_103204_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_103204'>烦翠羽，伴醒醉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_103204_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年</a>　有词与吴文英唱和。作品：《声声慢·和吴梦窗赋梅》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_103157' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103157' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103157?labeling=true' target='_blank'>声声慢 和吴梦窗赋梅</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103157")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103157_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103157'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103157'>挨晴拶暖，载酒呼朋，夷犹东圃西园。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103157'>绿萼枝头，两三初破轻寒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103157'>平生自甘寂寞，占冷妆、不为人妍。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103157'>林逋去，问影疏香暗，谁赋其间。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103157_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103157'>空想故山奇事，正烟横岭曲，月浸溪湾。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103157'>杏错桃讹，那时青子都圆。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103157'>惟饶梦窗知处，对翠禽、依约神仙。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103157'>休引角，怕征人、泪落塞边。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_103157_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年</a>　春日，游赵园，有词。作品：《蝶恋花·吴中赵园》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_103315' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103315' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103315?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蝶恋花<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>吴中赵园</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103315")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103315_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103315'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103315'>野树梅花香似扑。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103315_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103315'>小径穿幽，乐意天然足。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103315_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103315'>回首人间名利局。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103315_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103315'>大都一觉黄粱熟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103315_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103315'>别墅谁家屏簇簇。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103315_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103315'>绮户疏窗，尚有藏春屋。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103315_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103315'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_103315", 103315, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>镜断</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_103315", 103315, "Clauses/8/Comments/1")'>钗分</span>何处续。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103315_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103315'>伤心芳草庭前绿。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_103315_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年</a>　条具财计凋敝本末，以宽郡民，与王野争利害。授宝谟阁待制，提举太平兴国宫，改玉隆万寿宫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年</a>　有词赠别吴文英。作品：《浪淘沙·和吴梦窗席上赠别》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_103232' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103232' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103232?labeling=true' target='_blank'>浪淘沙令<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>和吴梦窗席上赠别</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103232")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103232_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103232'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103232'>家在敬亭东。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103232_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103232'>老桧苍枫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103232_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103232'>浮生何必寄萍蓬。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103232_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103232'>得似满庭芳一曲，美酒千钟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103232_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103232'>万事转头空。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103232_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103232'>聚散匆匆。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103232_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103232'>片帆稳挂晓来风。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103232_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103232'>别后平安真信息，付与飞鸿。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_103232_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
镇江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8556981bc3c843a0991586df2301b644_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8556981bc3c843a0991586df2301b644");'><span id='8556981bc3c843a0991586df2301b644_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1239')">1238-1239年</a>，44-45岁</div><div id='8556981bc3c843a0991586df2301b644' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年</a>　试户部侍郎，淮东总领财赋兼知镇江府，言边储防御等十五事。作品：《奏论江防五利》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1309846' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309846' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309846?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏论江防五利</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309846")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309846_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309846'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309846'>臣辄有江防末议，可以致悠久之利，而除目睫之害，僭用奏陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309846_comment'></div>照对本所近体探到镇江府节制司芦场一所，坐落建康府管下，其名曰杜真沙，周广一二十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309846_comment'></div>近因流民坌集，擅斫柴芦，渐觉生事，不免差承信郎、权镇江府节制司准备差遣胡拱之前去相视弹压。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309846_comment'></div>乃知此沙之上流民凡十七寨，寨各有长，老少不下十馀万口，强壮约一二万人，皆安、濠、真、滁四郡百姓，而总此十七寨者，则宗子时𣆳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309846_comment'></div>沙之对岸六和县界，地名郭墅、󱾀塘、王峡塔等处，又有强壮五千人，头目王瞻义，见行劄立硬寨，遥与时𣆳相为表里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309846_comment'></div>本所差官，既体探的实，遂亲行下时𣆳，立加晓譬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309846_comment'></div>旋据时𣆳状称，元系六合上户，丙申之冬，鞑贼侵犯六合城壁，总辖李江以城献贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309846_comment'></div>时𣆳兄成忠郎特差充黄州黄岗县尉时𣆺自率死士，与贼苦战，竟死于敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309846_comment'></div>时𣆳把持母亲，突围而出，仅得生全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309846_comment'></div>连年贼寇冲突，时𣆳团结乡井强壮，依险附险，屡与贼交锋，前后杀获，不知其计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309846_comment'></div>恐官司反行追取获到马匹，以此不敢闻官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309846_comment'></div>近于九月间，因探报鞑贼将并力于东淮，时𣆳深恐势不能敌，遂提十七寨老小渡江，于沙上屯泊，实不知其为使所芦场，荡析之民，未免采斫，结缚蘧芦，为遮蔽风雨之计，委非得已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309846_comment'></div>除遵依约束，告谕十七寨头目，督责所部，自相禁约，不敢侵斫，仍不敢一毫生事外，但念时𣆳忝出帝胄，每怀报国之心，不幸遭鞑贼之祸，真、滁之民以时𣆳自父祖以来粗有恩信于乡里，因推以为首，团结聚众，今十万老小，一二万强壮，目前虽有三两月之粮，尚可茍活，万一向去乡里未可归，生理无所仰，窃虑小人饥寒所迫，或稍违越于法禁之外，则时𣆳一身，万死何赎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309846_comment'></div>今虽蒙沿江制司差人前来，取责流民，单名细载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309846_comment'></div>缘别未有处分，闻又准行下起发五百人策应庐州，以此各寨头目未就团结。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309846_comment'></div>此来傥蒙使所时加区处，使之有可耕之田，无馁死之虑，则时𣆳乞将上项人听从官司拣选，籍充民兵，以备调遣，即不愿支破钱粮请给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309846_comment'></div>欲望务念淮民，疾速具申朝廷处置施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309846_comment'></div>臣按照杜真沙虽在大江，贴近南岸，并无限隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309846_comment'></div>今聚数万众于其上，所合早为区处，以消意外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309846_comment'></div>照得此沙芦场不下数万亩，其侧有赵姓、钟姓两户芦场，一以宝章，一以主簿立户，各不下数千亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309846_comment'></div>外此则有熟田三数万亩，只属两户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309846_comment'></div>一系真州长芦寺常住，今寺已焚荡，僧已散亡，是无主物业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309846_comment'></div>一系故将张俊府第之产。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309846_comment'></div>合三项芦场及两项田计之，约有二十馀万亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309846_comment'></div>区区之愚，拟将长芦寺田亩从官司拘管，张府田、赵钟二户芦场，并行拘籍，却将上项流民选精兵万人，人授田二十亩，令自耕种。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309846_comment'></div>却仿京淮民兵例，分为五将，总以统制一员，就令屯驻沙上，如此则立可收五利而去一害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309846_comment'></div>不仰朝廷请给，坐得万人精锐之卒，一利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309846_comment'></div>此沙正对滁河，设使此贼有意窃江，舟楫自滁河而出，沙上之军，便可迎剿，二利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309846_comment'></div>扬、滁、真三郡，或遭围闭，大军策应，其势实难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309846_comment'></div>此曹皆艰苦忍耐之卒，且屯驻江心，上岸击贼，洗脚下船，其势最为顺便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309846_comment'></div>使之解围劫寨，必能有济，三利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309846_comment'></div>升润之间，兵备素单，得此万人，增壮上下流声势，四利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309846_comment'></div>江淮血脉，易于间断，今沙上既有安、濠、真、滁四郡之人，则声闻相接，淮民之心，亦有系属，淮方之事，亦易体探，五利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309846_comment'></div>五利既具，而又可以弭萧墙不测之害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1309846_comment'></div>臣以为目前江防大虑，莫出于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1309846_comment'></div>欲望圣慈详酌事机，如以臣言为可采，即乞降圣旨，遵守施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1309846_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1309846'>〔贴黄〕再照得准黄榜指挥，招军头目人，如能团集一千人，补转一官资旨命，及二千人者补转两官资，以上等第推赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1309846_comment'></div>并乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1309846_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年</a>　奏选兵救合肥。作品：《奏乞选兵救合肥》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1309845' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309845' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309845?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞选兵救合肥</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉熙二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309845")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309845_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309845'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309845'>臣辄有管见，上冒宸严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309845_comment'></div>窃见鞑为不道，荐食边封，东哨真、滁，西哨丰、黄、濠、和，而顿重兵于合肥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309845_comment'></div>颇闻排舣木已立，炮座已起，其欲为窥伺合肥之计明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309845_comment'></div>合肥不支，则丰、黄、和已在掌股之中，而东方一无以自固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309845_comment'></div>东方不固，则江西之忧，浸浸乎有不可忌讳者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309845_comment'></div>故今日之策，莫急于救合肥，而救合肥之策，则有远近缓急轻重之宜，不可尝试而泛动也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309845_comment'></div>厥今兵力莫强于督府，当令史嵩之选精兵三万人，统以吕文德，道由巴河、三沟、凤凰崖，由山路取五糟河、火烧寨以东，至黄龙源、七里回、头驼河，出铁岭、小庭、糯米冲，以达舒城县，更百里即至庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309845_comment'></div>此所谓出于九地之下者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309845_comment'></div>其次，则淮东连年缉兵整武，虽号完固，然真、滁增兵，泗涟增兵，皆割维扬见存，若更抽摘，窃恐此贼乘虚捣袭，则根本动摇，不可不为长江门户之虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309845_comment'></div>谓宜令赵葵只于所部极力那拨北军五千人，令心腹爪牙之佐溯淮而上，至于濠、梁，就选北军二千人，又至寿春，更选北军三千人，又至安丰，更选北军二千人，合一万二千人，统以张仲宣，副以王安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309845_comment'></div>仍将一行人先与晋转官资，重犒金帛，许以解围之日高爵厚赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309845_comment'></div>仍暂令赵葵节制，调遣濠、寿春三郡策应人马，多方激励仲宣等，使之由安丰以进，其去庐亦只百一十里而近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309845_comment'></div>又其次，则当令沿江制阃办舟师万人，由当涂管下裕溪口或渗潭，入无为界，径进巢湖，姑止于湖心之巫山，以为西北两项步兵声援，遇便则进夺西口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309845_comment'></div>此贼年来轻视吾国，如入无人之境，不意吾之布置如此，纵使未能大挫其锋，其势必少沮矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309845_comment'></div>又须多募死士，往来三处，以通进止消息，及间道入合肥，以坚在城军民之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309845_comment'></div>但沿江所管地方，自池阳、当涂、建康以至镇江、许浦，多臣数年之间待罪之地，不惟兵籍空虚，而见在籍之兵，率多老弱憔悴，其可倚仗者十无一二，臣每为之寒心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309845_comment'></div>使其猝备万人，恐亦未易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309845_comment'></div>谓宜如畴昔周虎守历阳，西门垂陷，虎急募壮士，许以武翼郎，日支食钱一贯五百文，言未脱口，有应募者三百馀人下城死战，遂以却敌，保全一城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309845_comment'></div>今若立为赏格，令行招募江湖盗贼亡命，或可得三五千人，贴以正兵，统以良将，鼓行而前，恐能有济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309845_comment'></div>此固马隆之故智也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309845_comment'></div>又其次，则六安西山，虽经残破，尚有头目数人，自行团结，固守其间，合而计之，不下二三万人，皆频年百战之馀，坚苦忍耐之卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309845_comment'></div>谓宜遣才智忠勇之士，赍金帛诰命以往，抚其首领，激其士众，时出荡兵，相与挠劫，使此贼不得安意肆志，是又官军之一助也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309845_comment'></div>臣受国厚恩，恨无长策可解三边之急，僭越敷陈，罪当万死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309845_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1309845'>〔贴黄〕臣窃闻东淮自盱泗以北，鞑日增生兵，聚于应天海宿之境，伏而未动，未必不待淮扬兵力之分，为批亢捣虚之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309845_comment'></div>今又据真州干事人报，本州获到奸细一名张三者，称鞑将以十月半来攻仪真，先令其入城纵火为应，搜出火刀火石火药具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309845_comment'></div>以此推之，贼之狡计，又未可以其并力于西，而不东边根本之虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309845_comment'></div>并乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1309845_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年</a>　奏乞重濠、梁、招信戍守。作品：《奏乞重濠梁招信戍守》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1309847' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309847' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309847?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞重濠梁招信戍守</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309847")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309847_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309847'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309847'>臣辄有千虑之愚，上冒宸听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309847_comment'></div>窃见滁城被围，守将军民死守者三千馀口，不幸守臣陈广光死于飞炮，以故人心离骇，旋至陷没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309847_comment'></div>今贼已于二十六日摄寨入城，城内有朝廷桩管及两总所经常米斛，不下二十万馀，且弓刀箭凿器械火药石炮为数不少，贼皆得而有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309847_comment'></div>屈指春和，尚五六十日，无缘便肯退回巢穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309847_comment'></div>众人之虑，则以为贼必窥伺仪真、历阳，而臣之虑又有大于此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309847_comment'></div>盖滁乃江淮门户，自宣化至滁九十里，自滁至昭关三十里，自昭关至藕塘四十五里，自藕塘至定远六十里，自定远至濠州八十里，向北即是贼界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309847_comment'></div>由宣化而濠，大约止三百里，其间已无限隔，贼骑往来，不过一鞭而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309847_comment'></div>万一此贼袭取濠、梁，以通淮北之途，然后驻兵滁、扬，以为久留之计，则庐阳、盱、楚、真、和，反各在一隅，而贼固在腹心之内矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309847_comment'></div>江面之忧，将在旦夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309847_comment'></div>故今日之策，当死守濠、梁，以为东西淮砥柱，庶几贼犹有所牵制，不敢安息于滁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309847_comment'></div>俟其退归，或毁或徙，惟所以区处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309847_comment'></div>欲望圣慈亟赐睿断，令督府、淮西制司增添官兵，戍守濠、梁，以为必不可拔之基，实宗社之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309847_comment'></div>事体关系，非止一城，臣僭越敷陈，罪当万死，仰乞睿照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309847_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1309847'>〔贴黄〕臣再照得两日来淮东报，鞑贼见围绕招信，自青平山天长以至高邮宝应，绵亘二三百里，皆是贼寨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309847_comment'></div>以臣料之，贼若攻濠，其意盖欲通河南之贼，径至于滁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309847_comment'></div>贼若攻招信，其意盖欲通山东之贼，径至于滁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309847_comment'></div>滁至大寨九十里，大寨至青平山六十里，青平山至招信六十里，比之自濠至滁，道里相等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309847_comment'></div>然招信之外，尚有泗、宿，濠之外别无藩篱，则濠尤紧于招信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309847_comment'></div>大约二郡存则贼不容驻滁，一处不牢，则事势有难言者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309847_comment'></div>仰乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1309847_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年</a>　奏已差军剿逐鞑贼。作品：《奏已差军剿逐鞑贼》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1309848' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309848' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309848?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏已差军剿逐鞑贼</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309848")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309848_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309848'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309848'>照对本司连据探报，鞑贼摄移小寨，前来真州二才里头屯劄，时有哨骑薄真州城下，赶杀人民，直至江岸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309848_comment'></div>窃恐窥伺江面虚实，本司除先来已分布船只，严护诸邑，今又行劄差水军统制陈亮，领官民船一百二十只，精选人兵一千五百人，前去真州北岸一带，张耀巡逴，往来剿逐外，须至奏闻者。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1309848_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年</a>　奏论仪真存亡关系江面。作品：《奏论仪真存亡关系江面》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1309849' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309849' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309849?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏论仪真存亡关系江面</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309849")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309849_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309849'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309849'>臣辄有愚见，仰溷宸听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309849_comment'></div>窃见淮东人马虽已再入滁城，但郡经残破之馀，人民已尽，仓廪已空，楼橹已毁，守备之计，猝难插手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309849_comment'></div>今贼见窥伺仪真，事势颇急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309849_comment'></div>真之备御，素不逮滁，而真之存亡，关系江面，则其事体又非滁比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309849_comment'></div>故与其分兵力于贼已去之滁，孰若合兵力于吾必争之真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309849_comment'></div>真安则滁固自存，真危则守滁何益？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309849_comment'></div>欲望睿慈宣谕宰执，量事势之轻重，行下淮东制司，将复滁之兵，尽数抽入仪真捍御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309849_comment'></div>仍劄督府，令吕文德仍旧带所部人马，即赴仪真之急，非特固真，实以保江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309849_comment'></div>臣无任拳拳忧边体国之至，仰乞睿照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309849_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1309849'>〔贴黄〕臣窃闻近日吕文德在真，鞑之哨骑有至今城者，文德以单骑冲突，贼颇披靡，仪真之民，恃以为命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309849_comment'></div>比其提兵去真，人心为之骇沮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309849_comment'></div>以良将之去留，关系一城之休戚，委非细故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309849_comment'></div>并乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1309849_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年</a>　奏论本所团到流民丁壮攻劫鞑寨屡捷，置制司忌嫉兴谤等。作品：《奏论本所团到流民丁壮攻劫鞑寨屡捷置制司忌嫉兴谤等》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1309850' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309850' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309850?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏论本所团到流民丁壮攻劫鞑寨屡捷置制司忌嫉兴谤等</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309850")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309850_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309850'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309850'>照对臣昨缘去岁鞑寇侵犯淮东界分，有流民团聚建康府境内本所杜真沙上，侵斫官芦，本所遂差官前去抚谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309850_comment'></div>见有宗子时𣆳团到流民，头目不一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309850_comment'></div>沿江制司虽遣官招诱团结，缘所差之人多系武臣，但知倚势作威，乞觅搔扰，略不能以恩意抚纳，其时𣆳及以次头目等人，皆不肯受制司之令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309850_comment'></div>臣粗怀深远之虑，遂将时𣆳借补，檄令赴总领所禀议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309850_comment'></div>其时时𣆳闻令就道，臣即留之镇江，不复令再往沙上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309850_comment'></div>所有流民，却自行差官前往地头弹压，措置团结，并皆禀受约束，即无一毫生事作过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309850_comment'></div>只缘臣以鞑贼围闭滁阳，江面震动，而制司所调兵船在滁河口菖蒲荡等处，屡为鞑贼掩去兵稍，烧却船只。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309850_comment'></div>臣深虑事关利害，虽其地系建康界分，而臣以王人统隶江东，不敢坐视，遂分差胆勇兵将，并于时𣆳元团到流民内，选择精锐之士，时用小舟，夜渡过江，攻劫贼寨，屡枭到贼首及捉到投拜户，并夺到马匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309850_comment'></div>臣以其不足为贼大势轻重，不敢效近时一种欺罔之风，张皇奏捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309850_comment'></div>不谓沿江制司自不能遣兵过江，挠劫鞑寇，却归咎时𣆳，屡行下镇江节制司责问，谓时𣆳斫到贼首，夺到马匹，不应不解制司而解镇江府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309850_comment'></div>不知杀获之人，乃本所所遣，不识事势，或夺其财物，或取其稻谷，或污其妇女，或辱其衣冠，流民心不能平，遂以兵应，制司并不敢究问，亦不敢申明朝廷，何独于无过之时𣆳而加诬玷乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309850_comment'></div>此皆臣不合勇于体国，于建康境内团结丁壮，攻劫鞑寇，以致制司忮怒，而时𣆳遂为水蟹池鱼，臣实有愆，何可自逭！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309850_comment'></div>窃念臣一纪驰驱，惟知下朴实工夫，为国家抚恤军民，整葺武备，实不善饰口舌，以欺君父，诬同列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309850_comment'></div>今制司既过有申述，窃恐上关圣虑，臣万不得已，冒昧控陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309850_comment'></div>所有时𣆳已蒙朝廷特补承节郎，添差浙西安抚司准备将领，镇江府驻劄，见今在任管干，久已不干预沙上事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309850_comment'></div>仰乞睿照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309850_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1309850'>〔贴黄〕臣再照得当滁寇未退，人心动摇，沿江制臣又恐诸寨之人马溯江西上，谒督府于繁昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309850_comment'></div>时建康界内诸沙流民无不作过，而西沙颜文焕等为最，其安帖者惟杜真一沙而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309850_comment'></div>交焕固尝遣人邀约时𣆳以次头目，人欲表里相应，焚劫东杨以直至建康城外人民财物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309850_comment'></div>时𣆳之徒答以已受镇江吴侍郎团结，不敢随从作过，文焕等之流遂仅仅流毒于西沙而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309850_comment'></div>今制司不思本所密有功于制司，而反以招时𣆳为怼，支离粉饰，上以罔九重之聪，以欺公卿百执事之听，臣实惧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309850_comment'></div>欲望圣慈检照臣以母病请祠，俾寻香火之盟，不任大愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309850_comment'></div>并乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1309850_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年</a>　奏乞赏功，以兴起人心。作品：《奏乞赏功以兴起人心》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1309851' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309851' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309851?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞赏功以兴起人心</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309851")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309851_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309851'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309851'>臣窃惟有功不赏，有罪不诛，虽尧舜不能治天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309851_comment'></div>是知赏功罚罪，且不可废于平世，而况多事之日乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309851_comment'></div>照得去冬鞑为不道，既不得志于庐，遂并力于滁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309851_comment'></div>时知招信军余玠亲提精卒，转战入青平，戮力以赴滁之急，不幸师未达而滁溃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309851_comment'></div>贼既陷滁，悉兵乘时围玠于青平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309851_comment'></div>玠极力拒守，贼不获逞，乃以攻青平之师转而攻招信之虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309851_comment'></div>时适张子良叛于泗盱，内外无援，音信阻绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309851_comment'></div>玠以为盱一不守，则不惟青平不可保，淮东门户，将遂荡然，于是不顾危亡，复转战而入盱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309851_comment'></div>贼尽锐攻之，玠尽锐应之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309851_comment'></div>腊月二十六、二十七、二十八之战，杀贼无算，贼乃引去，玠被疮，几以不支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309851_comment'></div>盖去岁淮东却虏，玠之宣劳卫驾，绩实冠诸将，而未有以闻于上者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309851_comment'></div>虽玠昔为白鹿学徒，颇尝闻道，初不计功赏之有无，然两城士卒，用命鏖虏，似不可无以示劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309851_comment'></div>臣护饷东陲，实以报发御前军马文字为职，谊合敷陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309851_comment'></div>欲望圣慈特下有司，详酌施行，庶几有功见赏，足以兴起人心，其于边面，诚非小补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1309851_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年</a>　奏乞令东阃兼领总司以足兵食。作品：《奏乞令东阃兼领总司以足兵食》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1309852' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309852' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309852?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞令东阃兼领总司以足兵食</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309852")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309852_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309852'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309852'>臣窃惟四郊多垒之日，事有当通变者，制总两司之合是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309852_comment'></div>四总在绍兴间，本宣抚司钱粮官，秦丞相桧当国，与虏行成，遂创总领，以代抚司钱粮官之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309852_comment'></div>盖欲渐收诸将之权，以就和议，故其策不得不出于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309852_comment'></div>若今日之事体，则不可同而语矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309852_comment'></div>兵事方殷，调度益急，总所之权，素不能行于所部，则军籍之盈虚，戍兵之增减，钱粮之当支与不当支，皆莫可致诘，不过凭受给厅片纸销豁而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309852_comment'></div>其间事体之掣肘，移易之扦格，有不可尽述者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309852_comment'></div>此固势之所趋，非人之所为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309852_comment'></div>故臣以为总计并国之制司，有数利焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309852_comment'></div>以军伍言之，则缺额可稽，顶冒可核，一切冗滥可考；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309852_comment'></div>以钱粮言之，则利害自切于其身，戍兵之可减者减，生券之可省者省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309852_comment'></div>州郡将帅有所惮，而不敢妄取于受给厅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309852_comment'></div>受给厅有所凭，而不至受制于州郡将帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309852_comment'></div>以至籴买粮草，可以督责，不时借兑，可以那融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309852_comment'></div>纲船往来，郡县决不敢差踏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309852_comment'></div>纲米程限，巡尉决不敢羁违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309852_comment'></div>凡有行移，自如臂之使指，无不如意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309852_comment'></div>其与总所之自为总所，难易之相去殆不翅万万倍矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309852_comment'></div>臣愚欲望圣慈妙酌时宜，参用旧典，将淮东总领所职事，就令淮东制置大使司就行兼领，其于足食足兵，安边固圉之计，实非小补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309852_comment'></div>臣非欲籍此以辞繁难，亦非与制司别具异同，以此尝试朝廷，实以两尝护饷，亲见制总事宜莫便于此，是用冒昧奏陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309852_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1309852'>〔贴黄〕照得岁在癸巳，护饷西淮，尝摄沿江制置，臣以两司事体，自相通融，半年之间，为总所省生券钱二十馀万贯，米二万馀石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309852_comment'></div>此臣已试之验，非臆度之说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309852_comment'></div>况近年以来，如湖广累以制臣兼总，今孟珙亦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309852_comment'></div>嘉定间，岳珂为淮东总领，屡兼淮东制置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309852_comment'></div>制总互兼，其来已久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309852_comment'></div>今三边卒未有解甲之期，而淮东制司调度亦自不给，若令并领饷计，亦可使之伸缩进退，得以自如，实为边阃之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309852_comment'></div>并乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1309852_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年</a>　秋冬，在镇江，有词。作品：《水调歌头·焦山》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷二。）</span>《沁园春·多景楼》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_103132' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103132' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103132?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>焦山</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103132")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103132_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103132'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103132'>铁瓮古形势，相对立金焦。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103132'>长江万里东注，晓吹捲惊涛。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103132'>天际孤云来去，水际孤帆上下，天共水相邀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103132'>远岫忽明晦，好景画难描。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103132_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103132'>混隋陈，分宋魏，战孙曹。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103132'>回头千载陈迹，痴绝倚亭皋。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103132'>惟有汀边鸥鹭，不管人间兴废，一抹度青霄。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103132'>安得身飞去，举手谢尘嚣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_103132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_103132'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(103132)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><div id='poem_103161' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103161' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103161?labeling=true' target='_blank'>沁园春<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>多景楼</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103161")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103161_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103161'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103161'>第一江山，无边境界，压四百州。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103161_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103161'>正天低<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_103161", 103161, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>云冻</span>，山寒木落，萧条楚塞，寂寞吴舟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103161_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103161'>白鸟孤飞，暮鸦群注，烟霭微茫锁戍楼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103161_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103161'>凭阑久。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103161_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103161'>问匈奴未灭，底事菟裘。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103161_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103161'>回头。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103161_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103161'>祖敬何刘。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103161_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103161'>曾解把功名谈笑收。<div id='poem_sentence_7_103161_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_103161'>算当时多少，英雄气概，到今惟有，废垄荒丘。<div id='poem_sentence_8_103161_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_103161'>梦里光阴，眼前风景，一片今愁共古愁。<div id='poem_sentence_9_103161_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_103161'>人间事，尽悠悠且且，莫莫休休。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_103161_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年</a>　秋冬，在镇江，有词寄赵葵。作品：《酹江月·暇日登新楼望扬州于云烟缥缈之间寄赵南仲端明》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_103314' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103314' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103314?labeling=true' target='_blank'>酹江月/念奴娇<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>暇日登新楼，望扬州于云烟缈之间，寄赵南仲端明</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103314")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103314_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103314'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103314'>半空楼阁，把江山图画，一时收拾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103314_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103314'>白鸟孤飞飞尽处，最好暮天秋碧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103314_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103314'>万里西风，百年人事，谩倚阑干拍。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103314_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103314'>凝眸何许，扬州烟树历历。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103314_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103314'>应念老子年来，浮名浮利，已作虚空掷。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103314_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103314'>三径才寻归活计，又是飘零为客。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103314_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103314'>回首平生，惊心双鬓，容易成悽恻。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103314_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103314'>尊前一笑，且由醉帽攲侧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_103314_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年</a>　春日，寄词与赵葵，约期相会。作品：《贺新郎·寄赵南仲端明》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_103212' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103212' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103212?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺新郎<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span>寄赵南仲端明</a><span class='authorDate'>（1239年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103212")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103212_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103212'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103212'>烟树瓜洲岸。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103212'>望旌旗、猎猎摇空，故人天远。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103212'>不似沙鸥飞得渡，直到雕鞍侧畔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103212'>但徙倚、危阑目断。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103212'>自古钟情须我辈，况人间、万事思量遍。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103212'>涛似雪，风如箭。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103212_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103212'>扬州十里朱帘捲。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103212'>想桃根桃叶，依稀旧家庭院。<div id='poem_sentence_7_103212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_103212'>谁把青红吹到眼，知有醉翁局段。<div id='poem_sentence_8_103212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_103212'>便回首、舟移帆转。<div id='poem_sentence_9_103212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_103212'>渺渺江波愁未了，正淮山、日暮云撩乱。<div id='poem_sentence_10_103212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_103212'>阁酒盏，倚歌扇。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_103212_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='89deffd577bb4e4ca9abee0f5c890516_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("89deffd577bb4e4ca9abee0f5c890516");'><span id='89deffd577bb4e4ca9abee0f5c890516_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年</a>，45岁</div><div id='89deffd577bb4e4ca9abee0f5c890516' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年</a>　春日，游京口凤凰池，有词。作品：《满江红·京口凤凰池和芦川春水连天韵（池寔苏魏公旧游也）》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷二。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年5月</a>　改宝谟阁学士，兼浙西大提点坑冶，权兵部尚书，浙西制置使，申论防拓江海团结措置等事。作品：《奏乞增兵万人分屯瓜洲平江诸处防拓内外》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1309853' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309853' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309853?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞增兵万人分屯瓜洲平江诸处防拓内外</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉熙三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309853")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309853_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309853'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309853'>照对臣一介庸虚，猥叨选择，建阃浙右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309853_comment'></div>千里邦畿，固以镇静为第一义，但据诸处探报，鞑贼今岁入寇，蚤于常年，而窥伺淮东之意尤锐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309853_comment'></div>以形势言之，通州警则平江急，扬、泰警则江阴、常州急，真、扬警则京口急，而海道不虞之虑又不预焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309853_comment'></div>以口岸言之，则通之狼山，可以渡平江府福山，扬之柴墟，可以渡常州魏村，泰之石庄，可以渡江阴军申港，而支流泒港可以横截径渡之处又不预焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309853_comment'></div>凡此要害之区，旧虽隶沿江制司，然参以沿江制司去岁具申密院公牍，备述江防布摆之详，止谓以建康为下流，当涂为中流，池阳为上流，而京口、毗陵、平江、嘉兴、江阴五郡，无一画及之，则折柳之防，岂惟浙郡未尝措置，虽沿江制司，亦往往窘于事力之褊短，有不及措置者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309853_comment'></div>夫以积久无备之数州，而有上下数百里江海之忧责，警急之际，固未有无兵而能守者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309853_comment'></div>而臣科料所部军籍，以言乎步军，则镇江都统司元额计六万二千五百七十九人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309853_comment'></div>开禧间，胡海之变，尽招其徒为军，曰敢勇，曰精锐，曰武锋，通一万六千人，屯驻维扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309853_comment'></div>嘉定间，贾涉在淮东，镇江诸军之戍淮东诸郡者四千三十有五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309853_comment'></div>涉申闻于朝，就令移家永戍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309853_comment'></div>于是都统司之军，其去者已二万零三十五人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309853_comment'></div>续因江淮诸郡竞欲募军，朝廷又割都统司之额以与之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309853_comment'></div>扬州曰强勇军，五千六百人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309853_comment'></div>淮安州曰左右军，一万一千人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309853_comment'></div>淮阴县曰江水军，千人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309853_comment'></div>泗州曰归附义士军，一千四百二十一人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309853_comment'></div>青平山曰雄边军，一千人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309853_comment'></div>瓜洲曰防城军，一千二百四十七人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309853_comment'></div>镇江曰水军，五千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309853_comment'></div>通计三万二百六十八人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309853_comment'></div>于是都统司之军，其去者共五万三百单三人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309853_comment'></div>其在寨者，仅不过一万二千二百七十六人，而又有岁戍淮东诸郡县之军，计四千九十三人，系于在寨一万二千二百七十六人之中，选其强壮，以供征役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309853_comment'></div>于是实在寨之人才及八千馀人，而老弱者在焉，疾废者在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309853_comment'></div>诸色合千人，以至仓场库务职掌与夫军期摆铺应干差役皆在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309853_comment'></div>于是都统六军，虽曰元额六万二千五百七十九人，其实无一人可以为江南警急之备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309853_comment'></div>此步军然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309853_comment'></div>以言乎水军，仅有镇江五千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309853_comment'></div>去秋臣始上事，即加阅视，密记其人物坚壮可以出战者，极不过五百人，馀皆疲癃脆懦，纤细短弱，指一可什，决不能于惊涛巨浪之中飞戈走戟，击刺如神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309853_comment'></div>此皆三十年之积弊，既不堪战斗，又不可汰遣，惟可于江之南守寨栅、张旗帜而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309853_comment'></div>外此则许浦一军，见管一万一千五百八十六人，而戍淮东者二千二十五人，戍峡州者千人，戍鄂渚者五百人，戍金陵者千人，运淮西粮米者二千九十七人，诸杂巡逴防把差使窠役又千馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309853_comment'></div>其在寨者止二千五百四十人，而老弱疾废亦且三之一矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309853_comment'></div>如澉浦金山小军分合而计之，其在寨者通二千六百馀人，而老弱废疾亦且三之一矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309853_comment'></div>夫以三辅之郡，蔽遮行阙，而上下数百里江海之间，所恃水陆大军单虚如此，况积安久玩之厢禁卒乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309853_comment'></div>使天祐国家，虏马不至于饮江，犹之可也，万一果如叛臣宗雄武、金之才辈之虑之计，则江南之事岂不甚岌岌乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1309853_comment'></div>窃考韩世忠制置浙西，以八千之旅邀窘兀术于金焦之下，可谓以少击众，以弱御强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1309853_comment'></div>然其所将，皆西鄙劲卒，身经百战之人，而又是时蜀有吴玠、吴璘控制上流，荆湖有岳飞以必胜之军虎视河洛，加以帷幄之内，区处得宜，朝廷之上，是非不僭，人材错立，政治有章，故时世虽危，而实有善政不亡之證。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1309853_comment'></div>所以虏虽能过江，不敢以江南为可有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1309853_comment'></div>节节振起，遂成中兴。<div class='inline'
