id='poem_sentence_37_1309853_comment'></div>以今准昔，事体实难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1309853_comment'></div>而况臣之菲才，统空虚无备之数州，任上下数百里江海之忧责，岂不重可寒心也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1309853_comment'></div>区区欲望圣慈特发睿断，令本司另招万兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1309853_comment'></div>内步兵五千，专招淮人，屯戍瓜洲，外以助维扬掎角之势，内以张江面虎视之威；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1309853_comment'></div>内水军五千，专招浙人，分屯平江境内唐浦、江湾、福山，内以拱卫行都，外以弹压江海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1309853_comment'></div>臣决不效近世招军，或强驱市人，或泛募游手，徒费朝廷之钱米，无补国家之缓急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1309853_comment'></div>臣又当结以恩信，激以忠义，董以纪律，使之知有君亲，效死勿去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1309853_comment'></div>至于成败利钝，毁誉祸福，臣皆不暇计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1309853_comment'></div>触冒宸严，臣无任陨越俟命之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1309853_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_1309853'>〔贴黄〕臣窃惟理内所以制外，居重所以驭轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1309853_comment'></div>今以诸阃言之，京湖有兵二十馀万，淮西淮东各不下数万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1309853_comment'></div>只沿江制司，建康有马司戎司，又有靖安唐湾水军，又有游击军，又有制效；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1309853_comment'></div>当涂有水军五千人，雄江军五千人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1309853_comment'></div>池州有水军防江军八千人，又有戎司军；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1309853_comment'></div>江州有水军防江军数千人，又有戎司军；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1309853_comment'></div>兴国军有防江军三千人，通亦不下数万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1309853_comment'></div>浙右乃王畿之地，宗庙朝廷之所宅，而事势单绌如此，似不容不少关圣虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1309853_comment'></div>并乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_55_1309853_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年12月</a>　十二月，奏条画上流守备数事。作品：《奏条画上流守备数事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1309854' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309854' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309854?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏条画上流守备数事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1239年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309854")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309854_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309854'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309854'>臣一介庸虚，越在外服，固不应辄议朝廷大政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309854_comment'></div>然身列禁近，职预论思，苟有一得之愚，不当以疏远而自默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309854_comment'></div>窃见鞑为不道，侵突蜀江，虽督府倍道进师，京湖制臣竭力赴援，峡口近已肃静，施、黔似无疏虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309854_comment'></div>然臣窃观此贼用兵，无不取，无必取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309854_comment'></div>而无必取者，乃所以行其无不取之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309854_comment'></div>安知其目前之谋，不且并包巴蜀，占据江面上游，而迟至秋冬，方自瞿塘以下归、峡，道施、黔以窥鼎、澧，出黎、雅以瞰交、广乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309854_comment'></div>使彭大雅、陈隆之尚能立脚，则此贼犹有后顾之虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309854_comment'></div>若二帅或音问中绝，或奔迸东下，则臣之所料恐将十中七八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309854_comment'></div>今屈指日力，自一月以至七月，仅有半年，如救头然，犹惧不济，若复视以为安，则天下之事，自此恐有不可讳者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309854_comment'></div>谨条画如左，须奏闻者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309854_comment'></div>一、孟珙自其父宗政积有威惠于襄汉之间，而珙深沉宽厚，能得南北士心，又过于其父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309854_comment'></div>谓宜更加宠任，俾为京西湖南北四川宣抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309854_comment'></div>自八月以至二月，则移司公安；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309854_comment'></div>自三月以至七月，则回司鄂渚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309854_comment'></div>盖贼方有窥伺湖南之意，非并湖南北合为一司存，使任防托之责，则必致互有牴牾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309854_comment'></div>若岳阳，虽亦系上流，然处大江重湖之中，可以虎视而难于调遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309854_comment'></div>惟公安北可以应接江陵，西可以应接归、峡，当道里之中，为要冲之会，宣司驻足之地，无以易此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309854_comment'></div>仍乞朝廷多降金银钱帛，俾其得以展布。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309854_comment'></div>盖上流存则国存，上流破则国破，当倾竭事力以救之，非平时比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309854_comment'></div>一、鄂渚而上，既有所付托，其次则莫重于九江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309854_comment'></div>金陵相去千四百里，虽鞭之长，岂能及于马腹！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309854_comment'></div>谓宜仍劄沿江制置副使，于九江就兼江西安抚使，除鄂州外，凡前日副阃所隶之地，仍属焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309854_comment'></div>所有元来副司财赋，却令督府均拨付沿江京湖两司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309854_comment'></div>盖京湖既有湖南一路可以通融，则沿江副司财赋，亦可以不专仰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309854_comment'></div>九江守臣董魏宏毅忠壮，有托孤寄命之节，因加任使，决能称职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309854_comment'></div>一、天祐中国，蠢尔小夷，固决无侵越内地之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309854_comment'></div>然虑事宁过，图事宁豫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309854_comment'></div>自施而通澧，有禁山三数百里，土豪田、向二氏，世为朝廷主此山，宜优加奖录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309854_comment'></div>设有侵轶而至鼎、澧，则前有长沙之湘江；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309854_comment'></div>又设有侵轶而过长沙，则前有江西之章江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309854_comment'></div>二江虽非大江之比，然亦未易猝渡，皆当豫为防托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309854_comment'></div>一、辰、沅、靖三郡，皆有蛮人，勇捍善斗，亦宜于三郡土人中择有志之士，散入诸蛮，以恩赏结其蛮帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309854_comment'></div>若团得数千人，亦可为缓急一助之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309854_comment'></div>一、鞑之为害，犹曰外忧，而内忧之最急者，则流民是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1309854_comment'></div>去岁江东区处失宜，列郡村墟井邑，莽为焚劫之场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1309854_comment'></div>后虽不得已而招之，复忿其前过，诛杀其头目数十百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1309854_comment'></div>使今冬鞑复猖獗，则此曹又必骚动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1309854_comment'></div>若仍有团聚作过之人，岂复更可招抚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1309854_comment'></div>此腹心之大患也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1309854_comment'></div>臣以为流民与其处之江南而得所，不若处之江北得所之为愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1309854_comment'></div>今连年兵革所丧亡，饥寒所殍死，其存者盖已无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1309854_comment'></div>臣窃见安丰之六安山，联接光、舒、蕲三郡境界，周广八百里，兵法中所谓天关天牢者，此山是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1309854_comment'></div>其间生生之物及攻战之具，无所不有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1309854_comment'></div>今尚有残民万数，皆坚耐百战之馀，盘据于其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1309854_comment'></div>臣以为宜升六安县为军，择人为守，置司其内，凡光、舒、蕲附山之县皆据而属焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1309854_comment'></div>使自择令长，仍从朝廷给钱五十万缗、米五万石，使为守者举淮北流徙之民，凡属强壮，尽诱之入山，俾合为耕战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1309854_comment'></div>它日经理就绪，不惟可以壮淮西之势，塞鞑贼之冲，而又可以宽江南之扰，实为数利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1309854_comment'></div>仍乞择淮士二人，为刑狱常平使者，置司滁、和，俾任责往来，同共措置，年岁之间，必有成绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1309854_comment'></div>一、安庆府蕲州，既经残废之后，见移治沙洲，徒有州郡之名，无益于事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1309854_comment'></div>而于流民一节，多与九江、池阳两郡施行之间互有牴牾，于事体不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1309854_comment'></div>谓令九江守臣，就兼提督蕲州移治兵民公事，池阳守臣兼提督安庆府移治兵民公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1309854_comment'></div>其见屯泊之沙，则令两郡守臣就择通畅武臣一员，充各州钤辖，兼主管各州移治兵民公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1309854_comment'></div>庶几事权归一，其于处置流民，关系不小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1309854_comment'></div>一、多事之际，如湖南、福建、江东西、两浙东西，皆当团结民兵，以为缓急盗贼之备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1309854_comment'></div>然须各路委之贤明监司，庶可不扰而辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1309854_comment'></div>一、浙东、福建民船，其可用者甚多，常年以应官司者，不过具文而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1309854_comment'></div>谓宜令浙西向上监司，兼提举两路民船公事，使之自择士人，措置团结，以备缓急之须。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1309854_comment'></div>一、浙西沿江沿海一带，亡命剽悍，兴败公私之人，谓宜稍破拘挛，所属官司令作措置团结，庶几缓急之际，有调用之利，无啸聚之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1309854_comment'></div>专在任责得人，自然有益无损。</div><div id='poem_sentence_58_1309854_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年</a>　奏论平江可以为临幸之备。作品：《奏论平江可以为临幸之备》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1309855' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309855' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309855?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏论平江可以为临幸之备</a><span class='authorDate'>（1239年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309855")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309855_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309855'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309855'>窃见钱塘建都，百有馀年，以阴阳言之，全籍海门巽水，早晚两潮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309855_comment'></div>今沙涨潮塞，未必非天启国家以转移之机，大有为之会也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309855_comment'></div>况谍者所报，多云鞑贼为窥湖湘之计，万一不幸，设有疏虞，则去行都止隔袁、抚、衢、信而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309855_comment'></div>臣以为平江地势宽阔，物产富厚，他日或可为临幸之备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309855_comment'></div>盖南断长桥，阻松江，北决江湖之水，以断毗陵之路，则不患无形势；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309855_comment'></div>因三吴之饶，则不患无谷粟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309855_comment'></div>团江海亡命，则不患无兵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309855_comment'></div>而又去江上不远，可以系属人心，收召豪杰，有进之形，无退之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309855_comment'></div>欲乞试入圣抱，预作区处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309855_comment'></div>臣年来百病缠绵，心力殚竭，自度无用于世，已三上祠请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309855_comment'></div>惟是忠君爱国之忱不能自已，茍有所见，不敢顾忌讳而不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309855_comment'></div>区区无任拳拳恳切之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1309855_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
建瓯（建宁府）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8a590f708d3948a89128d70ddafb45a4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8a590f708d3948a89128d70ddafb45a4");'><span id='8a590f708d3948a89128d70ddafb45a4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1242&endYear=1242')">1242年</a>，48岁</div><div id='8a590f708d3948a89128d70ddafb45a4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1242&endYear=1242')">1242年5月</a>　五月，以台臣言夺职罢建宁府新任。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
福州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7e31dadc1cb24fe7ae24a6f1529e40df_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7e31dadc1cb24fe7ae24a6f1529e40df");'><span id='7e31dadc1cb24fe7ae24a6f1529e40df_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1248&endYear=1249')">1248-1249年</a>，54-55岁</div><div id='7e31dadc1cb24fe7ae24a6f1529e40df' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1248&endYear=1248')">1248年</a>　春日，到福州。作品：《秋七月因皇子进封忠王遵故事具奏录进旧来所得圣语乞付史馆》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1309868' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309868' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309868?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋七月因皇子进封忠王遵故事具奏录进旧来所得圣语乞付史馆<span class='inlineComment2'>（宝祐三年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1248年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309868")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309868_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309868'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309868'>臣伏见朝廷故事，每行下前宰执之家，宣索自来所得圣语，录付史馆，所以备纪载，扬休烈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309868_comment'></div>臣昨者恭睹皇帝陛下焕发神断，肇建皇储，增封王社，而皇子忠王德业日茂，令闻日章，薄海内外，莫不仰赞吾君之有子，实为社稷大庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309868_comment'></div>臣夙叨简拔，久侍清光，前后所闻玉音，关于国本之大计者颇详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309868_comment'></div>窃以为圣谟睿算，素定渊衷，蚤计预图，奠安宗社，巍巍圣功，诚非前代帝王之所能髣髴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309868_comment'></div>臣所合纪述本末，缮录家藏，以俟他时朝廷宣索。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309868_comment'></div>属臣频岁抱疴，近而转剧，深恐一旦溘先朝露，无以彰圣时之光明，谨具画一奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309868_comment'></div>欲望圣慈宣付史馆，登之琬琰，以昭示万世，与宋无极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309868_comment'></div>臣无任踊跃忭蹈之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309868_comment'></div>一、岁在丙午冬十月，臣蒙恩以兵部尚书召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309868_comment'></div>时皇子初除观察使，赐名某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309868_comment'></div>臣以十一月到阙，二十有一日蒙赐对于缉熙殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309868_comment'></div>臣第一劄子专以《复》卦为说，其间有云：「国必有副，立爱惟亲，此为陛下家之复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309868_comment'></div>得无有以迁延犹豫滞吾之复者乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309868_comment'></div>玉音云：「朕已喻卿意，此事朕意已有定属」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309868_comment'></div>臣恭聆圣训，谨寘诸心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309868_comment'></div>一、岁在丁未，臣待罪枢府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309868_comment'></div>七月初九日，同丞相郑清之、参政王伯大奏事，玉音云：「昨日有江西布衣王其姓者上书，其言诡异，颇于国本有关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309868_comment'></div>莫须稍示惩戒，以昭意向」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309868_comment'></div>臣与王伯大皆合辞赞和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309868_comment'></div>至十一月，郑清之谒告，臣与王伯大造朝，方坐漏舍，王伯大谓臣前日殿上所闻，可见主上圣谟高远，未尝顷刻忘天下大计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309868_comment'></div>吾辈何如将顺上意，因及国本正而后人心一之说，臣云甚善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309868_comment'></div>有顷奏事间，方稍稍敷陈，玉音即曰：「此事朕志已定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309868_comment'></div>但有两说，一则王夫人执谦，常有满盈之惧，犹未确许；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309868_comment'></div>二则某年方八岁，饮食起居，皆王夫人亲自看视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309868_comment'></div>若正名，须便入宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309868_comment'></div>万一起居饮食之间有失照管处，其间有多少事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309868_comment'></div>所以少迟岁月」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309868_comment'></div>臣与王伯大仰窥圣意之坚决，圣虑之深远，惟切赞诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309868_comment'></div>玉音又云：「朕以此事挂怀，兼年来国事多艰，焦劳忧虑，饮食亦自减少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309868_comment'></div>向来每日遇子午时，常宴坐移晷，收拾身心，近亦未免作辍」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309868_comment'></div>臣与王伯大奏：陛下处崇高富贵之中，而能凝神习定如此，万寿无疆，于此可卜，臣不胜叹仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309868_comment'></div>一、岁在庚戌，臣待罪政府，恭承陛下宣谕，郑清之等欲为皇子改赐嘉名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309868_comment'></div>一日玉音云：「朕欲于大字下寻一字」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309868_comment'></div>臣奏此乃老子《道德经》四大之义，蒙陛下首肯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1309868_comment'></div>臣有以仰见陛下期属皇子之意，非臣下管窥之所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1309868_comment'></div>一、岁在辛亥，臣待罪政府，闰十月二十有四日，同郑清之等奏事，恭奉玉音曰：「国本一事，朕志之定久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1309868_comment'></div>外论不察，犹多进定国本之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1309868_comment'></div>殊不知正名少迟者，盖以其年尚稚，未能便入禁中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1309868_comment'></div>况资善已建，更复何疑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1309868_comment'></div>恐缙绅间未尽知此意，卿等可以此说谕之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1309868_comment'></div>臣与同列恭领圣训而退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1309868_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1309868'>〔贴黄〕照对臣自丙午之冬，归文昌旧班，以至两登政地，迄于辛亥之冬，其闻玉音关于国本之重者，已备录在前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1309868_comment'></div>继而叨尘次辅，垂及期年，虽已窥圣意，必不出宝祐改元之后，资善志学之年，孚号正名，然为大臣之体，则惟有谨默将顺而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1309868_comment'></div>不谓萧泰来忽生异论，近又见有轮对者，复祖其说而阴煽之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1309868_comment'></div>臣窃以为陛下神谟睿烈，为社稷亿万年无疆之计，断在圣衷，岁月已久，皆非臣下一毫之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1309868_comment'></div>薄海内外之人，不论缙绅韦布，不论三军百姓，不论君子小人，向则延颈而企望，今则举手而欢欣，盖同此一心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1309868_comment'></div>而憸人邪士，乃凿空造隙，自为纷纷，以疑惑天下之听，甚无谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1309868_comment'></div>臣尝忝预宰司，休戚利害，与国同之，尤不可以不明言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1309868_comment'></div>伏乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1309868_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1248&endYear=1248')">1248年</a>　为友人梅应奇撰墓志铭。作品：《梅和甫税院墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1309917' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309917' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309917?labeling=true' target='_blank'>梅和甫税院墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳祐七年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309917")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309917_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309917'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309917'>梅为宣城著姓，国史有传者，给事中讳询，席殊宠于咸平；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309917_comment'></div>都官员外郎尧臣，扇盛名于嘉祐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309917_comment'></div>自时厥后，遗响不传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309917_comment'></div>予居是邦，尝物色其裔胄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309917_comment'></div>至绍定癸巳，护饷金陵，一日吏白有里中子梅姓者入谒，曰给事都官来昆行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309917_comment'></div>予油然喜，跃迎，则美须髯，丰下魁梧，谈天下事熟，而有大志，沈毅而善谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309917_comment'></div>遹怀前修，尚幸有后，桑梓敬心油油然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309917_comment'></div>将明试事功，则君以内艰去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309917_comment'></div>回首离逖垂十五年，百不一施，属予铭墓矣，呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309917_comment'></div>君讳应奇，字和甫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309917_comment'></div>弱冠通六艺，游乡校有隽声，试太常辄不中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309917_comment'></div>有劝以勇弁媒科第者，遂调武进校尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309917_comment'></div>再试江东转运司议事官，以边赏转承信郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309917_comment'></div>已而叹曰：吾本儒家子，何以鹖冠为哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309917_comment'></div>与其闻金鼓之声，孰若课子孙以弦诵？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309917_comment'></div>与其见干戈之扰，孰若娱宾客以豆觞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309917_comment'></div>浩然归欤，使者不能夺其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309917_comment'></div>于是渔于石港，有鱼有蟹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309917_comment'></div>田于车浦，有稻有粱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309917_comment'></div>覃及乡邻，冻者衣，馁者食，贫者赒恤，无一毫鄙吝意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309917_comment'></div>虽抱负蕴藉，迄不获伸，而幅巾杖屦，自适其适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309917_comment'></div>或忧时愤世无以寄兴，则担风而长啸，握月而浩歌，间亦假诗文以宣泄其不平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309917_comment'></div>尝曰：隐之有味哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309917_comment'></div>淳祐丙午正月乙未，以疾卒，得年若干岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309917_comment'></div>曾祖考某，妣某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309917_comment'></div>祖考某，妣某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309917_comment'></div>考某，妣某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309917_comment'></div>妻夏氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309917_comment'></div>男某，孙某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309917_comment'></div>将以明年己酉，葬于县之章务里清远石涧之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309917_comment'></div>子某等拜予而泣曰：孤不天，愿丐铭志，光贲幽壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309917_comment'></div>予论其世，奇其才，惜其不庸于时，姑志其族望岁月之大概，而系以铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1309917'>天降尔才，亦孔之厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309917_comment'></div>灌而养之，益畅以茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309917_comment'></div>而厄于期，害其不偶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1309917_comment'></div>生不有以亢厥先，死必有以鸿厥后。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1309917_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1249&endYear=1249')">1249年</a>　春罢福州。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
萧山
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='97e2bb160f844dc9a744329bb35fc96a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("97e2bb160f844dc9a744329bb35fc96a");'><span id='97e2bb160f844dc9a744329bb35fc96a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年</a>，62岁</div><div id='97e2bb160f844dc9a744329bb35fc96a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年9月1日</a>　过萧山，有诗。作品：《呈萧山知县（丙辰九月旦日，绝江扺萧山。老怀万感，偶成唐律一首呈邑大夫）》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_102990' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_102990' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/102990?labeling=true' target='_blank'>呈萧山知县<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1256年9月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_102990")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_102990_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_102990_0'>① 丙辰九月旦日，绝江抵萧山，老怀万感，偶成唐律一首呈邑大夫</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_102990'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_102990'>八年两唤浙江船，吴越青山相对妍。<div id='poem_sentence_0_102990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_102990'>长愧主恩难报答，不知人事几推迁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_102990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_102990'>香浮菊桂秋将暮，景迫桑榆岁可怜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_102990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_102990'>荒县今宵孤馆梦，四千里外楚云边。<div id='poem_sentence_3_102990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_102990'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_102990_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
宁波
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='798169d0c0af46adb552074e54c29e38_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("798169d0c0af46adb552074e54c29e38");'><span id='798169d0c0af46adb552074e54c29e38_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1259')">1256-1259年</a>，62-65岁</div><div id='798169d0c0af46adb552074e54c29e38' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年9月9日</a>　季秋到任，条奏有关国防、民政措施。作品：《奏行周燮义船之策以革防江民船之弊乞补本人文资以任责》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1309869' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309869' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309869?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏行周燮义船之策以革防江民船之弊乞补本人文资以任责<span class='inlineComment2'>（宝祐四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1256年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309869")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309869_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309869'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309869'>臣窃见朝廷自端平初，团结温台民船为十番，岁发一百四十只，前往镇江府，防拓江面，已二纪于此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309869_comment'></div>其始团结，固有定籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309869_comment'></div>岁月既久，元籍之舟，有坏于风水之飘没者，有陷于资贼之劫掳者，有家道贫乏无力脩葺而朽弊者，有转以售人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309869_comment'></div>有司但以旧额拘船，祖以及父，父以及子，子以及孙，逼令出备，不至于破家绝产流离死亡不已，其强悍者则未免转徙而为盗贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309869_comment'></div>迨至每岁发船，则县道召人，纠举白船，以补欠阙之数，又乘此以为骚扰乞取之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309869_comment'></div>凡邑之有舟者，不问大小，例皆根刷，有势者不敢问，有力者不敢问，有钱计会者不复问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309869_comment'></div>迨溪壑之欲既厌，然后姑以敝旧之舟、疏略之杠具、孱弱之稍火，文具塞责而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309869_comment'></div>间遇江淮制司拨上项舟船，载出戍军士以至上流，或般运粮饷，以弊舟弊人溯流犯险，则往往人船俱坏，死为客鬼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309869_comment'></div>于是庆元、温、台三郡边海之民，陆者不得安于陆，渔者不得安于渔，以起发隘船为一大阱，生者怨气充腹，死者冤气干霄，臣实伤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309869_comment'></div>始至，即行博询可行可久之策于知识之士，有台州漕贡进士周燮者，首以义船之策献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309869_comment'></div>其法以一县当出之舟若干只，分乡都之广狭，令凡有舟之家，以大小丈尺，均出钱物，置备舟只，以应每岁当发之额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309869_comment'></div>其有舟而止及七八尺以下者，不在纠率之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309869_comment'></div>且不待官司之文移，至期则合从应调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309869_comment'></div>船必坚牢，杠具必整齐，人丁必强壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309869_comment'></div>而燮又肯以身任责，以家助公，集事于指顾之间，而人不知扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309869_comment'></div>如温如庆元，皆以是为准，去秋调发，已见实效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309869_comment'></div>遂使沿海方二三千里有舟之民，得以安生乐业，无畴昔追呼烦扰困害愁叹之状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309869_comment'></div>其于肃清海道，消弭寇贼，此实为一义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309869_comment'></div>臣窃照得周燮疏财好义，识变知机，以孝悌称于闺门，以信行闻于里党，故能移忠于国家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309869_comment'></div>比其乡失伍犯上之徒，久稽邦宪，委燮逮捕，不动声色，剋期集事，亦可谓之才矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309869_comment'></div>燮自请寓试文解，已该四举，使其不第，以恩得官，亦不失一初品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309869_comment'></div>今来本司历试繁难，备著劳绩，若蒙朝廷特加旌异，缓急用之，必有卓然可观者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309869_comment'></div>欲乞圣慈补授周燮文资初阶，或与上州文学，实为赴功趋事者之劝。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1309869_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年</a>　条奏有关国防、民政措施。作品：《奏晓谕海寇复为良民及关防海道事宜》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷三。）</span>《奏禁私置团场以培植本根消弭盗贼》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷三。）</span>《奏论海道内外二洋利害去处防贵周密》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1309870' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309870' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309870?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏晓谕海寇复为良民及关防海道事宜</a><span class='authorDate'>（1256年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309870")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309870_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309870'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309870'>臣恭承知省卢允升传奏圣旨，宣谕：海道为今日急务，宜意外关防，以副朕意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309870_comment'></div>臣有以仰见陛下虑周四表，思患预防之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309870_comment'></div>臣所当竭尽驽力，上图报称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309870_comment'></div>但臣窃惟中外之所过忧者，鞑与李松寿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309870_comment'></div>然臣以为若内寇不作，则决不至于招引外寇，故今日海道之所急者，消弭内寇而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309870_comment'></div>于是臣于始至之时，即出榜晓谕海寇，改过自新，复为良民，以柔服其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309870_comment'></div>又自来犯盗之人，制司不问轻重，例是抄籍，以助支遣，于是臣复出榜晓谕，为盗之人，父母妻子未必一一知情，若一人犯罪，一家失业，深可悯念，应日后犯盗之人，并免抄籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309870_comment'></div>盖盗贼亦人耳，谁无父母妻子室家骨肉之念？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309870_comment'></div>臣又以此感动其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309870_comment'></div>又盗贼之发，惟重赏可以收捕，于是臣优立赏格，并行榜谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309870_comment'></div>盗贼知官司赏格之醲，必不能漏网，自然有所忌惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309870_comment'></div>臣又以此畏慑其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309870_comment'></div>所以前乎守臣，凌迟斩绞无虚日，而盗不止，臣领事数月，并无一尘之惊，不特臣平生仕宦所至，仰凭陛下威德，粗得人和，虽盗贼亦知信服，然亦藉微术以羁縻笼络之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309870_comment'></div>然臣又以为欲消弭内寇，必须先固结自家军民之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309870_comment'></div>于是臣考核郡计，见得本府以财赋窘乏，自来催理二税，至于四年八月，臣即痛与蠲放，为钱三百三十馀万贯文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309870_comment'></div>累政以来，交头钱物，多系积年公吏等人，负欠摊赖之钱，指为实在，以充数目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309870_comment'></div>臣始至之初，累累监欠者不下数百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309870_comment'></div>臣并与蠲放，却以本任趱积到钱物为前政补填虚数，然后外而田里，内而城市，莫不欢呼鼓舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309870_comment'></div>又此邦每岁起民船把隘，本不过一二百只，常苦于县吏作弊，科差不均，有船者倖免，无船者被抑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309870_comment'></div>遇每岁一番起发，则沿海之民，鸡犬为之一空，破家荡产，典妻卖子，比比而是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309870_comment'></div>臣遂创为义役，令各都各保均钱备船，每遇秋时，自此结集，资次赴官司把隘，听候差拨，更不出一文引，亦不差一吏卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309870_comment'></div>见此成立规模，以为此邦无穷之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309870_comment'></div>于是沿海百姓方知有生之乐，亦莫不欢呼鼓舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309870_comment'></div>又军者国之爪牙，本府所管定海水军，制领将佐而下，每月例有添给钱，禁军头目合千人，每月例有盐菜钱，皆以库藏枵虚，久已住支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309870_comment'></div>臣并与帮放，岁为钱九万七千馀贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309870_comment'></div>又定海水军出巡把港，警捕盗贼，皆经涉鲸波，自来并无生券。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309870_comment'></div>臣并与照诸处大军例，令支每日口券钱米，每岁约用钱三万六千二百八十馀贯，米二千八百二十二石四斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309870_comment'></div>又本府厢禁军，不下二三千人，率苦贫乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309870_comment'></div>臣于是每遇死亡，禁军给钱三十贯，厢军给钱二十贯，然后内外军伍，莫不欢呼鼓舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309870_comment'></div>又定海水军元额六千人，一向缘郡帑不支，阙额常近千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309870_comment'></div>臣见此措置军装等下钱，先招五百人选士，以壮军声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309870_comment'></div>军民之心既固，军旅之势渐张，盗贼之衅不作，则虽有外寇，且不能窥吾国之藩篱，何缘能入吾国之堂奥！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309870_comment'></div>此臣报陛下之职分也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309870_comment'></div>然海道之事，亦实有不必深虑者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1309870_comment'></div>臣不惟得于更历，亦自得于解悟，敢毕陈之，以上宽圣抱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1309870_comment'></div>大抵守江海与守两淮荆蜀不同，守两淮荆蜀全以人，守江海则半以天，半以人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1309870_comment'></div>何以言之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1309870_comment'></div>两淮荆蜀战在平陆之地，守在城池之间，必须强兵猛将，始可御敌，故曰专属人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1309870_comment'></div>若守江海，则异是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1309870_comment'></div>敌纵有千艘万舰，欲行侵犯，一才起柁，便为风水所使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1309870_comment'></div>所谓千艘万舰，风迅水疾，飘泊东西，无缘会成䑸合伴，并力向前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1309870_comment'></div>吾国不过得死士三千人，坚牢战船数十只，据要害敌所必经之地，一舟过则杀一舟，自可使之只轮不返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1309870_comment'></div>况鲸波万里，又有不测之风飓乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1309870_comment'></div>此臣所谓不必深虑者一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1309870_comment'></div>今高丽虽臣属于鞑，然每有疑畏鞑贼之心，迁都海岛，防其侵犯，决不至为鞑向导，纵使有窥中国之意，然无松杉木可以造船。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1309870_comment'></div>其国虽有船只，止是杂木，亦无钉铁，只可在其国近境往来卖买，岂能远涉鲸海！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1309870_comment'></div>纵曰李松寿在海州，所当防备，然北方平原万里，素亦不产松杉，其船不过用杨柳木打造，江且难涉，况于航海！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1309870_comment'></div>所以二十年来，未尝不传李松寿在海州造船，厚以银两，招南方水手，元不见其一毫动息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1309870_comment'></div>况吾国之新海州又瞰其旁，保无他虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1309870_comment'></div>昔辛巳逆亮犯顺，固尝航海，为李宝所败而遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1309870_comment'></div>是时亦止在海州之唐岛获捷，初未尝及吾二浙之海面也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1309870_comment'></div>此臣所谓不必深虑者二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1309870_comment'></div>臣空臆尽言，冒渎圣听，罪当万死，伏乞睿照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1309870_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_53_1309870'>〔贴黄〕臣既以海道事宜仰渎圣听，但有一事粗当防者，臣不敢隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1309870_comment'></div>此间舶船，常有贩高丽者，大率甲番三只到丽国，必乙番三只回归，丙丁亦如之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1309870_comment'></div>今庆元人见有在彼国仕宦者，却缘此等船只皆属朝廷分司，制司不可得而察其往来之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1309870_comment'></div>此间之舟一只，可以载二三百人，万一彼有异志，并吾甲乙两番之舟，并行拘夺，以渡鞑贼，则亦意外之过虑也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1309870_comment'></div>故臣以为若朝廷以舶务拨隶沿海制司，却择一收钱最高年分，责令制司抱解净钱，则于国课无亏，而发舶事权属之制司，可以操持考察，其所关事体颇为不细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1309870_comment'></div>况缓急之际，亦可团结大舟，为国家后户之备，此其为计，又在不言之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1309870_comment'></div>兼亦可以因发舶舟，令晓畅之人伪为商旅，至彼国审探鞑贼事宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1309870_comment'></div>等而上之，又有无穷利便，难以尽述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1309870_comment'></div>但此事臣不敢言，恐或者以为与朝廷争利，惟乞陛下自取决于圣衷而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1309870_comment'></div>今有《丽鞑本末》一册，并用缴进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1309870_comment'></div>伏乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_63_1309870_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1309871' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309871' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309871?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏禁私置团场以培植本根消弭盗贼</a><span class='authorDate'>（1256年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309871")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309871_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309871'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309871'>臣祗被宸命，代匮瀛阃，责以肃清海道之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309871_comment'></div>臣窃谓清海道莫先于安百姓，安百姓莫先于遂生理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309871_comment'></div>照得本府管下鲒埼镇倚山濒海，居民环镇者数千家，无田可耕，居廛者则懋迁有无，株守店肆，习海者则冲冒波涛，蝇营网罟，生齿颇多，烟火相望，而并海数百里之人，凡有负贩者皆趋焉，图志谓之小江下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309871_comment'></div>自古官司不置税场，正欲留此利源，养赡不耕不蚕之民，使之衣食稍给，则非心妄念不作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309871_comment'></div>比年以来，形势之家私置团场，尽网其利，民不聊生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309871_comment'></div>其间不得已者，未免沦而为盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309871_comment'></div>近幸势家自行住罢团局，听令民间自营生业，小民方有生意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309871_comment'></div>但一方奸猾之徒垂涎未已，或恐妄行投献府第，借声势以残民，创砂岸以龙断，使小民衣食之源得而复失，委关利害，所合敷奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309871_comment'></div>欲望圣慈降付尚书省，劄下本府，永行禁断，刊之于石，以垂不朽，实为培植本根、消弭盗贼之第一义。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1309871_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1309872' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309872' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309872?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏论海道内外二洋利害去处防贵周密<span class='inlineComment2'>（宝祐四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1256年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309872")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309872_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309872'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309872'>窃见朝廷近日措置，自东海县以至澉浦，分为二屯，以防里洋之寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309872_comment'></div>又令沿海制司，起发温、台、明系籍民船，摆布岑江等处，以防外洋之寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309872_comment'></div>其说不为不详，然尚有未尽之蕴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309872_comment'></div>照得新旧海州凡发兵船，欲入海道，其水路有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309872_comment'></div>贼若欲侵扰淮东，则自旧海发舟，直入赣口杨家寨盐城，此里洋也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309872_comment'></div>若欲送死浙江，则自旧海放舟，直出大洋，缘赣口之东社、苗沙、野沙、外沙、姚刘沙，以至徘徊头、金小澉浦，此外洋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309872_comment'></div>以上二洋，皆属淮东浙西之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309872_comment'></div>然贼舟若欲放此二洋，其源头皆须经由新海界分东陬山、西陬山之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309872_comment'></div>今来戍海诸部士卒，其脱身者多聚于东陬山，势须就两山审度，择宽平去处，创筑城垒，如淮阃之筑荆山，指顾而期，尽吾事力，创屯重兵，以防制之于未入吾境之先，则畿甸可以奠枕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309872_comment'></div>若俟其犯吾之三屯，则贼已入腹心矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309872_comment'></div>此当亟令淮阃措置者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309872_comment'></div>若更欲向里做一二层工夫，则赣口之东，诸沙累易，外洋去处，亦有可以聚船屯兵之地，此又当亟令淮阃措置者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309872_comment'></div>若淮阃以积久之威名，再图收复新海，则前二说，却自可缓，特不容不过计而预谋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309872_comment'></div>但收复旧海之策，或谓当以计困，未可以力取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309872_comment'></div>其说曰：新海眇在海中，我之据新海也，自淮安运粮，由淮河出赣口，沿沙岸直上，经从东陬山、西陬山之中，以达于旧海，其势稍便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309872_comment'></div>贼若据新海，则必自旧海运粮以往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309872_comment'></div>我若以数百舟横截石湫河之口，虎视新海，则贼运粮之舟，无缘可过以达于新海，纵不攻击，彼将绝粮自溃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309872_comment'></div>此又淮阃所当参刍荛之言，为万全之胜者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309872_comment'></div>若贼欲送死四明，则自旧海放舟，由东陬山之外望东行，便相转而南，则可直达昌国县之石㣚关岙，然后经岑海、岱山、三姑之境以至定海，又稍转而西，则可至金山澉浦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309872_comment'></div>此其势若易而实难，盖此路之不通已久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309872_comment'></div>然使东陬山有可守之城壁，可恃之重兵，则贼亦有后顾之虞，亦决未敢冒然瞢进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309872_comment'></div>若曰自登莱放舟，径至大七蛇山，以至澉浦，则此路虽南人皆所不谙，况北人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309872_comment'></div>犹记政和中，与女真结海上之盟，系自山东陆路至登州，与之约要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309872_comment'></div>盖女真每自辽东海道贩马至登州故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309872_comment'></div>使此间海舟径可至登州，登州海舟竟可至此间，则政和结约，必自此取道泛海而至登矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309872_comment'></div>后中原为虏所有，朝廷尝遣使至高丽，欲借路至登莱，以至女真之庭，丽主不从而回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309872_comment'></div>以此知此路之素隔，特不可不多为之备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309872_comment'></div>闻沿海制司去岁新创军屯于向头，以水军百五十人、土军一百人，分为两寨，与金山相为唇齿，已京师一重后户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309872_comment'></div>更乞行下沿海制司，于大小七山蛇山等处，以兵船常切探望，多立烽燧，如前来白劄子事理施行，庶几海道愈为周密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309872_comment'></div>伏乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1309872_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年</a>　创建厢院，以居讼民两造未备无亲故作保者。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年</a>　初到庆元，秋冬有诗作。作品：《登镇海楼》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷九。）</span>《对黄花》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷九。）</span>《分定》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷九。）</span>《自叹》2首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷九。）</span>《岁晏无聊收叔氏讯》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷九。）</span>《喜雪》2首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷九。）</span>《再赋喜雪》2首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_103061' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103061' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103061?labeling=true' target='_blank'>登镇海楼</a><span class='authorDate'>（1256年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103061")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_103061_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103061'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103061'>鄮山深处古明州，新有江南客倚楼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103061'>凤阙天连便望日，蛟门海晏不惊秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103061'>头颅已迫残年景，身口聊为卒岁谋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103061'>萧飒西风吹败叶，满眶清泪自难收。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103061'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_103061_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_103078' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103078' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103078?labeling=true' target='_blank'>对黄花</a><span class='authorDate'>（1256年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103078")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_103078_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103078'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103078'>当年脱却戏衫回，又被官差唤出来。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103078_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103078'>疾恶念轻缘练历，好名心懒为衰摧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103078_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103078'>莫愁白发家千里，且对黄花酒一杯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103078_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103078'>信美江山非我土，倚空凝伫更徘徊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103078_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103078'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_103078_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_103071' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103071' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103071?labeling=true' "poem_title_103071")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_103071_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103071'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103071'>丁年曾授此东州，恳恳笺天得罢休。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103071'>七上八下忽九闰，十洲三岛终一游。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103071'>人言官贵体当重，自笑儿痴病未瘳。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103071'>只为君恩深莫报，明年春尽得归不。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103071'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_103071_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_102982' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_102982' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/102982?labeling=true' target='_blank'>岁晏无聊收叔氏讯</a><span class='authorDate'>（1256年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_102982")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_102982_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_102982'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_102982'>豢成凋郡力难任，雪上加霜两鬓侵。<div id='poem_sentence_0_102982_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_102982'>四五更头猿鹤梦，数千里外鹡鸰心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_102982_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_102982'>老来倍觉光阴促，休去方知意味深<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：休去，禅家话。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_102982_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_102982'>陶白邵诗消遣具，晚窗无事且微吟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_102982_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_102982'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_102982_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_102980' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_102980' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/102980?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再赋喜雪二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1256年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_102980")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_102980_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_102980'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_102980'>黑风剪水作瑰琦，散落人閒贱似泥。<div id='poem_sentence_0_102980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_102980'>万象直教还朴素，千岐何幸尽平夷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_102980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_102980'>征人奔路昏投店，戍士乘城夜守陴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_102980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_102980'>不识艰难惟党二，销金帐底饮羔儿。<div id='poem_sentence_3_102980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_102980'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_102980_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_102979' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_102979' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/102979?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1256年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_102979_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_102979'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_102979'>夜深如水泼衣衾，晓看皑皑冒碧岑。<div id='poem_sentence_0_102979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_102979'>以洁藏污窥物理，由仁行义见天心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_102979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_102979'>但教南亩多呈瑞，何必东夷屡献琛。<div id='poem_sentence_2_102979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_102979'>麦熟吾时归印绶，不能者止念周任。<div id='poem_sentence_3_102979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_102979'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_102979_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年10月10日</a>　十月十日，有词。作品：《沁园春·丙辰十月十日》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一一。）</span><div id='poem_103163' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103163' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103163?labeling=true' target='_blank'>沁园春<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>丙辰十月十日</a><span class='authorDate'>（1256年10月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103163")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103163_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103163'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103163'>夜雨三更，有人欹枕，晓檐报晴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103163'>算顽云痴雾，不难扫荡，青天白日，元自分明。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103163'>权植油幢，聊张皂纛，坐听前驺鼓角鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103163'>君休诧，岂宣申南翰，成旦东征。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103163_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103163'>鸿冥。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103163'>哽噎秋声。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103163'>正万里榆关未罢兵。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103163'>幸扬州上督，为吾石友，荆州元帅，是我梅兄。<div id='poem_sentence_7_103163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_103163'>约束鲸鲵，奠安鼪鼠，更使嵎夷海晏清。<div id='poem_sentence_8_103163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_103163'>连宵看，怕天狼隐耀，太白沉枪。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_103163_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年1月</a>　兄渊除参知政事后数日，有词寿之。作品：《贺新凉·丁巳岁寿叔氏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一一。）</span><div id='poem_103205' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103205' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103205?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺新郎<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>丁巳岁寿叔氏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103205")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103205_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103205'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103205'>未是全衰暮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103205_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103205'>但相思、昭亭数曲，水村烟墅。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103205_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103205'>只比儿儿额上寿，尚有时光如许。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103205_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103205'>况坎子、常交离午。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103205_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103205'>须信火龙能陆战，更驱他、水虎蟠沧浦。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103205_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103205'>昆崙顶，时飞度。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103205_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103205'>东皇蓦向昆崙遇。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103205_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103205'>道如今、金阶玉陛，待卿阔步。<div id='poem_sentence_7_103205_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_103205'>犹恐荆人攀恋切，未放征帆高举。<div id='poem_sentence_8_103205_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_103205'>怕公去、狐狸嗥舞。<div id='poem_sentence_9_103205_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_103205'>江汉一诗谁作者，想声声、赞祝明良聚。<div id='poem_sentence_10_103205_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_103205'>天下久，望霖雨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_103205_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年</a>　创建广惠院。作品：《奏创养济院以存养鳏寡孤独之民》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1309874' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309874' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309874?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏创养济院以存养鳏寡孤独之民</a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309874")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309874_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309874'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309874'>臣窃见四明为浙左壮郡，生齿最繁，素无养济院，以存养鳏寡孤独之民，委为阙典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309874_comment'></div>臣尝备数□辅，每见陛下轸念黎元之意，与天地同其仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309874_comment'></div>今兹叨守近畿，所当求所以上称明旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309874_comment'></div>近因省并都酒务一所，就行增添屋宇，改创房屋，共为七十馀间，收养鳏寡孤独之民二百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309874_comment'></div>大口月支米六斗、钱十五贯，中口月支米五斗、钱十贯，小口月支米四斗、钱七贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309874_comment'></div>已于天基圣节之日，令入院居住养济，无非所以推广上恩，祝延睿算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309874_comment'></div>其岁用米约二千馀石，钱约六万馀贯，并于本府自行措置，上于朝廷系省钱无预，下于本府经常钱无关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309874_comment'></div>但止就本府自来有管淘湖米内分拨一千石，贴助支遣，所合专具奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309874_comment'></div>欲望圣慈降付尚书省，给降省劄，付本府永远遵守，实为千里无穷之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309874_comment'></div>伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1309874_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年</a>　奏给遭风倭商钱米。作品：《奏给遭风倭商钱米以广朝廷柔远之恩亦于海防密有关系》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1309873' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309873' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309873?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏给遭风倭商钱米以广朝廷柔远之恩亦于海防密有关系</a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309873")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309873_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309873'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309873'>臣窃惟自中兴南渡，声教与西北罕接，惟丽、倭二国，介于东南海隅，犹知向慕本朝，至今通商。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309873_comment'></div>但自来倭人间有失舟者，财本陷没，续食无计，虽寄口腹于牙人之家，率为牙人多算火帐，其失舟之倭则假贷于不失舟之倭以偿之，未免重困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309873_comment'></div>又有高丽境内船只，忽遇恶风，时亦飘至台、温、福建、庆元界分，万里流落，尤为可念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309873_comment'></div>臣两岁之间，一再见之，遂从有司每名日给白米二升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309873_comment'></div>其倭人则俟同䑸船只之回载与同归，丽人则俟此间商人入丽，优给钱米，使归其国，无非所以广朝廷之仁心仁闻于远人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309873_comment'></div>但自本司行之，终恐难继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309873_comment'></div>此来欲望朝廷行下市舶司，立为定例，遇有倭商不测遭风水之人，从舶务日支十七界一贯五百文，本司日支米二升养膳，候归国日住支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309873_comment'></div>仍行下浙东西福建诸州，遇有丽人飘流至各州界内，即仰各州支给钱米，发至本司，仍从舶司日支十七界一贯五百文，本司日支米二升存养，亦候归国日住支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309873_comment'></div>庶几远人皆知朝廷柔远之恩，亦于海道之防密有关系。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1309873_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年</a>　条奏海道备御六事。作品：《条奏海道备御六事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1309876' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309876' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309876?labeling=true' target='_blank'>条奏海道备御六事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309876")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309876_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309876'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309876'>一、绍兴初创立水军，屯驻定海，专为行都后户之防，未尝轻调一兵远戍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309876_comment'></div>自嘉熙年间，督府始行下调遣，前赴上流差使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309876_comment'></div>适统制林炜系督府旧校，勇于奔命，更不申闻制司，具申朝廷及督府免调，自是遂以为例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309876_comment'></div>至淳祐九年，统制纪智春备述利害，申告本司，本司备申朝廷，蒙从申免行出戍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309876_comment'></div>当年遂擒捕到积年大䑸海寇数百人，赶逐倭船出境，捕获铜钱二万馀贯，实得全军在寨之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309876_comment'></div>宝祐初，当国者不知东南事体，科降官钱，令本军造平底船，差军士四百人，驾往海州，就行捍御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309876_comment'></div>又准起发把隘民船一十五只，并往海州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309876_comment'></div>除民船梢工梢首共计三十人外，又令本军起差军士四百七十人，驾放上项船只。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309876_comment'></div>是为两戍通差官兵八百七十人，每遇更戍之时，又须别差八百七十人，或遵陆，或航海，前往抵替，方得前项戍军回司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309876_comment'></div>是一岁之间，常是一千七百四十人往来道涂，无休息之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309876_comment'></div>又宝祐元年八月，准密劄差官兵三百五十人，同民兵一百五十人，驾民船三十二只，往料角屯戍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309876_comment'></div>切照料角者，乃通州料家沙之角，民旅船只自扬子江口入海，不欲经涉大洋风涛之险，是以沿趁老岸，寻觅洪道，潮长则进，潮退则止，迂回转折，不计日程，以达于淮海，非防大敌之要害也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309876_comment'></div>徒辍国家门户之防，而置之无用之地，尤为无谓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309876_comment'></div>总三项而计之，是定海之军岁减二千九十人之实力矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309876_comment'></div>此军元额止六千人，自来四千人系庆元府通判厅、经总制司管认券钱，二千人系庆元府管给券钱，而米则尽系庆元府给饷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309876_comment'></div>近来缘郡计凋弊，而经总制司财赋亦复失陷，阙额常数百人，则所管之兵止五千人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309876_comment'></div>老弱疾患又居十分之一，则实可用之兵四千五百人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309876_comment'></div>而二千九十人之往来征戍于淮者，又皆选士，则其在寨者仅二千四百馀人之常卒而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309876_comment'></div>修备戎器，打造战船，收买军需，防守寨栅库务，率不下三四百人，则在寨之数仅仅二千馀人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309876_comment'></div>而又往年以州兵之鬨，移屯于郡者五百人，以盗贼之炽，分屯于东门者五百人，则定海本寨又仅仅千馀人尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309876_comment'></div>若海道之责，则西接许浦，南接福建，北接高丽，东接日本，广袤且踰万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309876_comment'></div>探望以舟师，巡逴以舟师，把守诸处隘口以舟师，又欲常整备三五百人，以为缓急不测之用，于是定海它无一卒可调矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309876_comment'></div>使幸而出一尘之警，尚可牵补驾漏，以过时日，每一长虑却顾，实为之寒心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309876_comment'></div>况许浦水军，顾管一万二千人，其任责止于扬子江口，北极如通泰、如料角，正与许浦相直，乃其地分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309876_comment'></div>不以许浦之军屯戍，而乃以定海之军屯戍，良由许浦以都统之重，可上告朝廷，而定海不过偏军下垒，情愬不能自达，前后制臣又无有为之申陈者，所以陵夷至此极也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309876_comment'></div>某虽见极力措办钱粮及备等下钱并七事件军装，一面招补阙额，然非仓卒之所能办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309876_comment'></div>欲望朝廷将近年创例出戍淮海两项戍兵免行调发，庶几本军兵力稍全，可以遵照朝廷指挥措置关防，不至疏虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309876_comment'></div>又其最可念者，海滨之人与北方风土不宜，至则疾病交作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309876_comment'></div>宝祐三年分徐欢所部四百人，亡殁一百一十六人，钟晟所部四百七十人，亡殁一百一人，加以数年，将尽为异乡之鬼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309876_comment'></div>又自宝祐元年调遣，以至四年，损失军器共计七千九百馀件。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309876_comment'></div>久戍之船，本军每岁又自差官前往修葺，四年之内，已用过钱一十三万八千二百馀贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309876_comment'></div>加以数年，此军亦将赤立，不复可支吾矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309876_comment'></div>臣窃惟两淮知院知府，威声震于沙漠，勋烈炳于丹青，黄头郎如林，下濑船如云，决不欠此千百人之弱卒、十数只之民艘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309876_comment'></div>若以此一千二百二十人之生券，自每岁为新会三万八千八百六十二贯文，为米九千六百三十石，到戍回戍，行府犒赐优厚，共为钱约新会二万贯，本司每岁遣戍，亦该新会一万贯，是统为新会六万八千六十二贯文矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1309876_comment'></div>以上项钱米就淮东招募一千二百二十人，并作上等效用，岁不过欠新会六万五千八百九十八贯，欠米三千七百六十二石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1309876_comment'></div>朝廷决不较此琐琐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1309876_comment'></div>使行府不失调兵之名，使本司不失见兵之实，其于内外边防，均为幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1309876_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_1309876'>一、防江海之险，与防平陆之险不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1309876_comment'></div>防平陆之险，专以人力；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1309876_comment'></div>防江海之险，专以人谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1309876_comment'></div>盖贼虽有千船万樯，才一开岸，即为风水所使，散漫四出，决不能成䑸合伴，并力于我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1309876_comment'></div>我但得精卒三千人，坚好之舟三十只，屯泊于贼所必经之地，一舟过即杀一舟，自可使之无复遗类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1309876_comment'></div>此机六韬三略之所不载，而前史往牒之所未详也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1309876_comment'></div>臣窃惟自中兴南渡，立国钱塘，所以创许浦水军于平江，创澉浦水军于嘉兴，创定海水军于庆元府，无非为京师左右前后门户之防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1309876_comment'></div>但许浦枕扬子江而置司，去京师为远，惟澉浦去京师为近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1309876_comment'></div>而不知澉浦之外，又有所谓金山，乃应干舟楫所必经往稍泊之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1309876_comment'></div>臣二纪之前假守嘉兴，适逆全有窥海之意，臣遂具申朝廷，创招水军千人于金山，又为澉浦之外拓，至今人以为宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1309876_comment'></div>今定海水军虽得控扼之地，然于防制倭丽则有馀，而于遮护京师则不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1309876_comment'></div>若曰山东之贼欲送死鲸波，则自胶西放洋，绕淮东料角诸沙之外，自有径截洪道，直达前所谓嘉兴之金山，不必更放大洋不测之渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1309876_comment'></div>臣今体访定海之里，有地名曰向头，至钱塘江只一潮汛，乃应干舟楫所必经从上潬之处，与嘉兴之金山无以异，而形势则过之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1309876_comment'></div>且有地可以建寨，有山可以藏舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1309876_comment'></div>臣欲招刺阙额水军五百人，人人必皆选士，就彼屯驻，设有缓急，则增兵占守，可以万举万全，而京师有金汤之固矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1309876_comment'></div>昔高庙朝，御史中丞沈与求尝奏云：「议者皆欲于向头置屯，使贼至此，已是入吾腹心之地」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1309876_comment'></div>盖是时登、莱、海、密尚与本朝相关，而高丽亦羁縻未绝，故或者犹有不肯厌安江沱之意，而与求之论所以欲向外下江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1309876_comment'></div>方今时异势殊，臣所以举此一节者，欲以證向头置屯，先朝诸臣固尝言之，非臣之茍言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1309876_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_55_1309876'>一、庆元府诸邑惟昌国、象山、定海枕海而处，奉化亦半之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1309876_comment'></div>沿海之人，多恶少亡命，以渔盐为业，大率剽悍轻捷，在水如龙，非官军比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1309876_comment'></div>浙之东西以及福建，凡并海而生者，虽无非习熟波涛之夫，独以庆元人为称首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1309876_comment'></div>凡贩海者以百人为率，庆元之人仅著十分之二三，盖恐其多则能并杀其徒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1309876_comment'></div>此可见此邦沿海之民，最悍而最可用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1309876_comment'></div>臣顷奏闻兴复砂岸，以六家上户之世业复归而还之，最令照右例输纳官租，正欲为团结之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1309876_comment'></div>今官司岁收不过十七界十四五万贯文，臣今欲仍弛以予之，却令当土大家随其地分及砂岸广狭事力，共团结强壮三千人，仍与各办衣装器械。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1309876_comment'></div>大略如往年两淮、近年沿江团结民兵之法，置立头目，部勒队伍，遇秋时渔田之业隙，则以千人合教于郡，三岁周而复始，盖一举而有三利焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1309876_comment'></div>缓急之际，此三千人可以当三万人之用，一利也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1309876_comment'></div>既就团结，则姓名皆在官司，为盗贼者不可容，贩私盐者亦可戢，此二利也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1309876_comment'></div>三利：大家上户，既永免砂岸纳钱，其利无穷，且永无寇攘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1309876_comment'></div>如近时三山小榭焚掠之虞，特不过一番置办军装器械之费，实系以合纳官钱而办官事，固其所乐从而喜听者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1309876_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_67_1309876'>一、本司自嘉熙年间准朝廷指挥，团结温、台、庆元三郡民船数千只，分为十番，岁起船三百馀只，前来定海把隘，及分拨前去淮东镇江戍守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1309876_comment'></div>夫以百姓营生之舟，而拘之使从征役，已非人情之所乐，使行之以公，加之以不扰，则民犹未为大害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1309876_comment'></div>奈何所在邑宰，非贪即昏，受成吏手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1309876_comment'></div>各县有所谓海船案者，恣行卖弄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1309876_comment'></div>其家地富厚真有巨艘者，非以赂嘱省吏隐免，则假借形势之家拘占，惟贫而无力者，则被科调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1309876_comment'></div>其二十年前已籍之船，或以遭风而损失，或以被盗而陷没，或以无力修葺而底沉，或以船身老朽而弊坏，往往不与销籍，岁岁追呼，以致典田卖产，货妻鬻子，以应官司之命，甚则损弃乡井而逃，自经沟渎而死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1309876_comment'></div>其无赖者，则流为海寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1309876_comment'></div>每岁遇夏初，则海船案已行检举，不论大船小船，有船无船，并行根括一次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1309876_comment'></div>文移遍于村落，乞取竭于鸡犬，环三郡二三千里之海隅，民不堪命，日不聊生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1309876_comment'></div>待至起到舟只，则大抵旧弊破漏，不及丈尺，杠具则疏略，稍火则脆弱，亦姑以具文塞责而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1309876_comment'></div>民被实害，官无实用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1309876_comment'></div>且天险之防，以人心为本，先使百姓憔悴，根本动摇，脱有缓急，何恃而亡恐！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1309876_comment'></div>臣已结为义船法，谓如一都每岁合发三舟，而有船者五六十家，则令五六十家自以事力厚薄，办船六只，船身必坚耐，杠具必齐整，稍火必强壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1309876_comment'></div>岁发三舟，而以三舟在家营生，一岁所得之息，则以充次年之船办杠具、招稍火之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1309876_comment'></div>立以程限，守以信必，岁岁遇当把隘之日，则如期驾发，以至军港，听候调遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1309876_comment'></div>于是有船者无倖免之理，无船者无科抑之患，永绝奸胥猾吏卖弄乞觅之苦，永销滨海居民破家荡产之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1309876_comment'></div>人心固则天险固，三郡边海之人，莫不欣然听从，事将就绪，实为海道无穷之利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1309876_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_84_1309876'>一、此邦沿海凡有寨口，大嵩管界海内白峰、岱山、三姑、岑江、螺头，计土军一千四百八十三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1309876_comment'></div>朝廷创立，本欲与定海水军相为掎角，肃清海道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1309876_comment'></div>承平既久，寨无可用之卒，卒无可用之舟，半是买闲，半是占借，教练不习，击刺不闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1309876_comment'></div>兼九寨巡检，名系军班，部吏孺子，并不谙所谓海道事宜，目不曾接风涛，足未尝履海岸，尝惟循袭故事，掊尅自肥而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1309876_comment'></div>故此一千四百八十馀人之土军，徒费国家钱粮衣赐，亡具甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1309876_comment'></div>区区欲望朝廷将九寨巡检向去遇有满替之人，许从制司选辟曾从军伍、谙熟海道、惯会船水之人，充巡检职事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1309876_comment'></div>庶几头目之人以渐更易，众听不惊，而寨卒亦渐可训齐教习，以无用为有用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1309876_comment'></div>仍遇有盗贼，许令定海水军主兵官会合调遣，一应功赏，并与水军一体施行，实为海道悠久便利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1309876_comment'></div>于海道之防，所急舟船器械、教阅训练，臣岂不愿仰遵宣谕指挥，尽心力而为之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1309876_comment'></div>但大概非赤<span class='inlineComment2'>（下缺）</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_93_1309876_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年3月12日</a>　因兄渊卒，于三月十二日以变生同气丐祠。作品：《以变生同气丐祠札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷四。宛敏灏《吴潜年谱》误“十二日”作“二十日”）</span><div id='poem_1309822' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309822' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309822?labeling=true' target='_blank'>以变生同气丐祠劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（宝祐五年三月十二日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年3月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309822")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309822_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309822'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309822'>臣辄沥危衷，仰干圣听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309822_comment'></div>臣去岁仰蒙圣恩，起之山林，付以藩阃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309822_comment'></div>服勤半载，凋弊之郡渐无捉衿见肘之形，夺攘之民粗著卖剑买牛之习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309822_comment'></div>誓免竭于分寸，图报效于万分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309822_comment'></div>而臣福分满盈，变生同气，身殁异乡，忧虑薰心，神情惚恍，虽强加于鞭策，惧难免于旷瘝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309822_comment'></div>欲望皇帝陛下轸文王哀茕独之心，推《中庸》体群臣之意，俯垂矜恻，改畀真祠，俾得亟还里社，少尽殁存之谊，实戴君父隆天厚地之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309822_comment'></div>臣干冒宸严，无任祈天望圣激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1309822_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年4月23日</a>　四月二十三日，再乞祠。作品：《再乞祠札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷四。宛敏灏《吴潜年谱》误“二十三日”作“二十二日”）</span><div id='poem_1309823' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309823' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309823?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再乞祠劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月二十三日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年4月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309823")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309823_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309823'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309823'>臣比缘迫切之情，僭上退閒之请，恭膺明诏，未拜俞旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309823_comment'></div>愈跼地以回皇，复仰天而祈吁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309823_comment'></div>载念臣兹叨委使，猥玷旬宣，所期殚积日累月之勤，以少课御众牧人之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309823_comment'></div>虽微如垤蚁，义敢废于君臣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309823_comment'></div>然急若原鸰，念难忘于兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309823_comment'></div>欲望皇帝陛下俯垂睿鉴，深察臣衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309823_comment'></div>傥俾赋祠，固出曲成之造；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309823_comment'></div>或加予告，尤为特异之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309823_comment'></div>臣叠冒宸严，无任瞻天望圣激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1309823_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年5月14日</a>　夏五月，游曹娥祠，有诗。作品：《舟舣娥祠敬留二绝（宝祐丁巳夏五中干前一日）》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一〇。）</span><div id='poem_102850' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_102850' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/102850?labeling=true' target='_blank'>舟舣娥祠敬留二绝<span class='inlineComment2'>（宝祐丁巳夏五中浣前一日）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年5月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_102850")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_102850_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_102850'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_102850'>孝娥何意要垂名，重在天伦一命轻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_102850_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_102850'>若订汉家彤史传，淳于公女尚偷生。<div id='poem_sentence_1_102850_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_102850'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_102850_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_102849' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_102849' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/102849?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年5月14日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_102849_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_102849'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_102849'>虽然墟墓一拳土，泰华衡常未必侔。<div id='poem_sentence_0_102849_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_102849'>感动行人忠孝泪，沧江不断水东流。<div id='poem_sentence_1_102849_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_102849'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_102849_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年</a>　秋日，有诗。作品：《劭农》3首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷九。）</span>《出郊用劭农韵》3首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷九。）</span>《闻同官会碧沚用出郊韵》3首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷九。）</span>《出郊再用韵赋三解》9首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷九。）</span>《再用出郊韵似延庆老》3首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷九。）</span>《登延庆佛阁用出郊韵》3首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷九。）</span>《再用出郊韵》3首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷九。）</span>《三用出郊韵》3首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷九。）</span>《四用出郊韵》3首。<span id='poem_sentence_0_102925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_102925'>田畴虽幸收成早，沟浍犹疑灌溉残。<div id='poem_sentence_1_102925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_102925'>劝课农桑心独苦，丁宁父老吻应乾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_102925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_102925'>米从布袋痴儿事，我辈须知稼穑难。<div id='poem_sentence_3_102925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_102925'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_102925_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_102924' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_102924' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/102924?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_102924_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_102924'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_102924'>看他南亩十分收，归去来兮事尚悠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_102924_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_102924'>梦里便寻青栎社，生来几过白蘋洲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_102924_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_102924'>向前七帙无多岁，更后三朝即半秋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_102924_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_102924'>如电如阴如幻境，还知生熟路头不。<div id='poem_sentence_3_102924_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_102924'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_102924_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_102923' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_102923' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/102923?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_102923_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_102923'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_102923'>冥鸿本拟与鸡连，一笑西风沆瀣前。<div id='poem_sentence_0_102923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_102923'>放步退来元有地，从头算去莫非天。<div id='poem_sentence_1_102923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_102923'>可怜高举抟风翮，争似低飞饮露蝉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_102923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_102923'>若使危机能彻底，盈虚消息岂其然。<div id='poem_sentence_3_102923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_102923'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_102923_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年9月</a>　九月，又续请休致。作品：《奏乞休致及蠲放官赋摊钱见在钱米增积之数》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1309875' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309875' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309875?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞休致及蠲放官赋摊钱见在钱米增积之数</a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309875")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309875_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309875'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309875'><span class='inlineComment2'>（原缺四十四字）</span>然亦且及期而已尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309875_comment'></div>今者抑凭帝力，稼事大登，上赖皇威，海氛寖息，而臣年冉冉其将暮，行昧昧而未休，疾病萦身，忧畏销骨，爰沥忱恂之悃，曲祈荫庇之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309875_comment'></div>恭望皇帝陛下垂念盖帷，许还印绶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309875_comment'></div>六十三而休谢，傥追范镇之踪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309875_comment'></div>生老死于太平，庶遂邵雍之愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309875_comment'></div>臣无任祈天望圣、激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309875_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309875_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1309875'>〔贴黄〕照对臣忝以旧辅典藩，素知陛下悯念黎元之心，故臣自去秋领郡，即将宝祐元年秋料、二年夏料住催，继又将二年秋料、三年折帛钱蠲阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309875_comment'></div>近又以门堂在近，须将三年应干官赋并行除放，前后共放过钱五百四十九万一千七百七十七贯六十文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309875_comment'></div>又累政以来，多将公使库寄拍户百姓逋负摊赖，各催之钱，理为交头。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309875_comment'></div>见在被监之人，不下数十百，儿累老幼，哀鸣可念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309875_comment'></div>某尽行蠲放，仍将本任趱积到钱代为填纳，总为钱六十三万一千七百九十七贯八百四十六文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309875_comment'></div>通前两项，共计六百一十二万三千五百七十七贯九百单六文，该载并见榜文簿历，历历非欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309875_comment'></div>今官无拖俸，军无欠粮，朝廷诸司无稽违纲解，而库中之积比元交割尚增会子一百馀万贯，见钱伍万贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309875_comment'></div>元交割米止一千八十三石，今仓中及见在平江收籴在路之米，共管二万馀石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309875_comment'></div>继臣之后者，自可卧而治之，在臣别无一毫规避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309875_comment'></div>并乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1309875_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年9月26日</a>　九月二十六日，再辞。作品：《乞休致札子·九月二十六日》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷四。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年9月</a>　外甥陶世雄卒，为墓志铭。作品：《陶隐君墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1309916' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309916' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309916?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陶隐君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（宝祐五年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309916")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309916_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309916'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309916'>陶世雄，字伯英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309916_comment'></div>曾祖安，妣奚氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309916_comment'></div>祖甄，妣崔氏、江氏、吴氏，吴即予之姑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309916_comment'></div>父允升，妣刘氏、魏氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309916_comment'></div>俱隐德弗仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309916_comment'></div>世雄五岁丧母，未几又丧父，继母毓之有恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309916_comment'></div>刘死，世雄执丧有礼，乡人两称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309916_comment'></div>养孀姑惟谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309916_comment'></div>雅重好书，善治生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309916_comment'></div>早贫，晚岁优游，治家教子，俱有法度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309916_comment'></div>宝祐丁巳四月十有一日，以疾卒，得年五十有一，以九月壬申葬于昆山白杨之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309916_comment'></div>娶刘氏，继以刘氏、高氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309916_comment'></div>子男三人，九皋、九云、九功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309916_comment'></div>女四人，长适进士张俊民，次适进士陈宏中，馀尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309916_comment'></div>陶氏世居姑孰，先君子正肃公笃友于之爱，俾迁于宣之慈溪，以便岁时叙集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309916_comment'></div>予兄弟时相与周旋九皋父子兄弟之间，别几年而九皋以缞绖请予铭墓矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309916_comment'></div>为之铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1309916'>宋正肃吴公甥孙陶世雄伯英之墓，积施有食，其在子孙乎！</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1309916_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年</a>　岁暮，有诗追念吴渊。作品：《小至三诗呈景回制干并简同官》<span id='poem_content_102920'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_102920'>六十三馀七十翁，颇从静里得些工。<div id='poem_sentence_0_102920_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_102920'>阴阳理向尘尘见，天地心于物物同。<div id='poem_sentence_1_102920_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_102920'>荔挺生来元不死，葭灰塞处自能通。<div id='poem_sentence_0_102919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_102919'>履袜已无亲可献，黍羔犹与俗相宜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_102919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103055_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103055'>可须滕巽同宣力，坐使颛冥不旷官。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103055_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
