id='poem_sentence_0_102890'>陈年古屋瓦浮虚，穿漏时将被覆书。<div id='poem_sentence_0_102890_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_102890'>集谢曾陪上相后，映孙难忘秀才初。<div id='poem_sentence_1_102890_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_102890'>砖花似镂多奇异，檐柱如排少阔疏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_102890_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_102890'>吏卒报衙天未晓，老身牵强类冠狙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_102890_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_102890'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_102890_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_102903' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_102903' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/102903?labeling=true' target='_blank'>十一二用喜雪韵四首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_102903")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_102903_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_102903'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_102903'>水泼衾裘夜卧难，也休暖足唤端端。<div id='poem_sentence_0_102903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_102903'>平生自是冰为氏，此际何妨火纪官。<div id='poem_sentence_1_102903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_102903'>无色图从天地展，有声画与古今看。<div id='poem_sentence_2_102903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_102903'>忽思十万边兵冷，肤体相关岂独胖。<div id='poem_sentence_3_102903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_102903'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_102903_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_102902' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_102902' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/102902?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_102902_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_102902'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_102902'>片片穿帷解捣虚，夜明细字亦堪书。<div id='poem_sentence_0_102902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_102902'>五车现瑞从今后，一尺呈祥复古初。<div id='poem_sentence_1_102902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_102902'>暖室温轩人起晏，远坊穷巷客来疏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_102902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_102902'>茅山见说黄精熟，山友迷踪餍黠狙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_102902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_102902'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_102902_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_102901' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_102901' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/102901?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_102901_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_102901'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_102901'>长安贫者再炊难，臛肉苍头饫舌端。<div id='poem_sentence_0_102901_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_102901'>食雪自应还猛将，饮冰只合付清官。<div id='poem_sentence_1_102901_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_102901'>尚兴塞外鸣弦想，剩欲江头把钓看。<div id='poem_sentence_2_102901_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_102901'>只恐逢他吹铁笛，骨寒股战失吾胖。<div id='poem_sentence_3_102901_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_102901'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_102901_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_102900' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_102900' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/102900?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_102900_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_102900'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_102900'>只堪闭户著潜虚，欲作遨头畏简书。<div id='poem_sentence_0_102900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_102900'>乍密乍稀云冻后，半融半落雨收初。<div id='poem_sentence_1_102900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_102900'>封条正恐观梅错，渍谷犹疑学稼疏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_102900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_102900'>却喜明朝春税驾，气苏𥜿𥜿与狙狙<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：𥜿音翡。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_102900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_102900'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_102900_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_102907' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_102907' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/102907?labeling=true' target='_blank'>十三四用喜雪韵四首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_102907")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_102907_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_102907'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_102907'>安西都护肯辞难，不怕亡胡起怨端。<div id='poem_sentence_0_102907_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_102907'>节义士知堪作使，神仙人岂恋为官。<div id='poem_sentence_1_102907_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_102907'>寒肩此际如楼耸，眩眼当年似席看。<div id='poem_sentence_2_102907_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_102907'>百丈山中谁筑室，是中非隘亦非胖。<div id='poem_sentence_3_102907_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_102907'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_102907_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_102906' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_102906' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/102906?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_102906_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_102906'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_102906'>瑞气应缠牛女虚，坐令三白历家书。<div id='poem_sentence_0_102906_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_102906'>竹寒不用歌周末，粟腐行将纪汉初。<div id='poem_sentence_1_102906_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_102906'>蟠际混同能广大，方圆成就更通疏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_102906_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_102906'>狐猿夜半疑天晓，叫起攀林挂树狙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_102906_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_102906'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_102906_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_102905' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_102905' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/102905?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_102905_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_102905'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_102905'>普博谁云仁道难，剪裁妙巧智之端。<div id='poem_sentence_0_102905_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_102905'>都将凡物换英物，尽欲热官成冷官。<div id='poem_sentence_1_102905_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_102905'>色即是空随手灭，恩生于害转头看。<div id='poem_sentence_2_102905_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_102905'>大千界里毫光彻，稽首惟应礼屈胖。<div id='poem_sentence_3_102905_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_102905'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_102905_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_102904' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_102904' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/102904?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_102904_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_102904'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_102904'>雪边好景说涵虚，欲往从之掣簿书。<div id='poem_sentence_0_102904_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_102904'>王道平平须有象，皇风浩浩恐无初。<div id='poem_sentence_1_102904_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_102904'>举遮正恐渠难耐，罢扫缘忧彼作疏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_102904_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_102904'>翠浪黄云来岁事，已应痴望到毚狙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_102904_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_102904'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_102904_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年</a>　阅城壁，有诗记之。作品：《阅城壁》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_103037' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103037' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103037?labeling=true' target='_blank'>阅城壁</a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103037")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_103037_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103037'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103037'>内江外海四周围，正是绸缪户牖时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103037_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103037'>北瞰登莱山不碍，东渐倭丽汛难期。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103037_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103037'>未须鹞鹢增威势，已觉狌鼯受指麾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103037_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103037'>敢谓虚名弹压得，多应一念老天知。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103037_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103037'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_103037_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年</a>　孙梦观卒，为墓志铭。作品：《孙守叔墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1309918' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309918' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309918?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孙守叔墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309918")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309918_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309918'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309918'>嘉熙丁酉，余以工部侍郎领吴牧，适常平使者阙，被旨摄事，始与鄞人孙守叔为同僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309918_comment'></div>即之久，见其人温纯肃洁，心异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309918_comment'></div>未几，守叔果拾级而上青云矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309918_comment'></div>其在朝廷，则靖共之度、正直之节，人尊而仰之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309918_comment'></div>其在郡国，则廉平之誉、恺悌之风，民歌而诵之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309918_comment'></div>然年未六十，遽弃明时，其命也夫，其可悲也夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309918_comment'></div>君讳梦观，守叔其字，雪窗其号也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309918_comment'></div>曾大父俊乂，故登仕郎、泗州招信县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309918_comment'></div>妣严氏，继张氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309918_comment'></div>大父才冠，故承信郎、监临安府于潜县税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309918_comment'></div>妣刘氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309918_comment'></div>考参，赠奉直大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309918_comment'></div>妣陆氏，赠令人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309918_comment'></div>君登丙戌进士第，与兄渊俱占南宫龟列，授迪功郎，调桂阳军教授、浙西提举司干办公事，差主管吏部架阁文字，除武学谕，添差通判严州，台州崇道观，复除武学博士，太常寺簿，诸王宫大小学教授，宗正丞，兼屯田郎官，将作少监，知嘉兴府，仍旧班兼右曹郎官，将作监，国子司业，知泉州，兼提举市舶事，改知宁国府，除司农少卿，兼资善堂赞读，太府卿，充御试编排官，宗正少卿，兼给事中，起居舍人，起居郎，直龙图阁，予祠，慈溪县开国男，食邑三百户，秘阁修撰，江淮等路提点铸钱公事，复除起居郎，兼右侍郎，给事中，兼赞读，兼国子祭酒，权吏部侍郎，集英殿修撰，知建宁府，积官至宣奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309918_comment'></div>君世居郡之慈溪，奉直公质直而好义，以善人称于乡，慈湖先生杨文元公尝志其墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309918_comment'></div>积厚报丰，遂生君，为闻人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309918_comment'></div>初与二兄因、渊自为师友，既中第，益留意古学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309918_comment'></div>为郡博士，专以考亭之书淑诸生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309918_comment'></div>州境有蛮寇，帅廉君宜于士而习其俗，越次命君摄事，寇即定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309918_comment'></div>浙右盐策最浩繁，为幕官者诸场岁时例有馈，君皆却绝，户庭如水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309918_comment'></div>王侍郎遂以侍从典州，以其学行才美荐于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309918_comment'></div>甫登畿，轮当面对，首论人主听言不容有所惮，尤不容有所玩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309918_comment'></div>惮则有言而不能容，玩则虽容其言而不能用，切中千古之病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309918_comment'></div>时乡衮执国柄，咸谓美官可券取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309918_comment'></div>君力请员外治中以去，旋引疾归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309918_comment'></div>踰季复召，横经朱𨚎，皇弟太傅嗣王嘉其三益之助，爱敬弥笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309918_comment'></div>复当陛对，援《周书》「抚后虐雠」及《文中子》「戎狄之德，黎民怀之」之说，恳恳为上陈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309918_comment'></div>寻以戎监转对，极言风宪之地，未闻有十人疏攻一竦者，封驳之司未闻有三舍人不肯草制者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309918_comment'></div>且论道揆不明，法守滋乱，天下之权将有所寄而倒持之患作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309918_comment'></div>当路者浸不悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309918_comment'></div>出守泉州，旋易宣，蠲逋减赋，不计缗石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309918_comment'></div>凡有汎入，尽籍于公，蔬食布衣，如苦行僧衲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1309918_comment'></div>时虽供亿甚繁而郡不告匮，版曹专官督赋如星火急，阖郡皇骇，莫知为计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1309918_comment'></div>君曰吾宁委官以去，毋宁病民以留，力丐祠，且将以郡印牒专官，专官闻之夜遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1309918_comment'></div>宣人至今言之，尚流涕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1309918_comment'></div>董丞相槐以枢密召还，上问江东廉吏，首以君对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1309918_comment'></div>上悦，除司农少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1309918_comment'></div>适资善讲官缺员，上遴选端良之士，亟命君兼赞读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1309918_comment'></div>轮当陛对，奏谓「国家必有所恃而后立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1309918_comment'></div>今内外之臣恃陛下以各遂其私，而陛下独一无可恃，可为寒心」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1309918_comment'></div>次论「郡国当为斯民计，朝廷当为郡国计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1309918_comment'></div>乞命大臣，应自前主计之臣夺州县之利而归版曹者复归所属，庶几郡国蒙一分之宽，则斯民亦受一分之赐」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1309918_comment'></div>其言一一如蓍龟，上首肯，且奉玉音：「卿在资善，更烦尽心」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1309918_comment'></div>先是有以越职言事削秩者，踰季黄犹在牍，君曰「此非法也」，即日涂归，且乞叙用其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1309918_comment'></div>时有为公论所指目者，除职予郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1309918_comment'></div>君奏谓「王安石欲去熙宁之君子则名以流俗，京、卞欲去元祐之君子则名为邪党，秦桧欲去绍兴之君子则名以异议，李沐、陈贾欲去庆元之君子则名以伪学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1309918_comment'></div>某人复倡为虚议论，以尽去更化以来所收召之君子，非所以为世道计」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1309918_comment'></div>四月，以资善堂满岁迁，制词有曰：「虽舍章从事，有訚訚侃侃似不能言之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1309918_comment'></div>及批敕涂黄，乃謇謇谔谔有凛不可犯之色」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1309918_comment'></div>盖上意也，当国者恶之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1309918_comment'></div>是月，免兼琐闼，进右螭，八上章引退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1309918_comment'></div>乙卯正月，进左螭，免牍三四上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1309918_comment'></div>憸人吴燧挤而击之，除直龙图阁，予祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1309918_comment'></div>十月，升秘撰，提泉诸道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1309918_comment'></div>丙辰正月，甫抵司存，复以旧班召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1309918_comment'></div>公闻命，凡泉司供帐悉付之护印者，归装萧然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1309918_comment'></div>抵门奏事，抗论益切，大概以「宠赂彰，仁贤逝，货财偏聚」为言，且谓未易相之前弊政固不少，既易相之后弊政亦自若，在廷之士皆危之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1309918_comment'></div>君曰：「吾以一布衣蒙上恩至此，虽捐躯无以报，利钝非所计也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1309918_comment'></div>未几，进侍郎右选，仍兼琐闼赞读如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1309918_comment'></div>皇子忠王闻君再为讲官，喜甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1309918_comment'></div>君每入讲，必援先儒格言，反覆开陈，王亦多所咨问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1309918_comment'></div>七月，进大司成，旋真除二卿，升翊善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1309918_comment'></div>君亲被主知，屡膺天奖，两地可以拾级而升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1309918_comment'></div>然雅志恬淡，入从仅三月即三疏祈閒，辞甚苦，至上留之不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1309918_comment'></div>二月，以殿撰宅牧武夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1309918_comment'></div>夏五领事，首以考亭先生絜矩之义谕郡人，蠲丝谷之积逋不趐以万计，不遣一卒下属邑，两造在庭，决以公是，虽丽于罚者无怨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1309918_comment'></div>布衣蔬食之操，视守宣有加焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1309918_comment'></div>建多君子，其达官显人徐知院清叟、蔡参政杭皆相推，以为有古循吏风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1309918_comment'></div>君每谓诸邑月解自盐运不续，凿空取办，展转病民，方欲为千里赤子祈哀于上，图所以变而通之者，遽以微疢至大故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1309918_comment'></div>未属纩前，犹揽衣危坐，曰：「吾荷上奇遇，忠言无不售。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1309918_comment'></div>虽屡为柄臣所排，独主上保全，以至于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1309918_comment'></div>今病，不可为论报，已矣」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1309918_comment'></div>口授遗表，忱实恳恻，不出于《大学》末章人才、货财之二事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1309918_comment'></div>草毕凝然而逝，七月十二日也，享年五十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1309918_comment'></div>讣闻，上悼惜久之，貤恩如律，加赙赠三百疋两，制词有曰：「贰铨省以抡材，其清如水；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1309918_comment'></div>登琐闼而批敕，有力回天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1309918_comment'></div>深悼遗忠，再加禭饰」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1309918_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1309918_comment'></div>君之报主未终而上之眷君益厚，君有遗憾而上则无遗憾矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1309918_comment'></div>君未薨前三日，郡人有梦从者甚都，迎祠山神，自郡治出，视之则公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1309918_comment'></div>俄而君不吊，阖郡士民相与惊异，多至泣下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1309918_comment'></div>君娶叶氏，平庵项公宣抚之亲甥，躬务勤俭，克相其夫，先君十八年卒，赠令人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1309918_comment'></div>子男六人，五人皆幼亡，从孙将以公致仕泽补承务郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1309918_comment'></div>女二人，在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1309918_comment'></div>从孙九月辛酉葬君于邑之郎官坪之原，并徙叶氏令人合隧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1309918_comment'></div>潜尝谓孔子才难之叹，以为唐虞之际，于斯为盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1309918_comment'></div>际者接也，言自唐虞下至于周而人才之盛方见于斯，意者自皋陶九德之目至周之九人而始备乎，故曰才难，不其然乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1309918_comment'></div>后世之才固未易与盛周时比，然如君者，亦几于宽栗、柔立、愿恭、乱敬、扰毅、直温、简廉、刚塞、彊义之大致矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1309918_comment'></div>其为人退然若不胜衣，然义所当为，奋往直前，虽贲育之勇不能过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1309918_comment'></div>故其立朝之节光明俊伟，与严霜烈日争光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1309918_comment'></div>至其治郡，则纯以宽大奉行诏令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1309918_comment'></div>在宣时，教条简便，刑罚寝息，日未晡吏散，庭宣帘阒然，人不知其为太守治所也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1309918_comment'></div>古所谓循吏非耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1309918_comment'></div>乃若居家孝友，居乡退逊，处赵魏之乡，争以陶朱、猗顿相雄长，而泊然自好，视货财如粪土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1309918_comment'></div>入都法从，出领藩符，不过败屋数间，人不堪其忧而君处之裕如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1309918_comment'></div>可谓清风高节，远追董孝而逼慈湖矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1309918_comment'></div>瞻众鸟之翔飞，怅祥凤之孤逝，得不重为世道惜耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1309918_comment'></div>潜与君交虽澹而意甚真，其死也不克临其棺，其藏也不克临其穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1309918_comment'></div>从孙以状来请志其墓，不忍辞而为之铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_98_1309918'>有德之人，默默循循。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1309918_comment'></div>内不足者，骄誇矜盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1309918_comment'></div>彼美雪窗，抱德怀节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1309918_comment'></div>退然无能，厥闻四达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1309918_comment'></div>越三十载，中外荐更。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1309918_comment'></div>不急不徐，维义之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1309918_comment'></div>淳祐中年，风宪消弭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1309918_comment'></div>乱匪自它，权贵所使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1309918_comment'></div>谁能抗疏，排云敷陈？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1309918_comment'></div>君于是时，王吉贾生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1309918_comment'></div>宝祐之初，朋引憸慝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1309918_comment'></div>邪燄欲炽，正理几蚀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1309918_comment'></div>谁遏其萌，罔俾复然？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1309918_comment'></div>君于是时，富弼李藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1309918_comment'></div>方在邸僚，里人当路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1309918_comment'></div>步要津，掉头引去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1309918_comment'></div>强御横行，谁敢侮予！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1309918_comment'></div>直唾怒虎，折箠奋呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1309918_comment'></div>身在南邦，心在王室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1309918_comment'></div>方徯东归，妖梦随入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1309918_comment'></div>名山大川，舒敛英灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1309918_comment'></div>明则为人，幽复为神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1309918_comment'></div>不以存存，不以亡坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1309918_comment'></div>亦理之常，无足怪者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1309918_comment'></div>千载而下，川陵变迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1309918_comment'></div>视诸斯文，敬心油然。</div><div id='poem_sentence_123_1309918_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年</a>　孙梦观卒，为像赞。作品：《孙守叔像赞》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1309914' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309914' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309914?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孙守叔像赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309914")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309914_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309914'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309914'>神气完固，胸次洒落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309914_comment'></div>云鹤游空，冰檗在壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309914_comment'></div>以敬义为执持，以经史为该博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309914_comment'></div>引君当道也，则天开日明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309914_comment'></div>为国除暴也，若风驱电却。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309914_comment'></div>可托孤而寄命，诚先忧而后乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309914_comment'></div>惜乎年甫六十而令终，失此北门之锁钥也，噫！</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1309914_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年1月15日</a>　元宵节，有词。作品：《水龙吟·戊午元夕》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一一。）</span><div id='poem_103110' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103110' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103110?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水龙吟 戊午元夕</a><span class='authorDate'>（1258年1月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103110")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103110_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103110'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103110'>十洲三岛蓬壶，是花锦、一团装就。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103110'>轻车细辇，绮罗香里，夜光如昼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103110'>朱户笙箫，画楼帘幕，有人回首。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103110'>想金莲灿烂，星毬缥缈，那风景、年时旧。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103110_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103110'>应念白头太守。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103110'>怎红旗、六街穿透。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103110'>铺排玳席，追陪珠履，且酾春酎。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103110'>楚舞秦讴，半慵莺舌，叠翻鸳袖。<div id='poem_sentence_7_103110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_103110'>把千门喜色，万家和气，祝君王寿。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_103110_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年2月17日</a>　二月十七日，有词赋四明窗。作品：《满江红·戊午二月十七日四明窗赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一一。）</span>《满江红·再和》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一一。）</span><div id='poem_103279' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103279' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103279?labeling=true' target='_blank'>满江红<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>戊午二月十七日四明窗赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1258年2月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103279")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103279_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103279'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103279'>芳景无多，又还是、乱红飞坠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103279'>空怅望、昭亭深处，家山桃李。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103279'>柳眼花心都脱换，蜂须蝶翅难沾缀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103279'>谩相携、一笑竞良辰，春醪美。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103279_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103279'>金兽爇，香风细。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103279'>金凤拍，歌云腻。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103279'>尽秦箫燕管，但逢场尔。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103279'>只恐思乡情味恶，怎禁寒食清明里。<div id='poem_sentence_7_103279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_103279'>问此翁、不止四宜休，翁归未。<div id='poem_sentence_8_103279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_103279'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_103279_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_103297' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103297' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103297?labeling=true' target='_blank'>满江红<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>再和</a><span class='authorDate'>（1258年2月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103297")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103297_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103297'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103297'>聊把芳樽，殷勤劝、斜阳休坠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103297'>吾老矣，难从仙客，采丹丘李。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103297'>且趁风光一百五，园林尚有残红缀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103297'>更忉忉、百舌对般春，声能美。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103297_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103297'>鸾钗绊，游丝细。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103297'>鸳袖惹，香尘腻。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103297'>想吴姬越女，踏青才尔。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103297'>争似江南樗枥社，俚歌声拂行云里。<div id='poem_sentence_7_103297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_103297'>又枝头、梅子正酸时，莺知未。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_103297_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年</a>　二月二十四，会碧沚亭，有词。作品：《满江红·戊午二月二十四日会碧沚》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一一。）</span>《满江红·碧沚月湖四用韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一一。）</span>《满江红·二园花卉仅有海棠未谢五用韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一一。）</span><div id='poem_103280' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103280' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103280?labeling=true' target='_blank'>满江红<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>戊午二月二十四日会碧沚，三用韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1258年2月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103280")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103280_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103280'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103280'>楼观峥嵘，浑疑是、天风吹坠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103280_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103280'>金屋窈，几时曾贮，粗桃凡李。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103280_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103280'>镜断钗分人去后，画栏文砌苍苔缀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103280_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103280'>想当年、日日醉芳丛，侯鲭美。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103280_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103280'>春水涨，鳞鳞细。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103280_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103280'>春草暗，茸茸腻。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103280_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103280'>算留连光景，古犹今尔。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103280_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103280'>椿菌鸠鹏休较计，倚空一笑东风里。<div id='poem_sentence_7_103280_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_103280'>喜知时、好雨夜来稠，秧青未。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_103280_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_103288' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103288' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103288?labeling=true' target='_blank'>满江红<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>碧沚月湖，四用韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1258年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103288")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103288_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103288'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103288'>一笑相携，且休管、兔升乌坠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103288_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103288'>那更是，可人宾客，未饶崔李。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103288_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103288'>金叵罗中醽醁莹，玉玲珑畔歌珠缀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103288_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103288'>望湖光、一片浸韶光，真双美。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103288_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103288'>云絮襞，能纤细。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103288_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103288'>云䌽聚，能粘腻。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103288_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103288'>料出山归岫，等闲间尔。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103288_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103288'>碧沚风流人去后，石窗景物春深里。<div id='poem_sentence_7_103288_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_103288'>算邯郸、客梦几经残，炊犹未。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_103288_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_103295' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103295' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103295?labeling=true' target='_blank'>满江红<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span>二园花卉仅有海棠未谢，五用韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1258年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103295")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103295_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103295'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103295'>问海棠花，谁留恋、未教飘坠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103295'>真个好，一般标格，娉梅奴李。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103295'>怯冷拟将苏幕护，怕惊莫把金铃缀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103295'>望铜梁、玉垒正春深，花空美。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103295_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103295'>非粉饰，肌肤细。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103295'>非涂泽，胭脂腻。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103295'>恐人间天上，少其伦尔。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103295'>西子颦收初雨后，太真浴罢微暄里。<div id='poem_sentence_7_103295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_103295'>又明朝、杨柳插清明，鹃归未。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_103295_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年</a>　乡举鹿鸣劝驾，有诗。作品：《乡举鹿鸣劝驾·戊午》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_102918' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_102918' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/102918?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乡举鹿鸣劝驾</a><span class='authorDate'>（戊午）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_102918")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_102918_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_102918'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_102918'>上苑春光已探来，诸公逸驾莫迟回。<div id='poem_sentence_0_102918_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_102918'>点头定有文惊坐，烧尾何妨酒吸杯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_102918_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_102918'>自是功名难躲避，须知气节要壅培。<div id='poem_sentence_2_102918_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_102918'>老夫亲手传衣钵，来岁图经用再开。<div id='poem_sentence_3_102918_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_102918'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_102918_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年</a>　奏按象山宰不放民间房钱。作品：《奏按象山宰不放民间房钱》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1309877' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309877' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309877?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏按象山宰不放民间房钱<span class='inlineComment2'>（宝祐六年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1258年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309877")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309877_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309877'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309877'>臣闻诸孟轲曰，「见无礼于其君者，如鹰鹯之逐鸟雀也」，臣终身诵之惟谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309877_comment'></div>照得朝廷近以雨泽愆期，遍行祈祷，恭奉圣旨，应民间房赁，不以大小，统放半月，汪濊之恩，被于海隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309877_comment'></div>臣奉行惟恐不虔，登时具文榜，行下诸县，一体遵守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309877_comment'></div>继闻县道多有与大家上户为伍，沉匿文榜，不行揭示者，遂分差人吏，前往监督县吏，逐一施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309877_comment'></div>续据差下象山县吏贴李奎回同供责称，本县自来凡朝廷及本府宽恤事宜，例不曾奉行，并取到市户胡三十太等具状称：三十太等今奉太使府差人前来契勘，放免官私房廊白地等赁钱等事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309877_comment'></div>且三十太等各系经纪小民，赁屋居住开店，每遇太使府及上司并奉圣旨节次行下，减放赁钱，无不感戴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309877_comment'></div>虽本县备榜晓示，缘本县乡里屋主，皆系寄居官户者，即不曾遵照指挥放免所是赁钱投月典还掠钱人交纳，如到冬节它放三日，岁节五日，上元节三日，其他即无减放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309877_comment'></div>设若赁客欲退官放，便被起离，所以并不敢执退官放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309877_comment'></div>所责證并是的实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309877_comment'></div>又据李奎供，本县因闻胡三十太等□状，其县吏毛益即取覆知县，追胡三十太勘断，责令退状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309877_comment'></div>口称屋主炒人，你若责状去州府，回后只来你身主讨事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309877_comment'></div>臣窃惟普天之下，莫非王土，率土之滨，莫非王臣，象山岂非王土乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309877_comment'></div>为象山之官吏与寄寓缙绅，非王臣乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309877_comment'></div>而奉旨蠲放房赁，大家上户，视之如无，县道官吏知有大家上户，而不知有君上，非所以辨上下、定民志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309877_comment'></div>事若甚微，关系实大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309877_comment'></div>司马光《通鉴》之首，专以名分为言，其旨深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309877_comment'></div>臣欲望圣慈特发睿断，将宣教郎、知象山县孙逢辰量与镌秩，以示惩警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309877_comment'></div>仍行下无干碍监司，根究本县寄居房赁最多、不有上旨、不伏蠲放之人，施行一二，庶足为慢上尅下者之戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309877_comment'></div>其于教化，不为小补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309877_comment'></div>须至奏闻者。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1309877_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年</a>　请就淮西管下岁籴以继军食之阙。作品：《奏乞就淮西管下岁籴以继军食之阙》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1309878' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309878' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309878?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞就淮西管下岁籴以继军食之阙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1258年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309878")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309878_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309878'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309878'>照对臣自前岁抵郡，夷考本府不可支吾之因，专苦于军粮之不继，遂行奏申，乞就淮西管下岁籴十万石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309878_comment'></div>已准尚书省劄子，备奉圣旨，许令本府据欠阙之数，前往收籴，亦不拘十万之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309878_comment'></div>本府两年之间，百计提聚官钱，仅能籴及六七万石，尚未及一岁十万之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309878_comment'></div>近缘青黄不接，军食正艰，遂差官吏往平江收籴四万石，以备支遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309878_comment'></div>并将昨来朝廷发还借支义仓米价钱四十万贯，收籴一万石，以偿上件义仓窠名，共为米五万石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309878_comment'></div>已差拨军船，雇募民船、摺运船载，出港之间，忽准发运司反汗拘拦，所有昨来已奉圣旨指挥，未肯行用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309878_comment'></div>缘本府尅期尅日，以待此米之至，支散二十四五日水军厢禁军土军，共一万馀人军粮，实是狼狈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309878_comment'></div>万一庚癸之呼，某一身不足恤，如国事何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309878_comment'></div>不免星驰具状申闻，欲望朝廷特赐敷奏，降付尚书省，劄下发运司，照所降圣旨指挥，即与通放施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309878_comment'></div>臣无任延颈俟命，如囚待赦之切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309878_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1309878'>〔贴子〕臣昨因郡境入春以来颇有旱意，深虑秋成难准，急在聚粮，倾竭帑藏所储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309878_comment'></div>又委本司参议官赵汝俳，前往嘉兴府收籴一万五千石，并委权本司计议官杜友宽，就镇江府管下收籴小米五千石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309878_comment'></div>虽据各官回申，已行籴下，伺候起发外，今来切恐各县仍复把持，不与通放，颇计利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309878_comment'></div>欲望圣慈并下尚书省，备劄各处及发运司，照应通放施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309878_comment'></div>伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1309878_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年5月5日</a>　五月五日，有词自寿。作品：《沁园春·戊午自寿》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一一。）</span><div id='poem_103160' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103160' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103160?labeling=true' target='_blank'>沁园春<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>戊午自寿</a><span class='authorDate'>（1258年5月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103160")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103160_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103160'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103160'>笑指颓龄，循环雌甲，卦数已圆。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103160_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103160'>叹蜀公高洁，休官去岁，温公耆旧，入社今年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103160_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103160'>底事崎岖，苍颜白发，犹拥貔貅护海堧。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103160_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103160'>君恩重，算何能报国，未许归田。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103160_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103160'>遥怜。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103160_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103160'>宛居山前。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103160_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103160'>正水涨溪肥系钓船。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103160_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103160'>纵葵榴花闹，菖蒲酒美，都成客里，争似家边。<div id='poem_sentence_7_103160_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_103160'>寄语儿曹，若为翁寿，只把鸥盟更要坚。<div id='poem_sentence_8_103160_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_103160'>翁还祝，愿欃枪日静，䆉稏云连。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_103160_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年5月17日</a>　五月十七日，饯别赵物斛。作品：《饯赵物斛·戊午五月十七日》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一〇。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年</a>　有诗寄方遇。作品：《秋思一首寄方君遇》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一〇。）</span><div id='poem_103023' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103023' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103023?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋思一首寄方君遇</a><span class='authorDate'>（1258年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103023")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_103023_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103023'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103023'>西风黄叶堕阶前，秋思撩人已可怜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103023_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103023'>身渐衰来非一日，心都懒处是今年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103023_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103023'>爱憎毁誉何关我，消息盈虚要识天。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103023_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103023'>六十四翁凡百足，只祈君相放归田。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103023_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103023'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_103023_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年8月1日</a>　八月初一，以两考乞休致。作品：《以两考乞休致札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1309825' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309825' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309825?labeling=true' target='_blank'>以两考乞休致劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（八月初一日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1258年8月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309825")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309825_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309825'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309825'>臣伏以代匮海垣，倏岁成之再考；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309825_comment'></div>循环天运，已卦气之一周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309825_comment'></div>理粗识于盈虚，分当知于止足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309825_comment'></div>仰瞻蠖濩，俯沥蚁忱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309825_comment'></div>伏念臣孑尔孤荑，枵然大匏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309825_comment'></div>思宁考延集英之对，龙头凡擢于十人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309825_comment'></div>自庆元数进士之题，鲐背仅馀于一老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309825_comment'></div>陛下继有邰之存，录丰芑之遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309825_comment'></div>雨露滋生，培植于根荄之日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309825_comment'></div>天地覆载，扶持于条达之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309825_comment'></div>莫名顶踵之大恩，迄被股肱之重寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309825_comment'></div>自惭鼎覆，求合遁藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309825_comment'></div>皇明不弃于盖帷，青冥复下于斧钺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309825_comment'></div>光阴易掷，绩效蔑闻，而臣徒以弊精神于簿书狱讼蹇浅之间，增疢疾于筋骸齿发衰迟之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309825_comment'></div>况值甲庚之数，适临己午之辰，聚并叠冲，沓刑互尅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309825_comment'></div>粤固形于宇宙，宜致寇于阴阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309825_comment'></div>觉暮景之难凭，恐长夜之忽至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309825_comment'></div>欲望皇帝陛下怜臣膂力之既竭，察臣悃愊之非欺，锡以安存，许其休谢，或仍赋汉祠之禄，俾退寻尧野之耕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309825_comment'></div>熊禽亦爱身，傥少逭西日桑榆之迫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309825_comment'></div>犬马知恋主，但虔伸南山松柏之祈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309825_comment'></div>臣无任瞻天望圣激切恳祈之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1309825_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年8月</a>　八月，有词。作品：《满江红·苍云堂后有桂树，为冬青遮蔽，低垂将陨矣。戊午八月呼梓人为伐而去之，赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一一。宛敏灏《吴潜年谱》“遮蔽”作“遮避”）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年8月15日</a>　中秋节，与刘锡等友人饮酒聚会，有词。作品：《满江红·戊午秋半偕胡景回、刘自昭二兄小饮待月》<span class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103286'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103286'>试问平生，几番见、中秋明月。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103286'>今老矣，一年紧似，一年时节。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103286'>底事层阴生障碍，不教玉界冰壶彻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103286'>莫姮娥、嫌此白头翁，心肠别。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103286_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103286'>风动处，浮云揭。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103286'>云绽处，清光泄。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103230_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103230'>有时推出赖他风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103230_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103230_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年8月17日</a>　八月十七，再乞休致。作品：《再乞休致札子》<span ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309826")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309826_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309826'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309826'>臣近尝具疏闻奏，乞畀祠官，恭奉诏书不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309826_comment'></div>涣攽温诏，犹俨对于威颜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309826_comment'></div>震惕危衷，合祗承于休命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309826_comment'></div>尚储丹悃，仰扣皇慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309826_comment'></div>载念臣夙被鸿恩，未殚蚁报，徒以涉历更尝之久，凛乎忧患疢疾之多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309826_comment'></div>心剿神疲，敢谓勤劳之故？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309826_comment'></div>气衰胆薄，良由迟暮而然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309826_comment'></div>比肃观湘弼醴泉之词，具恭睹歙相洞霄之制，莫不嘉其恬退，于是锡以优閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309826_comment'></div>如臣素惧于盈满，宁独不思于止足！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309826_comment'></div>况阅官成之再考，靡闻郡最之一书，其视具僚，尤虞不绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309826_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下俯加从欲，仍俾祝釐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309826_comment'></div>病颡长鸣，虽难忘于闲厩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309826_comment'></div>惊禽却顾，终愿返于山林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309826_comment'></div>臣叠冒宸严，无任瞻天望圣激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1309826_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: </span>夜来月佳甚，呈景回、自昭二兄。戊午八月十八日</a><span class='authorDate'>（1258年8月18日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103118'>过了中秋后，今夜月方佳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103118_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103118'>看来前夜圆满，才是阙些些。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103118_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103118'>扫尽乌云黑雾，放出青霄碧落，恰似我情怀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103118_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103118'>把酒自斟酌，脱略到形骸。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103118_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103118'>问渠侬，分玉镜，断金钗。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103118_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103118'>少年心事，不知容易鬓边华。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103118_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103118'>千古天同此月，千古人同此兴，不是旋安排。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103118_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103118'>安得高飞去，长以月为家。</div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年8月27日</a>　八月二十七日，于进思堂赏第二木樨，有词。作品：《满江红·戌午八月二十七日进思堂赏第二木樨》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一一。）</span><div id='poem_103271' id='poem_sentence_1_103271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103271'>树杪层层如宝盖，枝头点点犹金粟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103271'>叹吾今老矣，两难追逐。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103271'>休把淹留成感慨，时间赏玩时间福。<div id='poem_sentence_7_103271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_103271'>怕今宵、芳景便凋零，高烧烛。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_103271_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年9月7日</a>　九月七日，游碧沚亭，与刘锡有词唱和。作品：《满江红·戊子九月七日碧沚和制几韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一一。）</span><div id='poem_103287' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103287' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103287?labeling=true' target='_blank'>满江红<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>戊午九月七日，碧沚和制几韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1258年9月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103287")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103287_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103287'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103287'>岁岁重阳，何曾是、两般时景。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103287'>人自有、悲欢离合，晦明朝暝。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103287'>日月湖边来往艇，楼台水底参差影。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103287'>又何妨、时暂狎沧波，轻鸥并。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103287_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103287'>闲顿放，朱门静。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103287'>新结裹，朱帘整。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103287'>尽百年人事，移场换境。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103287'>欲插黄花身已老，强倾绿醑心先醒。<div id='poem_sentence_7_103287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_103287'>羡游鱼、有钓不能收，钩空饼。<div id='poem_sentence_8_103287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_103287'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_103287_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年9月9日</a>　九月九日，偕同官延庆阁，过碧沚，有词。作品：《水调歌头·戊午九日偕同官延庆阁，过碧沚》<span class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103129?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>戊午九月，偕同官延庆阁过碧沚</a><span class='authorDate'>（1258年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103129")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103129_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103129'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103129'>重九先三日，领客上危楼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103129'>满城风雨都住，天亦相遨头。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103129'>右手持杯满泛，左手持螯大嚼，萸菊互相酬。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103129'>徙倚阑干角，一笑与云浮。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103129_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103129'>望平畴，千万顷，稻粱收。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103113' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103113?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span>再用前韵</a><span id='poem_sentence_0_103113'>天宇正高爽，更蹑最高楼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103113_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103113'>长风为我驱驾，极目海山头。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103113_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103113'>不用牛山孟浩，不用齐山杜牧，人景自堪酬。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103113_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103113'>举酒酹空阔，汗漫与为游。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103113_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103113'>撚黄花，怜白首，恨难收。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103113_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103113'>颓龄使汝能制，何待更封留。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103113_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103113'>眼底朱甍画栋，往往人非物是，蟋蟀自鸣秋。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103113_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103113'>万里一搔首，无处著萧飕。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_103113_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年</a>　岁暮，游安晚园，有词。作品：《满江红·郑园看梅》<span id='poem_title_103272_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103272'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103272'>安晚堂前，梅开尽、都无留萼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103272'>依旧是、铁心老子，故情堪托。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103272'>长恐寿阳脂粉污，肯教摩诘丹青摸。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103272'>纵沉香、为榭䌽为园，难安著。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103272_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103272'>高节耸，清名邈。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103272'>六出不妨添羽翼，百花岂愿当头角。<div id='poem_sentence_7_103272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_103272'>尽暗香、疏影了平生，何其乐。<div id='poem_sentence_8_103272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_103272'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103291'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103291'>问信江梅，渐推出、红苞绿萼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103291_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年12月15日</a>　十二月望安晚园，赋梅上银烛。作品：《霜天晓角·戊午十二月望安晚园赋梅上银烛》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一一。）</span><div id='poem_103323' "poem_title_103323")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103323_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103323'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103323'>梅花一簇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103323_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103323'>花上千枝烛。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103323_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103323'>照出靓妆姿态，看不足、咏不足。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103323_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103323'>便欲和花宿。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103323_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103323'>却被官身局。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103323_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103323'>借问江南归未，今夜梦、难拘束。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_103323_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年</a>　应智春之请为其弟智原庙作记。作品：《忠节庙记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1309904' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309904' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309904?labeling=true' target='_blank'>忠节庙记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1258年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309904")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309904_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309904'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309904'>宝祐戊午九月，敌大举入寇淮东，围广陵，蹂通泰，躏仪真，驱略人畜而北归淮西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309904_comment'></div>总管智原策其过淮必取五湖渡，请以舟师剿之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309904_comment'></div>既而敌知有备，遂转由安丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309904_comment'></div>智原以节制司命提兵往援，至则合诸将会议，约蹙敌于城下，彼此缓急，必速救应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309904_comment'></div>众曰诺，遂引兵往西门，严阵以俟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309904_comment'></div>午后，敌拥众至安丰南门，智原激厉将士，奋入敌阵，自未至酉，战数十合，手刃敌首数人，横尸蔽野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309904_comment'></div>敌大惧，遂悉兵夹击我师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309904_comment'></div>智原奋呼，复鏖杀数百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309904_comment'></div>适敌后军至，其势愈张，智原战愈急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309904_comment'></div>会素与智原有隙者嫉其成功，拥兵自卫，坐视不救，智原军力屈势穷，犹勉励馀卒战，久之援绝而没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309904_comment'></div>事闻，赠武翼大夫、忠州刺史，庙祀于安丰，赐额忠节，以旌其功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309904_comment'></div>新庙落成，且葬有日，其兄智春等以书来求文为记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309904_comment'></div>其兄弟昔予部曲也，迹其事而有感焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309904_comment'></div>夫忠孝一本也，君亲一道也，家国一机也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309904_comment'></div>能孝于亲必能忠于君，能宜于家必能宜于国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309904_comment'></div>智原平日事亲以孝闻，庭闱之间，怡声下气，非学曾闵而有肃谨之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309904_comment'></div>吁天剔股，虽未中理，而情则真实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309904_comment'></div>别母临官，尽忠自誓，惧作亲羞，且以未能官封大人，无以答劬劳为辞，恳恻丁宁，类非武夫之所能为者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309904_comment'></div>《记》曰：战阵无勇非孝也，莅官不忠非孝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309904_comment'></div>智原平日临阵必欲死于敌，临官必欲忠于君，烈烈一命，勇往直前，宁杀其身，不敢亏为臣之道，英风义概，严于秋霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309904_comment'></div>使未死，奸雄胆寒肝裂，岂非推事亲之孝而致之欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309904_comment'></div>方智原与敌搏战之时，甚于睢阳之急也，使同事者无贺兰拥兵不救之奸，则敌必不能专力以向智原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309904_comment'></div>乃怀私憾，遂不复救。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309904_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309904_comment'></div>私憾可释也，国事不可不勉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309904_comment'></div>彼非人子耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1309904_comment'></div>不信于友，必不忠于君，不忠于君，必不孝其亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1309904_comment'></div>忠孝本心，既已俱亡，其去禽兽不远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1309904_comment'></div>然而此时武夫悍卒，嗜利无耻，乃其素心，尚未足多咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1309904_comment'></div>世固有以礼法自将，以忠孝自负，平居暇日，慷慨议论，无非捐躯徇国之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1309904_comment'></div>一旦临事，小有龃龉，则全身远害，往往嫁其祸于他人者，其视不援智原者尤其靡也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1309904_comment'></div>故因智原之事而极言之，以为来者之戒云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1309904_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年1月15日</a>　元宵节，有词。作品：《宝鼎现·和韵己未元夕》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一一。）</span>《昼锦堂·己未元夕》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一一。）</span>《永遇乐·己未元夕》3首。<span id='poem_sentence_0_103166_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103166'>将海外、银蟾推上，相映华灯辉万砌。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103166_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103166'>看舞队、向梅梢燃昼，丹燄玲珑玉蕊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103166_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103166'>渐陆地、金莲吐遍，恰似楼台临水。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103166_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103166'>老子欢意随人意。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103166_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103166_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103166'>多少吴讴联越吹。<div id='poem_sentence_7_103166_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_103166_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_103166'>闻说旧日京华，般百戏、灯棚如履。<div id='poem_sentence_10_103166_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_103183' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103183' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103183?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昼锦堂 己未元夕</a><span id='poem_sentence_7_103183_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_103137' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103137' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103137?labeling=true' ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103137")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103137_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103137'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103137'>和气熏来，这般光景，管无风雨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103137_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103137'>画栋朱甍，锦坊绣巷，娘子将嫫母。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103137_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103137'>星球高挂，灯楼趱出，良夜正消增五。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103137_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103137'>遨头事，牙旗铁马，且还那时鄞府。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103137_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103137'>甘泉见说，捷书频奏，渐次不烦鼙鼓。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103137_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103137'>双凤云间，六鳌海上，祝赞齐手舞。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103137_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103137'>三呼声里，君王万寿，岁岁传柑笑语。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103137_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103137'>便都把，升平旧曲，腔儿旋补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_103137_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_103142' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103142' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103142?labeling=true' target='_blank'>传言玉女 己未元夕</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年1月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103142'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103142'>众乐亭前，都是郁葱佳气。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103142'>越姬吴媛，粲珠钿翠珥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103142'>红销粉褪，几许粗桃凡李。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103142'>连珠宝炬，两行缇骑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103142_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103142'>自笑衰翁，又行春锦绣里。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103142'>禁肴宫酝，记当年宣赐。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103142'>休嫌拖逗，且向画堂频醉。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103142'>从今开庆，万欢千喜。<div id='poem_sentence_7_103142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_103142'></div><div
