ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年2月</a>　二月，劝农翠岩山，有诗。作品：《劭农翠山赋唐律二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_102989' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_102989' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/102989?labeling=true' target='_blank'>劭农翠山赋唐律二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（己未）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_102989")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_102989_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_102989'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_102989'>小队旌旗上翠岩，松风十里锁禅关。<div id='poem_sentence_0_102989_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_102989'>水深水浅高低涧，春淡春浓远近山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_102989_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_102989'>乡思猛随苍鸟去，客心暂与白云闲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_102989_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_102989'>天公已是多情杀<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：去声。）</span>，特把淋头雨放悭。<div id='poem_sentence_3_102989_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_102989'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_102989_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_102988' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_102988' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/102988?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（己未）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_102988_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_102988'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_102988'>老守忧民若己伤，三回奉诏劝耕桑。<div id='poem_sentence_0_102988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_102988'>周家绵远农开国，汉室兴隆谷腐仓。<div id='poem_sentence_1_102988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_102988'>麦缘少地锄山种，水怕多流累石防。<div id='poem_sentence_2_102988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_102988'>田里熙熙知乐土，更祈四表共平康。<div id='poem_sentence_3_102988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_102988'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_102988_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年2月</a>　二月，劝农翠岩山，有词。作品：《沁园春·己未翠山劝农》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一一。宛敏灏《吴潜年谱》“己未”误作“三未”）</span><div id='poem_103162' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103162' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103162?labeling=true' target='_blank'>沁园春<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>己未翠山劝农</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103162")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103162_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103162'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103162'>二十年前，君王东顾，诏牧此州。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103162'>念昔时豪杰，犹难辟阖，如今老大，却更迟留。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103162'>四载相望，三春又半，邂逅劭农得纵游。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103162'>田畴事，是桑条正长，麦含初抽。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103162_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103162'>悠悠。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103162'>身世何求。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103162'>算七十迎头合罢休。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103162'>谩绕堤旌纛，牵连鹢棹，喧天鼓吹，断送龙舟。<div id='poem_sentence_7_103162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_103162'>翠巘层边，碧云堆处，一担担来天外愁。<div id='poem_sentence_8_103162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_103162'>如何好，且同斟绿醑，自课清讴。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_103162_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年2月26日</a>　二月二十六日，行小圃，有诗与刘锡等友人。作品：《行小圃偶成唐律呈直翁自昭叔夏·己未二月二十六日》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一〇。）</span><div id='poem_102984' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_102984' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/102984?labeling=true' target='_blank'>行小圃偶成唐律呈直翁自昭叔夏<span class='inlineComment2'>（己未二月二十六日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年2月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_102984")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_102984_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_102984'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_102984'>今年花信已成空，白白红红苦雨中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_102984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_102984'>老境摧颓春更好，愁城高耸酒难攻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_102984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_102984'>一生当号知非子，万事都归亡是公。<div id='poem_sentence_2_102984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_102984'>巴得新晴天亦笑，东风吹梦过江东。<div id='poem_sentence_3_102984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_102984'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_102984_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年3月</a>　清明节，有咏物词。作品：《海棠春·己未清明对海棠有赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一二。）</span>《海棠春·再用韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一二。）</span>《海棠春·三用韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一二。）</span><div id='poem_103236' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103236' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103236?labeling=true' target='_blank'>海棠春<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>己未清明对海棠有赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103236")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103236_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103236'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103236'>海棠亭午沾疏雨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103236'>便一饷、胭脂尽吐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103236'>老去惜花心，相对花无语。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103236_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103236'>羽书万里飞来处。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103236'>报扫荡、狐嗥兔舞。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103236'>濯锦古江头，飞景还如许。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_103236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_103236'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(103236)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><div id='poem_103235' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103235' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103235?labeling=true' target='_blank'>海棠春<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>再用韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103235")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103235_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103235'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103235'>嫩晴还更宜轻雨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103235_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103235'>最好处、欲开未吐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103235_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103235'>一点聘梅心，千古凭谁语。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103235_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103235'>脸霞晕锦娇人处。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103235_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103235'>肯浪逐、红围翠舞。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103235_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103235'>银烛莫高烧，春梦无多许。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_103235_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_103234' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103234' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103234?labeling=true' target='_blank'>海棠春<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>三用韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103234")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103234_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103234'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103234'>苍龙夭矫停今雨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103234_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103234'>正不待、云吞雾吐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103234_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103234'>绝笑大夫松，今古闲言语。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103234_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103234'>清光冷艳侵人处。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103234_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103234'>漏月影、婆娑自舞。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103234_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103234'>拟作岁寒人，此愿天应许。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_103234_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年3月5日</a>　三月初五日，具奏乞归田里。作品：《三月初五日具奏乞归田里》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1309879' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309879' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309879?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三月初五日具奏乞归田里<span class='inlineComment2'>（开庆元年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年3月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309879")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309879_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309879'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309879'>臣辄沥危衷，仰干圣听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309879_comment'></div>臣一介疏远，祗事圣明，三纪于兹，旁无蚍蚁之报，自顶至踵，悉由陛下拔擢，悉由陛下保持，以至今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309879_comment'></div>伏念臣起自书生，叨尘宰辅，分量已极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309879_comment'></div>自壬子去国，坐享禄秩，优逸山林，即是臣上戴陛下始末之恩，结裹此生，了无遗欠矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309879_comment'></div>丙辰初夏，忽蒙陛下曲加纪录，起之鄞阃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309879_comment'></div>臣再三恳免，直涉季秋，叠奉宣谕，谓目今海道不异边险，且诏乡守谕旨准发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309879_comment'></div>臣上受主知，缅怀国事，感激流涕，遂不敢以衰病辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309879_comment'></div>虽知勉竭疲驽，竟亦何补毫发！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309879_comment'></div>去秋侥踰再考，复被因任之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309879_comment'></div>时适东海告警，连准密院奉旨行下，调遣兵船，申严海备，日不暇给，臣不当于此时乞身，黾勉就职，又越半岁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309879_comment'></div>然未尝不力告宰臣，乞赐密启，蚤俾归休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309879_comment'></div>近又尝以残躯百疾，死期三證，祈吁宰臣，其衰实非旋为饰说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309879_comment'></div>今春令已深，风色向顺，洋海保无它虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309879_comment'></div>如昨承朝命，团结三郡海艘，悉以办集，其数不下三数千只，见以籍册奏申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309879_comment'></div>其他兵政民务，无虑数十条，亦皆圆备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309879_comment'></div>且帑有馀赀，仓有馀粟，凡可以为此郡经久之计者，已无馀策，自此凋郡，恐成乐国，□臣复何贪恋，更不知止，矧重之以疾證死期乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309879_comment'></div>《易》之《谦》卦曰：「天道亏盈而益谦，地道变盈而流谦，人道恶盈而好谦，鬼神祸盈而福谦」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309879_comment'></div>盖天地人特具其理，而鬼神则直著其事，甚可畏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309879_comment'></div>是用殚沥悃忱，归命君父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309879_comment'></div>欲望圣慈恢天地好生之仁，广日月无私之照，念臣久侍帷幄，曾获备心膂股肱之寄，在内在外，不敢少负国家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309879_comment'></div>怜臣年事浸迫，血气已衰，譬之闲厩老马，惟有悲鸣，难任鞭策；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309879_comment'></div>察臣粗知消息进退之义，即非诡激以欺陛下，特出圣断，许臣挂神武之冠，或俾奉祠，退伏田里，获遂首丘之愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309879_comment'></div>又臣窃伏惟念先帝在御三十年，凡十放进士之榜，其被亲擢膺首选者俱已殂谢，惟独臣仅存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309879_comment'></div>陛下上轸丰芑之遗，次轸帷盖之旧，必赐兴恻，俯垂圣允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309879_comment'></div>臣干犯宸严，无任瞻天望圣、真切恳祈之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1309879_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年3月6日</a>　三月六日，四明窗会客，有词。作品：《青玉案·己未三月六日四明窗会客》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《强村丛书》本《履斋先生诗余别集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_103173' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103173' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103173?labeling=true' target='_blank'>青玉案 己未三月六日四明窗会客</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年3月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103173")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103173_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103173'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103173'>流芳只怕春无几。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103173'>拼夜饮、更才二。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103173'>不用追他欢乐事。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103173'>绮窗朱户，燕帷莺馆，多少人憔悴。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103173_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103173'>踏歌梦想江南市。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103173'>管春尽、扁舟放行李。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103173'>寒食休倾游子泪。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103173'>归去来兮，不如归去，铁定知今是。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_103173_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年3月6日</a>　三月六日，有词。作品：《贺圣朝·己未三月六日》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《强村丛书》本《履斋先生诗余别集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_103202' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103202' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103202?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺圣朝 己未三月六日</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年3月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103202")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103202_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103202'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103202'>捷书夜半甘泉去。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103202_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103202'>报天骄膏斧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103202_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103202'>摩空铜垒，闸流瞿滟，扫清云雾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103202_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103202'>楼兰飞馘，焉耆授首，谩夸称前古。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103202_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103202'>须知开庆，太平千载，方从今数。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_103202_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年3月23日</a>　三月二十三日，再具奏乞归田里。作品：《二十三日再具奏乞归田里》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1309880' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309880' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309880?labeling=true' target='_blank'>二十三日再具奏乞归田里</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年3月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309880")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309880_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309880'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309880'>臣近尝具疏乞归田里，恭奉诏书不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309880_comment'></div>祗承温诏，备极衮褒，衔戴洪恩，惟增深陨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309880_comment'></div>臣闻臣子之事君，以势分言则君犹天也，天忱不可渎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309880_comment'></div>以情分言则君犹父也，父则容可愬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309880_comment'></div>伏念臣行年虽六十有五，而涉世已踰四十年，心损于思虑之多，志丧于摧挫之多，胆薄于忧畏之多，气耗于酬酢之多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309880_comment'></div>积此四多，淫为百疢，于是臣实病矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309880_comment'></div>其所为尽瘁于职业者，盖恐食焉□□其事，不有人祸，必有天刑，如古人之所云，本非精力之有馀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309880_comment'></div>职事之最大者，无过于抚养下民，以奉艺祖紫云楼之诏誓，以体陛下培植根本之训彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309880_comment'></div>而此邦积蠹稔弊，其所由来者渐矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309880_comment'></div>前乎为守者，不过依违淟涊，以求不得罪于巨室，未尝为百姓伸枉冤，直是非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309880_comment'></div>臣自惟尝忝宰辅，为陛下抑豪强以扶贫弱，安田里以弭盗贼，臣之职分也，岂可使百姓失职，而坐视其叹息愁恨哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309880_comment'></div>于是事至有司，不得不奉国家之法令以行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309880_comment'></div>虽百姓稍获苏醒，但以臣之力拙，而致怨者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309880_comment'></div>怨之不已则谗谤兴，臣藉曰无愧于心，然以衰颓疾病之躯，而处谗谤四集之地，岂《大易》知进退存亡之义与老氏知止不殆之旨哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309880_comment'></div>仰惟陛下聪明圣哲，阿墨之毁誉，未尝不瞭然于圣衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309880_comment'></div>然孔子删诗为三百篇，而畏谗者十有二，其形容谗人之状，精微巧妙，有鬼神之所不能测度者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309880_comment'></div>于是臣之心志胆气，日营皇消砾，而百骸九窍之病日益矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309880_comment'></div>若非陛下曲赐覆持，俾获善罢，则身难保，何裨于国！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309880_comment'></div>恭望圣慈重加怜悯，检会前奏，放臣归老山林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309880_comment'></div>傥延一日之残喘，即是陛下赐以一日之生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309880_comment'></div>臣无任瞻天望圣、激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309880_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1309880_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年3月24日</a>　三月二十四日，为平桥水则作记。作品：《平桥水则记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1309907' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309907' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309907?labeling=true' target='_blank'>平桥水则记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年3月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309907")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309907_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309907'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309907'>四明郡阻山控海，水自高而卑，尽纳于海，则田无所灌注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309907_comment'></div>于是限以碶闸，水溢则启，涸则闭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309907_comment'></div>其启闭之则曰平水尺，往往以入水三尺为平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309907_comment'></div>夫地形在水之下者不能皆平，水面在地之上者未尝不平，执三尺以平水，水无不平矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309907_comment'></div>余三年积劳于诸碶，至洪水湾一役，大略尽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309907_comment'></div>己未劭农翠山，自林村由西门汎舟以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309907_comment'></div>暇日又自月湖沿竹洲舣城南，遍度水势，其平于田塍下者刻稿志之，归而验诸平桥下，伐石为准，榜曰「水则」，而大书「平」字于上方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309907_comment'></div>暴雨涨水没「平」字，戒吏卒请于郡，亟启钥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309907_comment'></div>若四泽适均，水沾「平」字，钥如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309907_comment'></div>平桥距郡治恭语可达也，都鄙旱涝之宜，求其平于此而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309907_comment'></div>后之来者，勿替于兹哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1309907_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年3月24日</a>　三月二十四日，和翁元龙诗。作品：《和翁处静赋木香·己未三月二十日四明堂》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一〇。）</span><div id='poem_102865' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_102865' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/102865?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和翁处静赋木香<span class='inlineComment2'>（己未三月二十日四明堂）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年3月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_102865")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_102865_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_102865'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_102865'>黄蕊檀心衬绿衣，细成棋架四方齐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_102865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_102865'>只缘鼻孔撩天去，特遣清香起自低。<div id='poem_sentence_1_102865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_102865'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_102865_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年3月25日</a>　三月二十五日，赏荼蘼，有词二首。作品：《浣溪沙·已未三月二十五日赏荼蘼》2首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一二。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年3月25日</a>　三月二十五日，游木香亭，有词。作品：《点绛唇·己未三月末浣木香亭赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《强村丛书》本《履斋先生诗余别集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_103190' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103190' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103190?labeling=true' target='_blank'>点绛唇 己未三月末浣木香亭赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年3月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103190")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103190_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103190'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103190'>岸舣扁舟，江南有个人归老。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103190_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103190'>簇新亭沼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103190_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103190'>分付还他了。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103190_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103190'>凝伫晴空，一抹天边鸟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103190_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103190'>嗟潦倒。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103190_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103190'>去多来少。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103190_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103190'>莫问钟昏晓。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_103190_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年4月6日</a>　四月初六日，高桥舟中，作七律二首。作品：《高桥舟中·己未四月初六日》2首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一〇。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年4月6日</a>　四月初六日，与刘锡有诗唱和。作品：《水云乡和制机刘自昭韵·己未四月六日》3首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一〇。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年4月9日</a>　夏四月初九日，复具奏乞祠。作品：《夏四月初九日复具奏乞祠》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1309881' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309881' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309881?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夏四月初九日复具奏乞祠</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年4月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309881")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309881_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309881'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309881'>臣三沥丹悃，上冒圣聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309881_comment'></div>臣顷缘身病于负薪之忧，心病于上棘之忧，荐贡封章，恳祈閒退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309881_comment'></div>圣恩天大，屡被温纶，至援尹吉甫《烝民》之诗，训臣以仲山甫之事业，且曲加谕旨，曰决未可言归，曰切不必重请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309881_comment'></div>臣祗承明诏，感极涕零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309881_comment'></div>但臣之真忱，实有不容自已者，谨即是诗而备陈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309881_comment'></div>且其诗曰「夙夜匪懈，以事一人」，所以表仲山甫之勤瘁，即诏旨所谓不惮其劳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309881_comment'></div>又曰「不侮矜寡，不畏强御」，所以表仲山甫之正直，即诏旨所谓不挠其志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309881_comment'></div>尹吉甫之于仲山甫，可谓能知其心，善著其事矣，而乃先之曰「既明且哲，以保其身」，何与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309881_comment'></div>臣深探尹吉甫之意，而验诸诗之下章曰「德輶如毛，民鲜克举之，我仪图之，维仲山甫举之，爱莫助之」，说者谓政事易耳，而人不能行，维仲山甫能举此德而行之，惜乎莫能助之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309881_comment'></div>是知尹吉甫欲仲山甫为保身之谋，正为仲山甫寡助之虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309881_comment'></div>夫以仲山甫赋政徂齐，每怀靡及，忠勋如此，而尹吉甫尚为之隐忧，臣实何人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309881_comment'></div>不堪为仲山甫执鞭，而竛𥩵孤立，则有类尹吉甫之所云者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309881_comment'></div>臣何敢独恃圣知，而不求所以保身之道乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309881_comment'></div>保身之道，惟在乞身以去尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309881_comment'></div>今臣之当去者，不特此邦之人以为宜，而天下之人莫不以为宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309881_comment'></div>此邦之人则曰「推而不去，是顽钝也，顽钝可耻也」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309881_comment'></div>天下之人则曰「久而不去，是贪恋也，亦可耻也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309881_comment'></div>于是臣不但畏此邦人之议，而且畏天下之议，身心之病，愈不可药矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309881_comment'></div>反覆而思，惟有积忱归命君父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309881_comment'></div>欲望皇帝陛下念其坎𡒄平生，怜其顾惜晚节，赦其攫拂威命，特推从欲之仁，俾遂首丘之愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309881_comment'></div>臣傥未遽溘先朝露，犹可退与乡人子弟讲明孝弟忠信之义，以铺扬圣化而歌咏太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309881_comment'></div>是陛下赐臣为圣世无玷缺之人，而或庶几于仲山甫明哲之万分一矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309881_comment'></div>葵藿寸衷，虽不获糜捐以效报，尚当衔结以酬恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1309881_comment'></div>臣神往形留，意长语短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1309881_comment'></div>惟是数渎宸严，无任瞻天望圣、激切惶惧之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1309881_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1309881_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年4月9日</a>　四月九日，会四明窗，有词。作品：《满江红·己未四月九日会四明窗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一一。）</span><div id='poem_103293' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103293' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103293?labeling=true' target='_blank'>满江红<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十五 </span>己未四月九日会四明窗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年4月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103293")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103293_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103293'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103293'>饤饾残花，也随分、红红白白。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103293_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103293'>缘底事，春才好处，又成轻别。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103293_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103293'>芳草萋迷归路远，子规更叫黄昏月。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103293_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103293'>倚阑干、触处是浓愁，凭谁说。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103293_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103293'>我不厌，樽罍挈。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103293_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103293'>君莫放，笙歌彻。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103293_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103293'>自河南丞相，有兹宾客。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103293_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103293'>一笑何曾千古换，半醺便觉乾坤窄。<div id='poem_sentence_7_103293_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_103293'>怕转头、天际望归舟，江山隔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_103293_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年4月27日</a>　四月二十七日，与友人有词唱和。作品：《念奴娇·戏和仲殊己未四月二十七日》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一一。）</span><div id='poem_103167' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103167' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103167?labeling=true' target='_blank'>念奴娇<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>戏和仲殊己未四月二十七日</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年4月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103167")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103167_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103167'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103167'>午飙褪暑，向绿阴深处，引杯孤酌。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103167'>啼鸟一声庭院悄，日影偷移朱箔。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103167'>杏落金丸，荷抽碧筒，景物挨排却。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103167'>虚檐长啸，世缘菌簟筼箨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103167_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103167'>休问雪藕丝蒲，佩兰钿艾，旧梦都高阁。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103167'>惟有流莺当此际，舌弄笙簧如约。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103167'>短棹双溪，么锄三径，归计犹谁托。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103167'>料应猿鹤，近来都怨离索。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_103167_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年5月5日</a>　五月五日，有词自寿。作品：《二郎神·己未自寿》2首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一一。）</span><div id='poem_103096' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103096' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103096?labeling=true' id='poem_content_103096'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103096'>古稀近也，是六十五翁生日。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103096_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103096'>恰就得端阳，艾人当户，朱笔书符大吉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103096_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103096'>卦气周来从新起，怕白发、苍颜难必。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103096_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103096'>随见定性缘，餐饥眠困，喜无啾唧。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103096_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103096'>盈溢。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103096_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103096'>书生做到，能高官秩。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103096_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103096'>况碌碌儿曹，望郎名郡，叨冒差除不一。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103096_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103096'>积世主恩，满家天禄，婚嫁近来将毕。<div id='poem_sentence_7_103096_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_103096'>还自祝，愿早悬车里社，始为收拾。</div><div class='inlineComment2'>（疒众）</span>在厥躬。<div id='poem_sentence_2_558293_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_558293'>天高元听下，一念岂难通。<div id='poem_sentence_3_558293_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_558293'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_558293_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年</a>　久雨喜晴，有诗。作品：《久雨喜晴检阅计院纪以舂容之篇敬用韵为谢（夜来坐客有蜀人邓君莘起勉余为全晚节计，故末句云然）》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一〇。）</span><div id='poem_103069' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103069' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103069?labeling=true' target='_blank'>久雨喜晴检阅计院纪以舂容之篇敬用韵为谢<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103069")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103069_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_103069_0'>① 夜来坐客有蜀人邓君莘起，勉余为全晚节计，故末句云然</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103069'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103069'>乐天何爱咏，尧夫非好吟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103069'>愧乏康济术，粗怀饥溺心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103069'>弥旬雨翻屋，耄倪泣苍䫒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103069'>微臣职刍牧，痒痛入肌深。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103069'>行若负刺芒，坐如隐毡针。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103069'>再拜告<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：入声。）</span>神明，寸心秉坚金。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103069'>蠲租还已债，议狱并弛刑。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103069'>但求讲实政，何暇竞虚名。<div id='poem_sentence_7_103069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_103069'>天威咫尺临，昏翳忽开明。<div id='poem_sentence_8_103069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_103069'>宿苗既丰硕，稚秧靡飘淫。<div id='poem_sentence_9_103069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_103069'>阿香亦效灵，排阴吐洪音。<div id='poem_sentence_10_103069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_103069'>推出太阳辉，天外旋收声。<div id='poem_sentence_11_103069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_103069'>老守宽近忧，浊醪呼客斟。<div id='poem_sentence_12_103069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_103069'>客有劝翁归，前身岂傅霖。<div id='poem_sentence_13_103069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_103069'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_103069_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年6月9日</a>　六月九日，雨后有词。作品：《秋霁·己未六月九日雨后赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《强村丛书》本《履斋先生诗余别集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_103201' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103201' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103201?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋霁<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>己未六月九日雨后赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年6月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103201")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103201_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103201'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103201'>阶砌吟蛩，正竹外萧萧，雨骤风驶。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103201'>凉浸桃笙，暑消葵扇，借伊一些秋意。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103201'>枕边茉莉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103201'>满尘奁、贮香能腻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103201'>也不用，玉骨冰肌，人伴佳眠尔。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103201_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103201'>谁信此境，渐入华胥，旷然不知，庄蝶谁是。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103201'>笑邯郸、羁魂客梦，贪他荣贵暂时里。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103201'>飞鼠扑灯还自坠。<div id='poem_sentence_7_103201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_103201'>展转惊寤，才听禁鼓三敲，夜声寥阒，又般滋味。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_103201_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年6月14日</a>　六月十四日，老香堂前月台玩月，有词。作品：《小重山·己未六月十四日老香堂前月台玩月》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《强村丛书》本《履斋先生诗余别集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_103107' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103107' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103107?labeling=true' target='_blank'>小重山 己未六月十四日老香堂前月台玩月</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年6月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103107")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103107_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103107'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103107'>碧霄如水月如钲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103107_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103107'>今宵知为我，特分明。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103107_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103107'>冰壶玉界两三星。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103107_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103107'>清露下，渐觉湿衣轻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103107_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103107'>高树点流萤。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103107_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103107'>秋声还又动，客心惊。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103107_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103107'>吾家水月寄昭亭。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103107_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103107'>归去也，天岂太无情。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_103107_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年6月17日</a>　六月十七日西郊观稼，与刘锡有诗唱和。作品：《赓刘自昭出郊佳什·己未六月十七日西郊观稼》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一〇。）</span><div id='poem_103065' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103065' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103065?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赓刘自昭出郊佳什<span class='inlineComment2'>（己未六月十七日西郊观稼）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年6月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103065")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_103065_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103065'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103065'>倦听衙官报两衙，出门山水即吾家。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103065_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103065'>浅深碧绿湖田稻，浓淡红黄野岸花。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103065_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103065'>草草人生知有限，悠悠客恨自无涯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103065_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103065'>凉飔特为驱袢暑，白鸟青天万里赊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103065_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103065'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_103065_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年6月17日</a>　六月十七日西郊观稼，有诗。作品：《出郊偶赋·己未六月十七日》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一〇。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年7月1日</a>　七月初一，重建逸老堂成，有记。作品：《重建逸老堂记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《履斋遗稿》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1309908' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309908' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309908?labeling=true' target='_blank'>重建逸老堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年7月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309908")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309908_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309908'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309908'>逸老堂者，绍兴十四年郡守莫侯将所创，并为文以记之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309908_comment'></div>其义盖摘李太白所云「四明逸老贺知章」之语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309908_comment'></div>按贺公字季真，唐开元十三年为礼部侍郎、集贤院学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309908_comment'></div>肃宗正储副，授秘书监、太子宾客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309908_comment'></div>天宝初，移疾请为道士，还乡里，诏赐剡川居焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309908_comment'></div>剡隶越，鄞故越封部，公亦自号四明狂客，故侯缔堂妥灵于是邦之月湖，且合太白而祀之，谓二公皆抱气识之全者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309908_comment'></div>然以予观之，太白初见明皇，倨傲鲜腆，待高力士辈若奴仆，其气真可以挥斥八极，驱役群动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309908_comment'></div>而其末也，乃陷于永王璘之党，毋亦气有馀而识未足耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309908_comment'></div>季真遭时遇主，弹指可睹显位，忽飘然引去，人知其为高而不知其所以高也，于是肃宗之人品已瞭于季真胸中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309908_comment'></div>使相与终始，则灵武之事犯父子之大伦，季真亦将不能逃万世之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309908_comment'></div>《易》曰「知几其神」，季真有焉，又岂止于蠛蠓富贵、涕唾卿相而已哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309908_comment'></div>此之谓真识，而非徒气之所能为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309908_comment'></div>是堂之建，殆今一百十五年矣，屋老圮坏，屡葺屡颓，片瓦尺椽几无存者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309908_comment'></div>予领郡之三年，始克鼎新之，规模宏敞，视昔稍异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309908_comment'></div>乃求季真之像于越，绘而龛之，且诔以词，述以赞，用诏永久，俾邦之人士景清风而企芳躅，或少裨于风教云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309908_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309908_comment'></div>自有天地以来，上下数千百年，其间据权位，擅势利，呼吸祸福，顾盼荣辱，以狂走盲趋一世之人者，不知其几矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309908_comment'></div>未几声消迹灭，影响无闻，甚者流腥遗臭，有孝子慈孙百世莫之能改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309908_comment'></div>乃若孤标劲节之士，身没而名愈彰，千载之下，虽渔人樵子亦为之兴起，不以时迁世换而二其心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309908_comment'></div>为士者宜知所择矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309908_comment'></div>堂既成而对涵虚馆，表里及东西两桥并缮治之，轮奂丹雘，皆灿然华美，要不可无以叙岁月，于是乎书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309908_comment'></div>开庆元年秋七月癸卯朔，观文殿大学士、银青光禄大夫、沿海制置大使、判庆元军府事、兼管内劝农使、金陵郡开国公、食邑五千九百户、食实封一千七百户吴潜撰，中散大夫、直秘阁致仕张即之书，朝散大夫、直宝章阁赵汝梅题盖<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1309908_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1309908'>「谓二公」句及下句「以予观之」：原脱，据《四明续志》补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1309908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1309908'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_21_1309908_1'>⑴ 《履斋遗稿》卷三。又见《四明续志》卷二，《敬止录》卷二五，嘉靖《宁波府志》卷一九，《两浙金石志》卷一二，《八琼室金石补正》卷一二○，国家图书馆藏拓片·章专三五○。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1309908_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年</a>　为逸老堂贺知章画像作赞。作品：《贺知章画像赞》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《八琼室金石补正》卷一二〇。）</span><div id='poem_1309915' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309915' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309915?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺知章画像赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309915")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1309915_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309915'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309915'>山林之士，去不可挽。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1309915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1309915'>市朝之士，出不知返。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1309915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1309915'>矫矫先生，高眄远视。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1309915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1309915'>可仕则仕，可止则止。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1309915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1309915'>粤惟二疏，辅导汉元。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1309915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1309915'>怍其即位，旋以飘然。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1309915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1309915'>粤惟先生，师傅唐肃。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1309915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1309915'>太阳未升，去之已速。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1309915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1309915'>前疏后贺，夫岂不情！<div id='poem_sentence_8_1309915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1309915'>知几识微，以全令名。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1309915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1309915'>狂非真狂，醉非真醉。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1309915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1309915'>诗侣酒徒，亦复尔尔。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1309915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1309915'>四明之阳，月白山空。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1309915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1309915'>平湖万顷，今古清风。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1309915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1309915'>金陵吴潜赞。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1309915_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年7月7日</a>　七夕，填词二首。作品：《鹊桥仙·己未七夕》2首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一二。）</span><div id='poem_103309' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103309' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103309?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鹊桥仙<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>己未七夕</a><span "poem_title_103309")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103309_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103309'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103309'>银河半隐，玉蟾高挂，已觉炎光向后。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103309_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103309'>穿针楼上未眠人，应自把、荷花挼揉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103309_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103309'>双星缥缈，霎时聚散，肯向鹊桥回首。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103309_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103309'>原来一岁一番期，却挨得、天长地久。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_103309_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年7月</a>　喜雨，作七律二首。作品：《喜雨二解·呈检阅同官诸丈己未七月》2首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一〇。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年8月1日</a>　秋八月初一日，具奏乞祠。作品：《秋八月初一日具奏乞祠》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1309882' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309882' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309882?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋八月初一日具奏乞祠</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年8月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309882")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309882_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309882'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309882'>臣辄沥丹忱，上干圣听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309882_comment'></div>衰悴之踪，待罪海阃，岁且三周，虽粗竭于疲驽，然日增于疢疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309882_comment'></div>固尝密陈悃愊，屡祈君父，兹以夏秋之交，暑气侵蚀，病体益难支吾，不敢辄具繁词，谨以情实吁告君父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309882_comment'></div>欲望圣慈特赐矜怜，即垂睿断，令臣归伏田里，退安晚节，或畀真祠之禄，少逸馀龄，实戴君父顶踵乾坤之造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309882_comment'></div>臣干冒宸严，无任激切恳祈之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309882_comment'></div>伏乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1309882_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_1_103199_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103199'>家僮归报道，快酿酒、休教醨薄。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103199_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103139_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103139'>人生歧路中，底用杨朱泣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103139_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' target='_blank'>南乡子<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>和韵，己未八月十日郊行</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年8月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103178")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103178_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103178'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103178'>野思浩难收。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103178'>坐看渔舟度远洲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103178'>芦苇已雕荷已败，风飕。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103178'>桂子飘香八月头。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103178_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103178'>虽则家山元是客，浮休。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年8月10日</a>　八月十夜同官小饮逸老堂，有词。作品：《行香子·开庆己未八月十夜同官小饮逸老堂李直翁制参中示东坡题钓台行香子走笔和韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一二。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年8月13日</a>　八月十三日，再具奏乞归。作品：《十三日再具奏乞归》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吴潜《许国公奏议》卷四。该篇《全宋文》无。）</span><div id='poem_1309880' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1309880' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1309880?labeling=true' target='_blank'>二十三日再具奏乞归田里</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年3月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_1309880")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1309880_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1309880'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1309880'>臣近尝具疏乞归田里，恭奉诏书不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1309880_comment'></div>祗承温诏，备极衮褒，衔戴洪恩，惟增深陨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1309880_comment'></div>臣闻臣子之事君，以势分言则君犹天也，天忱不可渎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1309880_comment'></div>以情分言则君犹父也，父则容可愬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1309880_comment'></div>伏念臣行年虽六十有五，而涉世已踰四十年，心损于思虑之多，志丧于摧挫之多，胆薄于忧畏之多，气耗于酬酢之多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1309880_comment'></div>积此四多，淫为百疢，于是臣实病矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1309880_comment'></div>其所为尽瘁于职业者，盖恐食焉□□其事，不有人祸，必有天刑，如古人之所云，本非精力之有馀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1309880_comment'></div>职事之最大者，无过于抚养下民，以奉艺祖紫云楼之诏誓，以体陛下培植根本之训彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1309880_comment'></div>而此邦积蠹稔弊，其所由来者渐矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1309880_comment'></div>前乎为守者，不过依违淟涊，以求不得罪于巨室，未尝为百姓伸枉冤，直是非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1309880_comment'></div>臣自惟尝忝宰辅，为陛下抑豪强以扶贫弱，安田里以弭盗贼，臣之职分也，岂可使百姓失职，而坐视其叹息愁恨哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1309880_comment'></div>于是事至有司，不得不奉国家之法令以行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1309880_comment'></div>虽百姓稍获苏醒，但以臣之力拙，而致怨者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1309880_comment'></div>怨之不已则谗谤兴，臣藉曰无愧于心，然以衰颓疾病之躯，而处谗谤四集之地，岂《大易》知进退存亡之义与老氏知止不殆之旨哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1309880_comment'></div>仰惟陛下聪明圣哲，阿墨之毁誉，未尝不瞭然于圣衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1309880_comment'></div>然孔子删诗为三百篇，而畏谗者十有二，其形容谗人之状，精微巧妙，有鬼神之所不能测度者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1309880_comment'></div>于是臣之心志胆气，日营皇消砾，而百骸九窍之病日益矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1309880_comment'></div>若非陛下曲赐覆持，俾获善罢，则身难保，何裨于国！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1309880_comment'></div>恭望圣慈重加怜悯，检会前奏，放臣归老山林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1309880_comment'></div>傥延一日之残喘，即是陛下赐以一日之生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1309880_comment'></div>臣无任瞻天望圣、激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1309880_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1309880_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年8月15日</a>　中秋无月，有词。作品：《水调歌头·己未中秋无月》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一二。）</span><div id='poem_103123' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103123' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103123?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>己未中秋无月</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年8月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103123")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103123_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103123'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103123'>今岁月和桂，不肯作中秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103123_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103123'>一年惟此佳节，底事白教休。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103123_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103123'>我已侵寻七秩，况复轮囷万感，合恨更分愁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103123_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103123'>先自无聊赖，雨意得能稠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103123_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103123'>天柱峰，知何处，老难游。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103123_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103123'>痴云如妒，不知弦管可吹不。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103123_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103123'>安得风姨扫荡，推出团圆月姊，便遣桂香浮。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103123_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103123'>世事十常九，不使展眉头。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_103123_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年8月15日</a>　中秋，与友人有词唱和。作品：《水调歌头·和晦翁韵预赋山中乐己未中秋中浣书于老香堂》4首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·梅应发、刘锡《四明续志》卷一二。《全宋词》“晦翁”作“梅翁”）</span><div </span>和梅翁韵预赋山中乐，己未中秋中浣书于老香堂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年8月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103125'>已是三堪乐，更是百无忧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103125'>山朋溪友呼酒，互劝复争酬。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103125'>钓水肥鲜鳊鳜，采树甘鲜梨栗，䆉稏一齐收。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103125'>树底飞轻盖，溪上放轻舟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103125_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103125'>笑鸱夷，名已谢，利还谋。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103125'>蜗蝇<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_103125", 103125, ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年8月17日</a>　八月十七日，依旧观文殿大学士判宁国府，特进崇国公。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年8月</a>　八月间答许月卿书。作品：《宋履斋吴公帖》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·许月卿《先天集》附录上。该篇《全宋文》漏。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年8月</a>　获准还乡，有词。作品：《水调歌头》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《强村丛书》本《履斋先生诗余别集》卷二。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年8月</a>　准备还家，与友人有词唱和。作品：《谒金门·老香堂和韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《强村丛书》本《履斋先生诗余别集》卷二。）</span>《谒金门·和韵赋茶》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《强村丛书》本《履斋先生诗余别集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_103250' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103250' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103250?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谒金门<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>老香堂和韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103250")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103250_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103250'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103250'>秋已老。又是败荷衰草。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103250_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103250'>客子安排归棹了。回头烟树渺。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103250_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103250'>檀板休教歌杳。金兽且教香绕。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103250_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103250'>一醉秋堂秋夜悄。从他霜漏晓。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103250_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103250'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_103250_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_103245' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103245' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103245?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谒金门<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>和韵赋茶</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103245")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103245_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103245'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103245'>汤怕老。缓煮龙芽凤草。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103245_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103245'>七碗徐徐撑腹了。卢家诗兴渺。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103245_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103245'>君岂荆溪路杳。我已泾川梦绕。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103245_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103245'>酒兴茶酣人语悄。莫教鸡聒晓。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103245_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103245'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_103245_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年8月</a>　准备还家，有词。作品：《谒金门》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《强村丛书》本《履斋先生诗余别集》卷二。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年8月</a>　秋社，维舟逸老堂，口占一词。作品：《水调歌头·开庆己未秋社维舟逸老堂口占》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《强村丛书》本《履斋先生诗余别集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_103115' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103115' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103115?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>开庆己未秋社维舟逸老堂口占</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103115")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103115_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103115'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103115'>倚舵秋江浒，明日征帆轻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103115'>从头点检身世，百事已圆成。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103115'>及第曾攀龙首，仕宦曾居鸱阁，衣锦更光荣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103115'>若又不知止，天道恐亏盈。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103115_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103115'>借称呼，遮俗眼，便归耕。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103115'>但馀心愿，朝暮香火告神明。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103115'>一愿君王万寿，次愿干戈永息，三愿岁丰登。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103115'>四愿老安乐，疾病免相萦。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_103115_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年8月</a>　准备还家，有词别同僚。作品：《水调歌头·奉别诸同官》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《强村丛书》本《履斋先生诗余别集》卷二。）</span>《贺新郎·和惠检阅惜别》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《强村丛书》本《履斋先生诗余别集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_103120' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103120' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103120?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>奉别诸同官</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103120")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103120_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103120'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103120'>便作阳关别，烟雨暗孤汀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103120_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103120'>浮屠三宿桑下，犹自不忘情。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103120_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103120'>何况情钟我辈，聚散匆匆草草，真个是云萍。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103120_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103120'>上下四方客，后会渺难凭。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103120_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103120'>愿诸公，皆衮衮，喜通津。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103120_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103120'>老夫从此归隐，耕钓了馀生。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103120_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103120'>若见江南苍鴚，更遇江东黄耳，莫惜寄音声。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103120_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103120'>强阁儿女泪，有酒且频倾。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_103120_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_103209' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_103209' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/103209?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺新郎 和惠检阅惜别</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25271, "南宋", "吴潜", "poem_title_103209")'>吴潜</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_103209_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_103209'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_103209'>晚打西江渡。<div id='poem_sentence_0_103209_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_103209'>便抬头、严城鼓角，乱烟深处。<div id='poem_sentence_1_103209_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_103209'>无限珠玑双手接，颇觉奚囊暴富。<div id='poem_sentence_2_103209_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_103209'>强载月、空舟回去。<div id='poem_sentence_3_103209_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_103209'>劝子不须忧百草，四周维、自著灵鳌柱。<div id='poem_sentence_4_103209_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_103209'>互今古，只如许。<div id='poem_sentence_5_103209_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_103209'>杭州直北还乡路。<div id='poem_sentence_6_103209_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_103209'>想山中、猿呼鹿啸，鹭翔鸥舞。<div id='poem_sentence_7_103209_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_103209'>尽道翁归真个也，只怕颜容非故。<div id='poem_sentence_8_103209_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_103209'>愿从此、耕云钓雨。<div id='poem_sentence_9_103209_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_103209'>盘谷幽深空谷杳，但书来、时寄相思句。<div id='poem_sentence_10_103209_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_103209'>千里外，镇延伫。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_103209_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
